# copyright_long:       Publisher: Free Bible Software Group<br>Source: Riverside New Testament for e-Sword http://www.thechan.com/<br>Rights: The Riverside New Testament (1923), by William G. Ballantine, Boston: Houghton Mifflin Co.<br><br> The translation was made directly from the original Greek. Nestle's text was generally followed. However, he also used The Twentieth Century New Testament, Weymouth's New Testament in Modern Speech, Moffat's New Translation of the New Testament, the Revised Version, and the King James Version. Proper names were left as they were in the American Revised Version. It was written in paragraph form with no verse numbering, but with chapter numbers in Roman numerals.
40001001	THE ancestral line of Jesus Christ , son of David , son of Abraham :
40001002	Abraham was the father of Isaac ; Isaac was the father of Jacob ; Jacob was the father of Judah and his brothers ;
40001003	Judah was the father of Perez and Zerah ; Perez was the father of Hezron ; Hezron was the father of Ram ;
40001004	Ram was the father of Amminadab ; Amminadab was the father of Nahshon ; Nahshon was the father of Salmon ;
40001005	Salmon was the father of Boaz ; Boaz was the father of Obed ;
40001006	Jesse was the father of David the King . David was the father of Solomon ;
40001007	Solomon was the father of Rehoboam ; Rehoboam was the father of Abijah ; Abijah was the father of Asa ;
40001008	Asa was the father of Jehoshaphat ; Jehoshaphat was the father of Joram ; Joram was the father of Uzziah ;
40001009	Uzziah was the father of Jotham ; Jotham was the father of Ahaz ; Ahaz was the father of Hezekiah ;
40001010	Hezekiah was the father of Manasseh ; Manasseh was the father of Amon ; Amon was the father of Josiah ;
40001011	Josiah was the father of Jechoniah and his brothers at the time of the Babylonian exile .
40001012	After the Babylonian exile , Jechoniah was the father of Shealtiel ; Shealtiel was the father of Zerubbabel ;
40001013	Zerubbabel was the father of Abiud ; Abiud was the father of Eliakim ; Eliakim was the father of Azor ;
40001014	Azor was the father of Sadoc ; Sadoc was the father of Achim ; Achim was the father of Eliud ;
40001015	Eliud was the father of Eleazar ; Eleazar was the father of Matthan ; Matthan was the father of Jacob ;
40001016	Jacob was the father of Joseph the husband of Mary , of whom was born Jesus , who is called Christ .
40001017	So there were in all fourteen generations from Abraham to David , and fourteen generations from David to the Babylonian exile , and fourteen generations from the Babylonian exile to the Christ .
40001018	The birth of Jesus was in this way : His mother Mary had been betrothed to Joseph , but before they came together she was found to be with child by the Holy Spirit .
40001019	Joseph , her husband , being an upright man , and yet not willing to make her a public example , resolved to dismiss her privately .
40001020	But while he was thinking this over , an angel of the Lord appeared to him in a dream and said , " Joseph , son of David , do not be afraid to take Mary as your wife , for what has been conceived in her is of the Holy Spirit .
40001021	She will bear a son and you shall call his name Jesus , for he will save his people from their sins . "
40001022	All this happened in fulfillment of what the Lord had spoken through the prophet :
40001023	" Behold the virgin will conceive and will bear a son , and they will call his name Immanuel " .
40001024	When Joseph awoke from sleep , he did as the angel of the Lord had bidden him , and took his wife to his home .
40001025	But he did not live with her as a husband until she had borne a son . He called his name Jesus .
40002001	AFTER Jesus had been born in Bethlehem , in Judaea , in the days of Herod the King , wise men from the East arrived at Jerusalem ,
40002002	saying , " Where is he who has been born King of the Jews ? For we saw his star in the East and have come to do homage to him . "
40002003	When King Herod heard it , he was disturbed , and so was all Jerusalem .
40002004	Then he called together all the high priests and scribes of the people and inquired of them where the Christ was to be born .
40002005	They said to him , " In Bethlehem , in Juda . For so it was written by the prophet ,
40002006	' And thou , Bethlehem , land of Judah , art by no means least among the leaders of Judah ; for from thee will come a leader who will shepherd my people Israel . ' "
40002007	Then Herod secretly summoned the wise men and learned from them exactly the time of the star's appearance ,
40002008	and as he sent them to Bethlehem he said , " Go and make careful inquiries about the child , and when you have found him bring me word , so that I too may come and do homage to him . "
40002009	After hearing the king , they journeyed on , and the star which they had seen in the East went before them until it came and stood over where the child was .
40002010	When they saw the star , they were very joyful .
40002011	They entered the house and saw the child with Mary his mother , and they fell down and did him homage . Then they opened their treasures and presented to him gifts , gold and frankincense and myrrh .
40002012	After this they were warned in a dream not to return to Herod , and so went by another mad back to their own country .
40002013	After they had gone , an angel of the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph and said , " Rise up , and take the child and his mother and flee into Egypt , and be there until I tell you , for Herod will search for the child in order to kill him . "
40002014	So Joseph rose up , and took the child and his mother in the night and went away to Egypt ,
40002015	and was there until the death of Herod , in order that the word of the Lord spoken through the prophet might be fulfilled , " Out of Egypt I called my Son . "
40002016	Then Herod , seeing that he had been outwitted by the wise men , became furious , and sent out and killed all the boy babies two years old and under in Bethlehem and all its neighborhood , guided by the date which he had carefully learned from the wise men .
40002017	Then was fulfilled what was spoken through Jeremiah the prophet when he said ,
40002018	" A voice was heard in Ramah , wailing and bitter lamentation , Rachel weeping for her children , and she would not be comforted because they are not . "
40002019	But after Herod had died , an angel of the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph in Egypt
40002020	and said , " Arise , and take the child and his mother and go into the land of Israel , for they are dead who sought the child's life . "
40002021	So he arose , and took the child and his mother and came into the land of Israel .
40002022	But when he heard that Archelaus was reigning over Judaea in place of his father Herod , he was afraid to go there , and being directed in a dream he went away to the region of Galilee
40002023	and settled in a town called Nazareth , so that what had been spoken through the prophets might be fulfilled , " He will be called a Nazarene . "
40003001	IN those days John the Baptist came preaching in the wild part of Judaea
40003002	and saying , " Repent ; for the kingdom of heaven is at hand .
40003003	For this is he who was foretold through Isaiah the prophet when he said : ' The voice of one crying aloud in the wilderness , Make ready the way of the Lord , make straight his paths . ' "
40003004	This John had his clothing of camel's hair and wore a leather belt around his waist , and his food was locusts and wild honey .
40003005	Then went out to him Jerusalem and all Judaea and all the neighborhood of the Jordan
40003006	and were baptized by him in the Jordan River , confessing their sins .
40003007	When he saw many of the Pharisees and Sadducees coming for baptism , he said , " Brood of vipers , who directed you to flee from the coming wrath ?
40003008	Produce fruit fitting for a change of heart ,
40003009	and do not think of saying to yourselves , ' We have Abraham for our father , ' for I tell you God is able out of these stones to raise up children for Abraham .
40003010	Now the axe is lying at the root of the trees . Every tree that does not yield good fruit will be cut down and cast into the fire .
40003011	I baptize you with water for a change of heart , but he who is coming after me is more powerful than I ; I am not worthy to carry his shoes ; he will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire .
40003012	He has his fan in his hand and will thoroughly clean his threshing-floor . He will gather his grain into his storehouse , but the chaff he will burn with fire unquenchable . "
40003013	Then Jesus came from Galilee to the Jordan to John to be baptized by him .
40003014	But John opposed him , saying , " I have need to be baptized by you , and do you come to me ? "
40003015	Jesus replied , " Permit it now , for so it is fitting for us to complete every righteous act . " Then he permitted him .
40003016	Jesus , as soon as he was baptized , went up from the water , and the heavens were opened and he saw the Spirit of God descending as a dove and coming upon him .
40003017	A voice from the heavens said , " This is my Son , the beloved in whom I delight . "
40004001	THEN Jesus was led by the Spirit up into the wild country to be tempted by the Devil .
40004002	After he had fasted forty days and forty nights he was hungry .
40004003	Then the tempter came and said to him , " If you are the Son of God , tell these stones to turn into loaves of bread . "
40004004	But he answered , " It is written , ' Man shall not live on bread alone , but on every word that comes from the mouth of God . ' "
40004005	Then the Devil took him with him to the holy city and placed him on the top of the temple
40004006	and said to him , " If you are the Son of God , throw yourself down ; for it is written , ' To his angels he will give charge of you , and on their hands they will bear you lest you strike your foot against a stone . ' "
40004007	Jesus said to him , " It is written , too , ' Thou shalt not try the Lord thy God . ' "
40004008	Again the Devil took him with him to a very high mountain and showed him all the kingdoms of the world and their glory ,
40004009	and said to him , " All these things I will give you if you will fall down and do homage to me . "
40004010	Jesus said to him , " Begone , Satan , for it is written , ' To the Lord thy God alone shalt thou do homage , and him alone shalt thou serve . ' "
40004011	Then the Devil left him , and angels came and waited upon him .
40004012	When Jesus heard that John had been betrayed , he went away into Galilee .
40004013	Leaving Nazareth , he came and lived in Capernaum on the lake shore on the borders of Zebulun and Naphtali ,
40004014	so that the word spoken by the prophet Isaiah might be fulfilled :
40004015	" Land of Zebulun and land of Naphtali , road to the sea , country beyond the Jordan , Galilee of the Gentiles ,
40004016	the people that sat in darkness saw a great light and upon those sitting in the land and shadow of death light dawned . "
40004017	From that time Jesus began to proclaim and say , " Repent , for the kingdom of heaven is at hand . "
40004018	As he was walking along the shore of the lake of Galilee , he saw two brothers , Simon who is called Peter , and Andrew his brother , casting a net into the lake , for they were fishermen ;
40004019	and he said to them , " Follow me and I will make you fishers of men . "
40004020	They at once left the nets and followed him .
40004021	Going on from there , he saw two other brothers â James the son of Zebedee and John his brother â in their boat with Zebedee their father , mending their nets ; and he called them .
40004022	They at once left the boat and their father and followed him .
40004023	Jesus went around through the whole of Galilee , teaching in the synagogues and proclaiming the good news of the Kingdom , and healing every disease and every infirmity among the people .
40004024	His fame spread out into all Syria , and they brought to him all who were sick with various diseases and those suffering from acute pain , demoniacs , lunatics , and paralytics , and he healed them .
40004025	Great crowds followed him from Galilee and Decapolis and Jerusalem and Judaea and from beyond the Jordan .
40005001	SEEING the crowds , he went up on the mountain , and when he had seated himself his disciples came to him .
40005002	He opened his mouth and taught them , saying :
40005003	" Blessed are the poor in spirit ! For theirs is the kingdom of heaven .
40005004	" Blessed are they that mourn ! For they will be comforted .
40005005	" Blessed are the gentle ! For they will inherit the land .
40005006	" Blessed are those who hunger and thirst for righteousness ! For they will have abundance .
40005007	" Blessed are the compassionate ! For they will receive compassion .
40005008	" Blessed are the pure in heart ! For they will see God .
40005009	" Blessed are the peacemakers ! For they will be called sons of God .
40005010	" Blessed are those who have been persecuted for righteousness ! For theirs is the kingdom of heaven .
40005011	" Blessed are you when men revile you and persecute you and say every evil thing against you falsely for my sake !
40005012	Rejoice and be exceedingly glad , for your reward is great in heaven . For so they persecuted the prophets who were before you .
40005013	" You are the salt of the earth . But if the salt becomes flat , with what can it be salted ? It is good for nothing but to be thrown out and trodden under foot by men .
40005014	You are the light of the world . A city cannot be hidden if set on a hill .
40005015	People do not light a lamp and put it under a peck-measure , but on the stand , and it gives light for all in the house .
40005016	So let your light shine before men that they may see your good works and give glory to your Father in heaven .
40005017	" Do not think that I have come to do away with the Law or the Prophets . I have not come to do away with them , but to fill them full .
40005018	I tell you truly , until heaven and earth pass away not the smallest letter or part of a letter will pass away from the Law , until all is done .
40005019	Whoever breaks one of these commandments , the least of them , and teaches men to do so , will be called least in the kingdom of heaven , and whoever does them and teaches them , he will be called great in the kingdom of heaven .
40005020	For I say to you that , unless your righteousness far exceeds that of the scribes and Pharisees , you will not enter into the kingdom of heaven .
40005021	" You have heard that it was said to the men of old , ' Thou shalt not commit murder . Whoever commits murder shall answer for it to the court . '
40005023	So then if you are bringing your gift to lay on the altar , and there you remember that your brother has something against you ,
40005024	leave your gift there before the altar and go , first be reconciled to your brother , and then come and offer your gift .
40005025	Get on good terms with your adversary quickly while you are on the road with him , for fear that he may deliver you to the judge and the judge may deliver you to the officer and you may be cast into prison .
40005026	Truly I tell you you will not come out until you pay the last penny . "
40005027	" You have heard that it was said , ' Thou shalt not commit adultery . '
40005028	But I say to you that every one who looks at a woman with lustful thoughts has already committed adultery with her in his heart .
40005029	If your right eye is a snare to you , pluck it out and cast it from you ; for it is better for you that one of your members should be lost and not your whole body be cast into Gehenna .
40005030	And if your right hand is a snare to you , cut it off and cast it from you . It is better for you that one of your members should be lost and not your whole body go into Gehenna .
40005031	" It was said , ' Whoever divorces his wife must give her a certificate of divorce . '
40005032	But I say to you that every one who divorces his wife , unless for the cause of unchastity , makes her commit adultery , and whoever marries a divorced woman commits adultery .
40005033	" Again , you have heard that it was said to the men of old , ' Thou shalt not swear falsely , but shalt perform to the Lord thine oaths . '
40005034	But I tell you not to swear at all ; neither by heaven , because it is God's throne ;
40005035	nor by the earth , because it is his footstool ; nor by Jerusalem , because it is the city of the Great King ;
40005036	nor must you swear by your head , for you cannot make one hair white or black .
40005037	But let your yes be yes and your no be no . Whatever is more than these is from evil .
40005038	" You have heard that it was said , ' An eye for an eye and a tooth for a tooth . '
40005039	But I tell you not to resist a wicked man , but if any one strikes you on the right cheek , turn to him also the other ;
40005040	and if any one is determined to sue you for your tunic , let him have your cloak too ;
40005041	and if any one commandeers you for a mile , go with him two .
40005042	To him who begs , give ; from him who wishes to borrow of you , do not turn away .
40005043	" You have heard that it was said , ' Thou shalt love thy neighbor and hate thine enemy . '
40005044	But I say to you , Love your enemies and pray for those who persecute you ,
40005045	that you may be sons of your Father in heaven ; for he makes his sun to rise upon the bad and the good , and sends rain upon the just and the unjust .
40005046	For if you love those who love you , what reward have you ? Do not also the tax collectors do the same thing ?
40005047	And if you salute your brothers only , what superiority have you ? Do not the Gentiles do the same ?
40005048	You must be perfect as your heavenly Father is perfect .
40006001	" BE careful not to do your religious actions before men in order to be seen by them . Otherwise you have no reward from your Father in heaven .
40006002	When you give gifts of mercy , do not sound a trumpet before you as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets , in order that they may be honored by men . I assure you they get their payment in full .
40006003	But you , when you are giving a gift of mercy , must not let your left hand know what your right hand is doing ,
40006004	so that your gift may be in secret , and your Father , who sees in secret , will repay you .
40006005	" When you pray , you must not be like the hypocrites , for they love to stand and pray in the synagogues and on the street corners so as to be seen by men . I assure you they get their payment in full .
40006006	But you , when you pray , go into your inner room and shut your door and pray to your Father who is in secret , and your Father , who sees in secret , will reward you .
40006007	" When praying do not keep repeating , as the Gentiles do , for they think that they will be heard because of their multitude of words .
40006008	Do not be like them , for your Father knows what you have need of before you ask him .
40006009	Pray in this way : ' Our Father in heaven , Thy name be kept holy ;
40006010	Thy kingdom come ; Thy will prevail ; As in heaven , so on earth .
40006011	Our bread for the coming day Give us to-day ;
40006012	And forgive us our failures As we forgive those who fail toward us ;
40006013	And bring us not into trial , But save us from evil . '
40006014	For if you forgive men their wrongdoings , your heavenly Father will also forgive you ;
40006015	but if you do not forgive men , neither will your Father forgive you your wrongdoings .
40006016	" When you fast , do not wear gloomy faces as hypocrites do . For they disfigure their faces so as to be seen by men to be fasting . I assure you they get their payment in full .
40006017	But you , when fasting , anoint your head and wash your face ,
40006018	so as not to appear to men to be fasting , but to your Father who is in secret , and your Father , who sees in secret , will reward you .
40006019	" Do not lay up for yourselves treasures on the earth , where moth and rust corrode and where thieves break in and steal .
40006020	But lay up for yourselves treasures in heaven , where neither moth nor rust corrodes and where thieves do not break in nor steal .
40006021	For where your treasure is there will your heart be also .
40006022	" The lamp of the body is the eye . If your eye is clear your whole body will be lighted up ,
40006023	but if your eye is bad your whole body will be darkened . If the light that is in you is darkness , how great the darkness is !
40006024	No one can serve two masters . For either he will hate one and love the other or he will hold to one and despise the other . You cannot serve God and Mammon .
40006025	" Therefore I tell you , do not be anxious about your physical life â what you are to eat or what you are to drink ; nor about your body â what you are to wear . Is not the life more than the food and the body more than the clothing ?
40006026	Look at the birds of the air . They do not sow nor reap nor gather into barns , but your heavenly Father feeds them . Are you not of more value than they ?
40006027	But who of you by being anxious can add to his height one foot ?
40006028	And why are you anxious about clothing ? Consider the lilies of the field , bow they grow . They neither toil nor spin .
40006029	But I tell you that not even Solomon in all his splendor was arrayed like one of these .
40006030	If God so clothes the herbage of the field , to-day growing and to-morrow thrown into the oven , will he not much more clothe you , O you of so little faith ?
40006031	So do not be anxious , saying , What are we to eat ? or , What are we to drink ? or , What are we to wear ?
40006032	For all these things the pagans seek after . For your heavenly Father knows that you need all these things .
40006033	But you must seek first his kingdom and his righteousness , and all these things will be supplied to you .
40006034	Do not be anxious about to-morrow , for to-morrow will take care of itself . Enough for the day is its own trouble .
40007001	" DO not judge , so that you may not be judged .
40007002	For with whatever judgment you judge you will be judged , and with whatever measure you measure you will be measured .
40007003	Why do you look at the speck that is in your brother's eye , while you do not perceive the beam in your own eye ?
40007004	Or how will you say to your brother , ' Let me get out the speck from your eye , ' when there is a beam in your own eye ?
40007005	You hypocrite , first get the beam out of your own eye , and then you will see clearly to get the speck out of your brother's eye .
40007006	" Do not give what is holy to the dogs , nor east your pearls before swine , for they may trample them under their feet and turn and tear you .
40007007	" Ask and it will be given to you ; seek and you will find ; knock and the door will be opened .
40007008	For every one who asks obtains , and he who seeks finds , and to him who knocks the door is opened .
40007009	Is there any man of you who if his son asks him for bread will give him a stone ?
40007010	Or if he asks for a fish will give him a serpent ?
40007011	If you , though evil , know how to give good gifts to your children , how much more will your heavenly Father give good things to those who ask him .
40007012	" All things that you wish men to do for you , do yourselves for them ; for this is the Law and the Prophets .
40007013	" Enter through the narrow gate . For wide and spacious is the road that leads away to ruin , and many there are who go through it ;
40007014	but narrow is the gate and contracted is the road that leads into life , and few there are who find it .
40007015	" Beware of false prophets , such as come to you in the clothing of sheep , but inwardly are ravenous wolves .
40007016	From their fruits you will know them . Are grapes gathered from thorns or figs from thistles ?
40007017	Just so every good tree yields fine fruit , but a worthless tree yields bad fruit .
40007018	It is not possible for a good tree to yield had fruit nor for a worthless tree to yield fine fruit .
40007019	Every tree that does not yield fine fruit is cut down and thrown into the fire .
40007020	So then , from their fruits you will know them .
40007021	" Not every one who says to me , ' Master , Master , ' will enter into the kingdom of heaven , but he who does the will of my Father who is in heaven .
40007022	Many will say to me on that day , ' Master , Master , did we not prophesy in your name , and in your name east out demons , and in your name do many miracles ? '
40007023	And then I will tell them plainly , ' I never knew you . Depart from me , you who work lawlessness . '
40007024	" Every one , therefore , who hears these words of mine and does them will be like a wise man who built his house upon the rock ;
40007025	and the rain descended and the rivers rose and the winds blew , and they beat upon that house ; but it fell not , for it had been founded on the rock .
40007026	And every one who hears these words of mine and does not do them will be like a foolish man who built his house upon the sand .
40007027	And the rain descended and the rivers rose and the winds blew , and they struck upon that house and it fell , and great was the ruin of it . "
40007028	When Jesus ended these words , the crowds were astonished at his teaching .
40007029	For he taught them like one who had authority , and not as their scribes taught .
40008001	WHEN Jesus had come down from the mountain , great crowds followed him .
40008002	And a leper came up and bowed before him , and said , " Sir , if you have the will , you have power to make me clean . "
40008003	Jesus stretched out his hand and touched him and said , " I have the will , be cleansed . " Instantly his leprosy was cleansed away .
40008004	Jesus said to him , " Be sure and do not say a word to any one , but go and show yourself to the priest and offer the gift which Moses prescribed as evidence for them . "
40008005	When Jesus had entered Capernaum there came to him a Centurion who implored his help .
40008006	" Sir , " he said , " my servant lies in my house a paralytic , in great distress . "
40008007	Jesus said to him , " I will come and heal him . "
40008008	The Centurion answered , " Sir , I am not worthy to have you come under my roof ; but just speak the word and my servant will be cured .
40008009	For I am a man , â under authority , â with soldiers under me , and I say to this one , ' Go , ' and he goes , and to another , ' Come , ' and he comes , and to my slave , ' Do this , ' and he does it . "
40008010	When Jesus heard this , he was astonished and said , " Truly I tell you , I have not found so great faith on the part of any one in Israel .
40008011	I tell you many will come from the east and from the west and will recline at table with Abraham and Isaac and Jacob in the kingdom of heaven .
40008012	But the sons of the kingdom will be cast out into the darkness outside . There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth . "
40008013	Then Jesus said to the Centurion , " Go . As you have believed , so be it to you . " His servant was healed that very hour .
40008014	When Jesus entered the house of Peter , he saw his wife's mother lying sick with fever .
40008015	He touched her hand and the fever left her . Then she arose and waited upon him .
40008016	When evening came , they brought to him many demoniacs and he cast out the spirits by a word , and all their sick he healed .
40008017	This was in order to fulfill what was spoken through Isaiah the prophet , " He took our weaknesses and bore away our diseases . "
40008018	When Jesus saw a crowd around him , he gave directions to go over to the other side of the lake .
40008019	Then a certain scribe came to him and said , " Teacher , I will follow you wherever you go . "
40008020	Jesus said to him , " The foxes have holes and the birds of the air have coverts , but the Son of Man has not where to lay his head . "
40008021	Another of his disciples said to him , " Sir , let me first go and bury my father . "
40008022	But Jesus said to him , " Follow me , and let the dead bury their own dead . "
40008023	Then he got into the boat and his disciples followed him .
40008024	Soon a great storm broke on the lake so that the boat was hidden under the waves ; but he was sleeping .
40008025	His disciples came to him and woke him and said , " Master , save us . We are going down . "
40008026	But he said , " Why are you frightened , you men of little faith ? " Then he rose and rebuked the winds and the lake , and there was a great calm .
40008027	The men were astonished and said , " What sort of a person is this , whom even the winds and the lake obey ? "
40008028	When he arrived at the other side , the country of the Gadarenes , there met him two demoniacs coming out of the tombs . They were very fierce , so that no one was able to pass along that road .
40008029	Suddenly they shouted , " Son of God , what have you to do with us ? Have you come here to torment us before the time ? "
40008030	There was far off from them a herd of many swine feeding .
40008031	The demons begged him , " If you cast us out , send us into the herd of swine . "
40008032	He said to them , " Go . " So they went out and entered into the swine . Then suddenly the whole herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and died in the waves .
40008033	The herdsmen fled and went away to the town and told everything , including what had happened to the demoniacs .
40008034	Then at once all the town came out to meet Jesus , and when they saw him they begged him to depart from their neighborhood .
40009001	SO Jesus got into the boat and crossed over and came to his own city .
40009002	They brought to him a paralytic lying on a bed . When Jesus saw their faith he said to the paralytic , " Have courage , boy , your sins are forgiven . "
40009003	At once some of the scribes said to themselves , " This man is speaking profane words . "
40009004	Jesus knew their thoughts and said , " Why are you thinking evil thoughts in your hearts ?

40009012	Jesus heard it and said , " The strong have no need of a physician , but the sick have .

40009014	Then the disciples of John came to Jesus and said , " Why are we and the Pharisees fasting while your disciples are not fasting ? "
40009015	He said , " Can the bridal party fast while the bridegroom is with them ? But days will come when the bridegroom will be taken from them , and then they will fast .
40009016	No one puts a patch of unshrunk cloth on an old cloak , for the filling pulls away from the cloak and the result is a worse tear .
40009017	Nor do they pour new wine into old wine-skins , for if they do the skins burst . So the wine is spilled and the skins are ruined . But they put new wine into fresh wine-skins and both are preserved . "
40009018	While Jesus was talking to them , a synagogue Director came and bowed down before him and said , " My daughter has just died ; but come and lay your hand upon her and she will live . "
40009019	Jesus rose and followed him , and so did his disciples .
40009020	Suddenly a woman who had been suffering for twelve years from hemorrhage came up behind him and touched the tassel of his cloak .
40009021	For she said to herself , " If I touch only his cloak , I shall be healed . "
40009022	But Jesus turned and , seeing her , said , " Courage , daughter , your faith has healed you . " The woman was cured from that hour .

40009030	And their eyes were opened . Jesus sternly commanded them , " Be sure and let no one know of this . "

40010001	THEN , calling to him his twelve disciples , he gave them authority over impure spirits to cast them out , and power to cure every disease and every infirmity .
40010002	The names of the twelve apostles are these : Simon who is called Peter , and Andrew his brother , James the son of Zebedee and John his brother ,
40010003	Philip and Bartholomew , Thomas and Matthew the tax collector , James the son of Alphaeus and Thaddaeus ,

40010006	But go rather to the lost sheep of the house of Israel .
40010007	As you go proclaim , The kingdom of heaven is at hand .
40010008	Heal sick men , raise dead men , cleanse lepers , cast out demons . You received without paying , give without being paid .
40010009	Provide no gold nor silver nor copper in your belts ,
40010010	no bag for the road , nor two tunics nor shoes nor stick , for the workman has a right to his food .
40010011	Whatever city or village you go into , inquire who in it is worthy and stay with him until you leave the place .
40010012	When you enter the house , salute it .
40010013	If the house is worthy , let your peace come upon it ; but if it is not worthy , let your peace return to you .
40010014	If any one does not receive you or hear your words , as you go out of that house or that city shake off the dust of your feet .
40010015	I tell you truly it will be more tolerable for the land of Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of judgment than for that city .
40010016	See , I am sending you out as sheep in the midst of wolves . Be as wise as serpents and as pure as doves .
40010017	Be on your guard against men . For they will deliver you up to councils , and in their synagogues they will scourge you ,
40010018	and you will be brought before governors and kings for my sake , for a witness to them and to the Gentiles .
40010019	But when they deliver you up , do not worry how or what you are to speak . For it will be given to you in that hour what you are to say .
40010020	For it is not you who speak , but the Spirit of your Father that speaks within you .
40010021	Brother will betray brother to death , and father will betray child , and children will rise up against parents and put them to death .
40010022	And you will be hated by all for my name's sake . He who endures to the end , that one will be saved .
40010023	" When they persecute you in one city , flee to another . I tell you truly , you will not have gone through the cities of Israel before the Son of Man comes .
40010024	The scholar is not above his teacher , nor the servant above his master .
40010025	It is sufficient for the scholar to fare like his teacher and for the servant to fare like his master . If they have called the master of the house Beelzebul , how much more the members of his household .
40010026	Do not be afraid of them ; for there is nothing hidden which will not be revealed , nor secret which will not be known .
40010027	What I say to you in darkness speak in the light , and what is whispered into your ear proclaim on the housetops .
40010028	Do not fear before those who kill the body but cannot kill the soul . Rather fear him who can destroy both soul and body in Gehenna .
40010029	Are not two sparrows sold for a penny ? Yet one of them will not fall on the ground without your Father .
40010030	But even the hairs of your head are all numbered .
40010031	So do not fear . You are worth more than many sparrows .
40010032	Every one who shall confess me before men I too will confess before my Father in heaven .
40010033	Every one who shall disown me before men I too will disown before my Father in heaven .
40010034	" Do not think that I came to send peace on the earth . I came not to send peace , but a sword .
40010035	For I came to set a man against his father and a daughter against her mother and a daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law .
40010036	A man's enemies will be the members of his own household .
40010037	He who loves father or mother more than me is not worthy of me . He who loves son or daughter more than me is not worthy of me .
40010038	Whoever does not take his cross and follow after me is not worthy of me .
40010039	He who finds his life will lose it , and he who loses his life for my sake will find it .
40010040	He who receives you receives me , and he who receives me receives him that sent me .
40010041	He who receives a prophet because he is a prophet will get a prophet's reward , and he who receives a righteous man because he is a righteous man will get a righteous man's reward .
40010042	Whoever gives merely a cup of cold water to one of these little ones to drink because he is a disciple , I tell you truly he will not lose his reward . "
40011001	WHEN Jesus had finished instructing his twelve disciples , he went away from that place to teach and preach in the towns .

40012001	AT that time Jesus went on the Sabbath through the grain-fields . His disciples were hungry and began to pluck heads of grain to eat .
40012002	When the Pharisees saw it they said , " See , your disciples are doing what is not allowable on the Sabbath . "
40012003	He said to them , " Have you not read what David did , when he and his men were hungry ?
40012004	how he entered the house of God and ate the consecrated bread which it was not allowable either for him to eat or for his men , but only for the priests ?
40012005	Or have you not read in the Law that on the Sabbath the priests in the Temple break the Sabbath and yet are guiltless ?
40012006	I tell you that something greater than the Temple is here .
40012007	If you had understood this , ' I desire kindness and not sacrifice , ' you would not have condemned the guiltless .
40012008	For the Son of Man is lord of the Sabbath . "
40012009	Passing over from there , he came into their synagogue .
40012010	A man was there with a withered hand . They asked Jesus , " Is it allowable to heal on the Sabbath ? " â so that they might have something to accuse him of .
40012011	He said to them , " What man is there of you who , if he has one sheep , and it falls into a pit on the Sabbath , will not lay hold on it and lift it out ?
40012012	But how much more is a man worth than a sheep ! So it is allowable to do good on the Sabbath . "
40012013	Then he said to the man , " Stretch out your hand . " He stretched it out and it was restored as sound as the other .
40012014	The Pharisees went out and plotted against him how they could destroy him .

40012016	but he gave strict orders to them not to make him known .

40012018	" Behold my servant whom I have chosen , the Beloved in whom my soul delights . I will put my spirit upon him and he will proclaim justice to the Gentiles .
40012019	He will not strive nor cry , nor will any one hear his voice in the streets .
40012020	A bruised reed he will not break , and a low-burning wick he will , not quench , until he has carried justice to victory .

40012022	Then there was brought to Jesus a demoniac , blind and dumb . He healed him so that he spoke and saw .
40012023	All the crowds were astonished and said , " Is not this man the Son of David ? "
40012024	The Pharisees when they heard it said , " This man casts out demons only through Beelzebul the Chief of the demons . "
40012025	But he knew their thoughts and said to them , " Every kingdom divided against itself becomes a desolation , and no city or house divided against itself will stand .
40012026	If Satan casts out Satan , he is divided against himself . How then will his kingdom stand ?
40012027	If I by Beelzebul am casting out demons , by whom do your sons cast them out ? Therefore they shall be your judges .
40012028	But if I am casting out demons by the Spirit of God , then the kingdom of God is right upon you .
40012029	How can any one enter the house of a strong man and seize his goods unless he first binds the strong man ? Then he can plunder his house .
40012030	" He who is not with me is against me , and he who does not gather with me scatters .

40012032	Whoever says a word against the Son of Man will be forgiven , but whoever speaks against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven either in this world or in the world to come .
40012033	Either make the tree good and its fruit good or make the tree bad and its fruit bad . For from the fruit the tree is known .
40012034	Brood of vipers , how can you who are evil speak good things ? For from the overflow of the heart the mouth speaks .
40012035	The good man out of his good treasury pours out good things , and the bad man out of his bad treasury pours out bad things .
40012036	I tell you , for every idle word that men speak they will give full account in the day of judgment ,
40012037	for from your words you will be justified and from your words you will be condemned . "
40012038	Then some of the scribes and Pharisees said to him , " Teacher , we wish to see a sign from you . "

40012040	For as Jonah was in the belly of the whale three days and three nights , so will the Son of Man be in the heart of the earth three days and three nights .
40012041	The men of Nineveh will stand up at the judgment with this generation and will condemn it , for they repented at the preaching of Jonah , and more than Jonah is here .
40012042	The Queen of the South will rise up at the judgment with this generation and will condemn it , for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon , and more than Solomon is here .
40012043	" When the impure spirit has gone out of a man , he passes through waterless places seeking rest and finds none .
40012044	Then he says , ' I will return into my house that I left . ' And he comes and finds it vacant , swept and in order .
40012045	Then he goes and takes with him seven other spirits worse than himself , and they enter and live there . So the last state of that man becomes worse than the first . Just so will it be with this wicked generation . "
40012046	While Jesus was still speaking to the crowds , his mother and his brothers were standing outside , trying to speak to him .

40013001	ON that day Jesus went out of the house and sat beside the lake .
40013002	Great crowds gathered to him so that he got into a boat and sat in it , while all the crowd stood on the shore .
40013003	He spoke at length to them in illustrations . " A sower , " he said , " went out to sow .
40013004	And as he was sowing some seeds fell at the roadside and the birds came and ate them up .
40013005	Others fell on rocky places where they had not much soil , and at once they sprang up because they had no depth of soil .
40013006	But when the sun rose they were scorched , and because they had no roots they withered .
40013007	Others fell among thorns and the thorns grew up and choked them .
40013008	Others fell on good ground and made a yield , some of a hundred fold , some of sixty fold , some of thirty fold .
40013009	He who has ears , let him hear . "
40013010	Then his disciples came to him and said , " Why do you talk to them in figures of speech ? "
40013011	He answered , " Because to you it is granted to know the mysteries of the kingdom of heaven , but to those people it is not granted .
40013012	For whoever has , to him will be given and he will have abundance . But whoever has not , from him will be taken even what he has .
40013013	For this reason I speak to them in figures , because , though they see , they do not see , and though they hear , they do not hear nor understand ,
40013014	and to them is fulfilled the prophecy of Isaiah : ' You will plainly hear , but you will not understand , and you will clearly look , but you will not see .
40013015	For the heart of these people has grown fat , and with their ears they are dull of hearing and their eyes they have closed ; so that they may not see with their eyes and hear with their ears and understand with their heart and repent and I should heal them . '
40013016	But blessed are your eyes , for they see , and your ears , for they hear .
40013017	I tell you truly many prophets and righteous men desired to see the things you see , but they did not see them , and to hear the things you hear , but they did not hear them .
40013018	So listen to the story of the sower :
40013019	When any one hears the message of the kingdom and does not understand it , the Evil One comes and snatches away what was sown in his heart . This is the man who receives seed by the roadside .
40013020	He who received seed on stony ground is he who bears the word and receives it at once with joy ,
40013021	yet has no root in himself , but is inconstant , and when trouble or persecution arises on account of the message he stumbles and falls .
40013022	He who received seed among thorns is he who hears the message , but the care of the world and the deceitfulness of wealth choke the message and it becomes fruitless .
40013023	He who received seed in good ground is he who hears the message and understands it and makes a yield of a hundred , or sixty , or thirty fold . "
40013024	Another illustration he put before them . He said , " The kingdom of heaven is like a man who sowed good seed in his field .
40013025	But while people were sleeping his enemy came and sowed weeds through the wheat , and went away .
40013026	When the blades shot up and formed grain , the weeds also appeared .
40013027	Then the servants of the owner came and said to him , ' Sir , did you not sow good seed in your field ? Where do the weeds come from ? '
40013028	He replied , ' An enemy did this . ' The servants said to him , ' Do you want us to go and gather them up ? '
40013029	He said , ' No , for in gathering up the weeds you might pull up the wheat along with them .
40013030	Let both grow together until the harvest . At the time of harvest I will say to the harvesters , Gather up first the weeds and tie them into bundles for burning , but bring the wheat into my granary . ' "
40013031	Another illustration he put before them . He said , " The kingdom of heaven is like a mustard seed which a man took and sowed in his field .
40013032	It is the least of all the seeds , but when it grows up it is greater than the garden herbs and becomes a tree , so that the birds of the air come and live in its branches . "
40013033	Another illustration he spoke to them . " The kingdom of heaven is like yeast which a woman took and hid in three measures of flour until it was all leavened . "
40013034	All of these things Jesus spoke to them in illustrations , and without an illustration he spoke nothing to them ,
40013035	to fulfill the words of the prophet when he said , " I will open my mouth in illustrations , I will utter things hidden since the foundation of the world . "
40013036	Then leaving the crowds he came into the house , and his disciples came to him and said , " Explain to us the illustration of the weeds of the field . "
40013037	He replied , " He who sows the good seeds is the Son of Man .
40013038	The field is the world . The good seeds are the sons of the kingdom . The weeds are the sons of the Evil One .
40013039	The enemy that sowed them is the Devil . The harvest is the end of the world . The reapers are angels .
40013040	As the weeds are gathered up and burned with fire , so shall it be at the end of the world .
40013041	The Son of Man will send his angels and they will gather up from his kingdom all stumbling-blocks and those who practice lawlessness ,
40013042	and will cast them into the furnace of fire . There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth .
40013043	Then will the righteous shine out like the sun in the kingdom of their Father . He who has ears , let him hear .
40013044	" The kingdom of heaven is like treasure hidden in a field , which a man finds and hides again , and for joy goes and sells all that he has and buys that field .
40013045	" Again the kingdom of heaven is like a merchant in search of fine pearls .
40013046	Having found one very precious pearl he went away and sold everything that he had and bought it .
40013047	" Again the kingdom of heaven is like a net cast into the lake that gathered up every sort .
40013048	But when it was filled they drew it to the beach and sat down and gathered the good into pails , but threw the worthless away .
40013049	So will it be at the end of the world . The angels will come forth and will separate the wicked from among the righteous
40013050	and will cast them into the furnace of fire . There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth .
40013051	Have you understood all these things ? " They said , " Yes . "
40013052	He said to them , " Therefore every scribe educated in the kingdom of heaven is like a man who is a householder who brings out from his storehouse new things and old things . "
40013053	When Jesus had finished these illustrations , he went away from that place .
40013054	Then he came to his native place and taught them in their synagogue so that they were astonished and said , " Where did this man get this wisdom and these miracles ?
40013055	Is not this the carpenter's son ? Is not his mother named Mary and his brothers James and Joseph and Simon and Judas ?
40013056	And his sisters â are they not all here with us ? Where then did he get all this ? "
40013057	So they fell into mistake about him . But Jesus said to them , " A prophet is not without honor except in his native place and in his own house . "
40013058	Because of their unbelief he worked there but few miracles .

40015001	THEN scribes and Pharisees came to Jesus from Jerusalem and said ,
40015002	" Why do your disciples violate the tradition of our forefathers ? For they do not wash their hands when they eat food . "
40015003	He answered them , " And why do you violate the command of God for the sake of your tradition ?
40015004	For God said , ' Honor thy father and thy mother , ' and , ' If any one speaks evil of father or mother , let him surely die . '

40020001	" THE kingdom of heaven is like a man who was a householder , who went out in the early morning to hire laborers for his vineyard .

41001001	THE Beginning of the Good News of Jesus Christ .
41001002	It is written in Isaiah the prophet , " Behold , I am sending my messenger before your face , who will prepare your way .

41004001	AGAIN Jesus began to teach beside the lake , and a very great crowd gathered around him , so that he got into a boat on the lake and sat down , and all the crowd was on the shore near the lake .
41004002	He taught them many things by figures of speech . He said to them in his teaching ,
41004003	" Listen ; a sower went out to sow ,
41004004	and it happened , as he was sowing , that some seed fell beside the road and the birds came and ate it .
41004005	Other seed fell on stony places where it had not much earth , and it sprang up at once because it had no depth of soil ,
41004006	but when the sun came up it was scorched and because it had no root it withered away .
41004007	Other seed fell among thorns and the thorns grew up and choked it and it yielded no grain .
41004008	Other seed fell into good ground and grew tall and strong and yielded thirty , sixty , or a hundred fold . "
41004009	He said to them , " Let him who has ears to hear with hear . "
41004010	When he was alone , his close friends and the twelve asked him about the illustrations .
41004011	He replied , " To you the mystery of the kingdom of God has been confided . But to outsiders all things come in figures of speech
41004012	so that they may look straight and yet not see , and hear plainly , yet not understand , and thus they will never repent and be forgiven . "
41004013	He said to them , " Do you not understand this illustration ? How , then , will you understand all the illustrations ?
41004014	The sower sows the word .
41004015	These are those in whom the message is sown by the roadside â such as hear , but immediately Satan comes and takes away the message that was sown in their minds .
41004016	These are they likewise who received seed on stony places â such as hear and immediately and gladly receive the word ,

41006001	LEAVING there , he came to his own native place accompanied by his disciples .

41007001	ONCE the Pharisees gathered about him with some of the scribes who had come from Jerusalem ,
41007002	and they saw that some of his disciples were eating bread with " common , " that is , unwashed , hands .
41007003	For the Pharisees and all the Jews never eat without first washing their hands up to the wrist , holding faithfully to the tradition of their forefathers ,
41007004	and when they return from market they do not eat until they have washed . There are also many other traditions which they have been taught to hold tenaciously , such as washing cups and pitchers and copper vessels .
41007005	The Pharisees and scribes asked him , " Why do not your disciples live according to the tradition of our fore-fathers ? Why do they eat their bread with common hands ? "
41007006	He replied , " Well did Isaiah prophesy about you hypocrites when he wrote : ' This people honor me with their lips , but their heart is far from me ;
41007007	in vain they worship me , while they teach what are merely commandments of men . '
41007008	Neglecting the commands of God , you hold firmly to the traditions of men . "
41007009	He said further to them , " How thoroughly you set aside the command of God so that you may keep your tradition !
41007010	For Moses said , ' Honor thy father and thy mother , ' and , ' He who speaks evil of father or mother must surely die . '

41007012	you no longer let him do anything for his father or his mother ,

41007017	After he had gone into the house , his disciples asked about his figurative language .

41007019	for it does not go into his heart , but into his stomach and passes out into the sewer ? " Thus he pronounced all foods clean .
41007020	" But , " he said , " what comes out of a man is what defiles him ;
41007021	for from within , out of the hearts of men , come evil thoughts , unchastities , thefts , murders ,
41007022	adulteries , lusts , wickednesses , deceit , sensuality , an evil eye , slander , arrogance , recklessness â
41007023	all these had things come out from within , and they defile the man . "
41007024	Leaving that place , Jesus went into the borders of Tyre . He entered a house and did not wish any one to know it , but he could not escape notice .

41011015	They came to Jerusalem , and he went into the Temple courts and began to cast out those who were buying and selling there . He overturned the tables of the money-changers and the seats of the dove-sellers ,
41011016	and would not allow any one to carry anything through the Temple courts ,
41011017	for he taught and said to them , " Is it not written , ' My house shall be called a house of prayer for all the nations ' ? But you have made it a den of robbers . "
41011018	When the high priests and the scribes heard of this they tried to contrive to put him out of the way , for they were afraid of him because the people were deeply impressed by his teaching .
41011019	When evening came , Jesus and his disciples used to go out of the city .
41011020	As they were passing by early in the morning they saw the fig tree withered from the roots .
41011021	Peter , calling to mind , said to him , " Rabbi , see , the fig tree that you cursed has withered up . "
41011022	Jesus answered , " Have faith in God .
41011023	I tell you truly whoever says to this mountain , ' Be taken up and be cast into the sea , ' and does not doubt in his mind , but believes that what he says will be , will have it .
41011024	For this reason I say to you , all things whatever that you pray and ask for , believe that you have obtained them and you will have them .
41011025	And when you stand praying , forgive if you have anything against any one , so that your Father in heaven may forgive you your failings . "
41011027	They came again to Jerusalem , and as he was walking about in the Temple courts , the high priests and the scribes came to him
41011028	and said , " By what authority do you do these things ? Or who gave you authority to do them ? "
41011029	Jesus replied , " I will ask you one question ; answer me and I will tell you by what authority I am doing these things .
41011030	The baptism of John â was it from heaven or of men ? Answer me . "
41011031	But they discussed among themselves , " If we say ' From heaven , ' he will say , ' Then why did you not believe him ? '
41011032	But if we say , ' From men , ' â they feared the people , for all regarded John as really a prophet .
41011033	So they answered Jesus , " We do not know . " And he replied , " Neither will I tell you by what power I am doing these things . "
41012001	THEN he began to speak to them in figures : " There was a man who planted a vineyard and put a fence around it and dug for a wine-vat , and built a tower and let it out to grape-growers , and then went abroad .
41012002	At the proper season he sent a servant to the grape-growers to receive from them some of the fruits of the vineyard .
41012003	But they took him and beat him and sent him away empty-handed .
41012004	Again he sent another servant to them , and him they beat over the head and insulted .
41012005	He sent another , and him they killed . He sent many others , some of whom were beaten and some killed .
41012006	He had still one , a beloved son . He sent him last to them , saying , ' They will respect my son . '
41012007	But those grape-growers said to one another , ' This is the heir . Come , let us kill him and the inheritance will be ours . '
41012008	Then they took him and killed him and threw him out of the vineyard .
41012009	What will the owner of the vineyard do ? He will come and destroy the grape-growers and will give the vineyard to others .
41012010	Have you never read this Scripture , ' The stone which the builders despised has become the chief stone of the corner ;
41012011	this corner stone came from the Lord and is wonderful in our eyes ' ? "
41012012	They kept trying to seize him , but were afraid of the crowd . For they knew that he had meant the illustration for them . So they left him and went away .
41012013	Then they sent to him some of the Pharisees and of the Herodians to entrap him in his talk .
41012014	When they came , they said to him , " Teacher , we know that you are true and are not afraid of any one ; for you do not look at the social standing of men , but you teach the way of God in truth . Is it right to pay tribute to Caesar or not ?
41012015	Shall we pay or shall we not pay ? " But he , knowing their hypocrisy , said to them , " Why are you testing me ? Bring me a coin and let me see it . "
41012016	They brought one . Then he said , " Whose head is this and whose inscription ? " They said to him , " Caesar's . "
41012017	Jesus said to them , " Pay what is Caesar's to Caesar , and what is God's to God . " They were astonished at him .
41012018	Then there came to him some Sadducees , who say that there is no resurrection . They asked him ,
41012019	" Teacher , Moses wrote a law for us that if any man's brother dies and leaves a wife , but no child , the brother shall take the wife and raise up off-spring for his brother .
41012020	Now there were seven brothers . The first took a wife and died leaving no child ,
41012021	then the second took her and died leaving no child , then the third likewise .
41012022	None of the seven left any child . Last of all the woman died also .
41012023	In the resurrection when they rise again whose wife will she be ? For the seven had her as wife . "
41012024	Jesus said to them , " Do you not err for the reason that you do not know either the Scriptures or the power of God ?
41012025	For when they rise from the dead , they neither marry nor are given in marriage , but are like the angels in heaven .
41012026	And concerning the dead , that they rise , have you not read in the book of Moses in the passage about the Bush , how God said to him , ' I am the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac and the God of Jacob ' ?
41012027	He is not a God of dead men , but of living men . You are much mistaken . "
41012028	Then came one of the scribes , and , after listening to their discussion and knowing that he had answered them well , asked , " Which is the first commandment of all ? "
41012029	Jesus answered , " The first is , ' Hear , O Israel , the Lord our God is one Lord ,
41012030	and thou shalt love the Lord thy God with all thy heart and with all thy soul and with all thy mind and with all thy strength . '
41012031	This is the second , ' Thou shalt love thy neighbor as thyself . ' There is no other commandment greater than these . "
41012032	The scribe said to him , " Right , teacher ; you have said truly that he is one and there is no other beside him ,
41012033	and to love him with all the heart and with all the understanding and with all the strength and to love one's neighbor as one's self is more than all the whole burnt offerings and sacrifices . "
41012034	Jesus , seeing that he had answered with intelligence , said to him , " You are not far from the kingdom of God . " After that no one dared question him further .
41012035	Then Jesus asked , while teaching in the Temple courts , " How do the scribes say that the Christ is the son of David ?
41012036	David himself , guided by the Holy Spirit , said , ' The Lord said to my Lord , sit at my right hand till I put your enemies under your feet . '
41012037	David himself called him ' Lord ' ; how is he then his son ? " A great crowd listened to him with delight .
41012038	In his teaching he said , " Beware of the scribes , who like to walk about in long robes and to have greetings in the market-places
41012039	and front seats in the synagogues and the best couches at banquets .
41012040	They eat up widows ' houses and hypocritically make long prayers . These men will receive a severer condemnation . "
41012041	Having seated himself across from the contribution box , he was watching how the crowd dropped money into the box . Many rich people were dropping in large gifts .
41012042	There came a poor widow and dropped in two mites , in value one penny .
41012043	Then Jesus called his disciples to him and said to them , " I tell you truly , this widow , poor as she is , has dropped in more than all the others who are dropping money into the contribution box .
41012044	For they all contributed out of their superfluity , but she out of her poverty dropped in all that she had â the whole of what she had to live on . "
41013001	AS he was going out of the Temple courts , one of his disciples said to him , " Teacher , see what great stones and what great buildings ! "
41013002	Jesus said to him , " Do you see these great buildings ? There will not be left one stone upon another which will not be thrown down . "
41013003	Then , when he was sitting on the Mount of Olives across from the Temple buildings , Peter and James and John and Andrew asked him privately ,

41013008	For nation will rise against nation and kingdom against kingdom . There will be earthquakes in various places and there will be famines . These things are the beginning of birth-pangs .

41013015	and let him who is on top of the house not descend and enter to take anything from his house ,

41013028	" From the fig tree learn a comparison . When once her branch becomes tender and puts out leaves , you know that summer is near .
41013029	So , when you see these things happening , know that he is nigh , yes , at the door .
41013030	I tell you truly that this generation will not pass away until all these things come to pass .
41013031	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will not pass away .
41013032	" But of that day or that hour no one knows , not even the angels in heaven , not even the Son , but the Father only .
41013033	" Be watchful , be wakeful , for you do not know when the time is .
41013034	It is just as when a man going abroad leaves his house and gives to his servants authority and to each his work and commands the porter to watch .
41013035	Watch , therefore , for you do not know when the Master of the house will come , whether at evening or at midnight or at cock-crowing or in the morning .
41013036	Otherwise coming suddenly he may find you sleeping .
41013037	What I say to you , I say to all , Watch . "
41014001	THE Passover and the Feast of Unleavened Bread were to come after two days . The high priests and the scribes were contriving how they might seize him by some stratagem and kill him .
41014002	For they said , " Not at the feast ; there might be a popular outbreak . "

42001001	INASMUCH as many have taken in hand to draw up a narrative of those facts which are firmly believed among us ,
42001002	just as those who from the beginning were eye-witnesses and who became bearers of the message handed them down to us ;
42001003	it has seemed good to me also â since I have followed everything from the beginning accurately â to write a consecutive account for you , most excellent Theophilus ,
42001004	so that you may know the exact truth in regard to the matters which you have been taught by word of mouth .
42001005	There was in the days of Herod , King of Judaea , a certain priest by the name of Zacharias , of the course of Abijah . His wife was of the daughters of Aaron , and her name was Elizabeth .
42001006	They were both righteous before God , walking in all the commandments and regulations of the Lord blameless .
42001007	But they had no child , for Elizabeth was barren , and they were both advanced in years .
42001008	It happened that as Zacharias was performing his priestly duties before God in the order of his course ,
42001009	according to the custom of the priesthood , it fell to him to enter the Temple of the Lord and offer the incense .
42001010	All the congregation of people was in prayer outside , at the hour of incense .

42005001	IT happened that , as the crowd was pressing upon him and listening to the word of God , he was standing on the shore of Lake Gennesaret ,

42005005	Simon answered , " Master , we have worked all night and caught nothing . But at your word I will let down the nets . "

42005037	And no one puts new wine into old wine-skins . If he did , the new wine would burst the skins and it would be spilled , and the skins would be ruined .
42005038	But new wine must be put into new wine-skins .
42005039	And no one after drinking old wine wishes to drink new , for he says , ' The old is fine . ' "
