42006006	It happened on another Sabbath that he went into the synagogue and was teaching . There was a man there whose right hand was withered .
42006007	The scribes and Pharisees watched to see whether he would heal him on the Sabbath , wishing to find something to accuse him of .
42006008	But he knew their thoughts and said to the man with the withered hand , " Rise , and stand in the center . " He rose and stood .
42006009	Jesus said to them , " I ask you , is it lawful on the Sabbath to do good or to do evil , to save life or to destroy it ? "
42006010	He looked around at all of them , then said to the man , " Stretch out your hand . " He did so and his hand was restored .
42006011	But they were filled with blind fury , and discussed with one another what they could do to Jesus .
42006012	It happened during those days that he went out to the mountain and prayed and was all night in prayer to God .
42006013	When day came , he called to him his disciples and chose from them twelve , whom also he named " Apostles " :
42006014	Simon , whom he named Peter , and Andrew his brother , and James and John , and Philip and Bartholomew ,
42006015	and Matthew and Thomas , and James the son of Alphaeus , and Simon called the Zealot ,
42006016	and Judas the son of James , and Judas Iscariot , who became a traitor .
42006017	He went down with them and stood on a level spot where were gathered a great crowd of his disciples and a great multitude of people from all Judaea and Jerusalem and the sea-coast of Tyre and Sidon , who had come to hear him and to be cured of their diseases .
42006018	Those who were troubled by impure spirits were healed .
42006019	The whole crowd tried to touch him , because power went out from him and healed all .
42006020	He raised his eyes to his disciples and said : " Blessed are you poor ! For yours is the kingdom of God .
42006021	" Blessed are you who are hungry now ! For you will be abundantly fed . " Blessed are you who are weeping now ! For you will laugh .
42006022	" Blessed are you when men hate you and when they shut you out and reproach you and cast out your name as evil because of the Son of Man !
42006023	Rejoice on that day and leap for joy . For , indeed , your reward will be great in heaven . Just so their fathers treated the prophets .
42006024	" But alas for you rich men ! For you have now your comfort in full .
42006025	" Alas for you who are filled now ! For you will hunger . " Alas for you who are laughing now ! For you will mourn and wail .
42006026	" Alas for you , when all men speak well of you ! Just so their fathers treated the false prophets .
42006027	But I tell you , my hearers , love your enemies ; act nobly to those who hate you ;
42006028	bless those who curse you ; pray for those who insult you .
42006029	To him who strikes you on one cheek , offer also the other . To him who takes your cloak , do not refuse your tunic .
42006030	To every one who asks , give , and from him who takes your things , do not ask them back .
42006031	Do to men just as you wish them to do to you .
42006032	If you love those who love you , what grace have you ? For sinners also love those who love them .
42006033	If you do good to those who do good to you , what grace have you ? Sinners also do the same .
42006034	If you lend to those from whom you hope to receive , what grace have you ? Sinners also lend to sinners in order to get back as much .
42006035	But love your enemies and do good and lend without hope of return , and your reward will be great and you will be sons of the Most High . For he is generous to the ungrateful and wicked .
42006036	Become compassionate as your Father is compassionate .
42006037	Do not judge and you will not be judged . Do not condemn and you will not be condemned . Forgive and you will be forgiven .
42006038	Give and it will be given to you . Good measure , pressed in , shaken down , and running over they will pour into your lap . For with the measure that you measure with will the return to you be measured . "
42006039	He gave them an illustration : " The blind cannot lead the blind , can he ? Will not both fall into the ditch ?
42006040	A scholar is not superior to his teacher . Every scholar when finished will be like his teacher .
42006041	Why do you look at the speck in your brother's eye while you do not perceive the beam in your own eye ?
42006042	How can you say to your brother , ' Brother , let me get out the speck that is in your eye , ' while you yourself never notice the beam in your own eye ? Hypocrite , take out first the beam from your own eye , and then you will see clearly to get out the speck in your brother's eye .
42006043	" There is no good tree that yields worthless fruit , nor is there a worthless tree that yields fine fruit .
42006044	Every tree will be known by its own fruit . They do not gather figs from thorns , nor from a bramble-bush do they harvest grapes .
42006045	A good man from the good treasury of his heart brings forth what is good , and the evil man from his evil treasury brings forth what is evil . Out of the overflow of the heart the mouth speaks .
42006046	" Why do you call me : ' Master , Master , ' and yet not do what I say ?
42006047	Every one who comes to me and hears my words and does them , I will show you whom he is like .
42006048	He is like a man building a house , who dug and went deep and laid a foundation on the rock . When a flood came , the river dashed against that house , and could not shake it , because it had been well built .
42006049	But he who hears and does not do is like a man building a house on the earth without foundation , against which the river dashed , and at once it fell , and the wreck of that house was great . "
42007001	WHEN he had finished all his discourses in the hearing of the people , he went into Capernaum .
42007002	The servant of a certain Centurion was sick and about to die . He was highly valued by his master ,
42007003	who hearing about Jesus sent to him some elders of the Jews , asking him to come and save his servant .
42007004	When they came to Jesus they begged him earnestly , saying , " He deserves to have this done ,
42007005	for he loves our nation and he built us our synagogue . "
42007006	Jesus went with them . When he was not far from the house , the Centurion sent friends to say to him , " Do not trouble yourself , Sir , for I am not fit to have you come under my roof .
42007007	On that account I did not think myself worthy to come to you . But say the word and have my servant cured .
42007008	For I am a man â under authority â with soldiers under me , and I say to this one , ' Go , ' and he goes , and to that one , ' Come , ' and he comes , and to my slave , ' Do this , ' and he does it . "
42007009	When Jesus heard this , he wondered , and , turning to the crowd that was following him , he said , " I tell you , in Israel I have not found such faith . "
42007010	Those who had been sent returned to the house and found the servant well .
42007011	It happened soon afterwards that he went to a city called Nain , and his disciples and a great crowd were going along with him .
42007012	As he approached the gate of the city , they were carrying out a dead man , the only son of his mother , and she was a widow . A great crowd from the city was with her .
42007013	When the Master saw her , he had compassion on her and said to her , " Do not weep , "
42007014	and he went up and touched the bier . The bearers stopped . He said , " Young man , I say , arise ! "
42007015	The dead man sat up and began to speak , and he gave him to his mother .
42007016	All were awe-struck , and they gave praise to God , saying , " A great prophet has arisen among us and God has visited his people . "
42007017	The reports about him spread through all Judaea and all the region of the Jordan .
42007018	John's disciples told him about all these things .
42007019	So he called to him two of his disciples and sent them to the Master to ask , " Are you ' the Coming One ' or are we to expect some other person ? "
42007020	When they came to him , the men said , " John the Baptist sent us to you to ask , Are you ' the Coming One ' or are we to expect some other person ? "
42007021	At that very time he was curing many of diseases and pains and wicked spirits , and to many blind people he was giving sight .
42007022	He answered them , " Go and relate to John what you have seen and heard . Blind men see , lame men walk , lepers are cleansed , deaf men hear , dead men are raised , poor men hear good news .
42007023	Blessed is he who does not stumble through misunderstanding me ! "
42007024	After John's messengers had left , Jesus began to speak to the crowds about John : " What did you go out into the wild country to look at ? A reed shaken by the wind ?
42007025	But what did you go out to see ? A man dressed in soft clothes ? Indeed , the people in splendid clothing and living in luxury are in kings ' palaces .
42007026	But what did you go out to see ? A prophet ? Yes , I tell you , and more than a prophet .
42007027	For this is he about whom it was written , ' Behold , I send my messenger before your face , who will make ready your way before you . '
42007028	I tell you there is not among those born of women a greater than John . But an inferior in the kingdom of God is greater than he . "
42007029	( All the people , even the tax collectors when they heard him , had confessed that God was right by being baptized with the baptism of John .
42007030	But the Pharisees and the lawyers had thwarted the purpose of God in reference to themselves by not being baptized by him . )
42007031	" To what then shall I compare the men of this generation ? What are they like ?
42007032	They are like children sitting in the market-place and calling to one another , ' We played the flute for you but you did not dance . We mourned but you did not wail ! '
42007033	For John the Baptist has come , not eating bread nor drinking wine , and you say , ' He has a demon . '
42007034	The Son of Man has come eating and drinking , and you say , ' See there a man who is a glutton and wine-drinker , a friend of tax collectors and sinners ! '
42007035	Yet Wisdom is shown to be in the right by all her children . "
42007036	One of the Pharisees kept asking him to dine with him . Entering the house of this Pharisee , he reclined at the table .
42007037	Now there was a certain woman in the city , a sinner , and when she learned that he was at table in the Pharisee's house , she brought an alabaster jar of ointment
42007038	and took her place behind , beside his feet , weeping . Her tears began to rain down on his feet , and with the hair of her head she wiped them off , and she passionately kissed his feet and anointed them with the ointment .
42007039	When the Pharisee who had invited him saw this , he said within himself , " This man , if he were a prophet , would have known who and what this woman who is touching him is , for she is a sinner . "
42007040	Jesus , answering his thought , said to him , " Simon , I have something to say to you . " " Teacher , " he said , " say it . "
42007041	" A certain money-lender had two debtors ; one owed him five hundred shillings ; the other fifty .
42007042	Because they had nothing to pay with , he graciously forgave both . Which of them will love him most ? "
42007043	Simon answered , " I suppose the one to whom he forgave most . " He said to him , " You have answered correctly . "
42007044	Then , turning to the woman , he said to Simon , " Do you see this woman ? I entered your house ; you gave me no water for my feet . But she has rained tears upon my feet and has wiped them with her hair .
42007045	You gave me no kiss , but she , since I came in , has not ceased passionately kissing my feet .
42007046	My head with oil you did not anoint , but she has anointed my feet with ointment .
42007047	For this reason I tell you her sins , many as they are , have been forgiven , for she loved much . For he to whom little is forgiven loves little . "
42007048	He said to her , " Your sins have been forgiven . "
42007049	The other guests began to say to themselves , " Who is this that even forgives sins ? "
42007050	He said to the woman , " Your faith has saved you . Go in peace . "
42008001	SHORTLY afterwards he was making his way through cities and villages preaching and telling the good news of the kingdom of God . The twelve were with him ,
42008002	and certain women who had been relieved of evil spirits and infirmities â Mary , who was called Magdalene , out of whom seven demons had gone ,
42008003	and Joanna , the wife of Chuzas , Herod's manager , and Susanna , and many others . These women provided for Jesus and his apostles out of their means .
42008004	When a great multitude was coming together and some from every city were crowding upon him , he spoke to them with an illustration :
42008005	" A sower went out to sow his seed . As he sowed , some seed fell along the roadside and was trodden on , and the birds of heaven ate it up .
42008006	Other seed fell on the rock , and when it sprang up it withered away because it had no moisture .
42008007	Other seed fell among thorns , and the thorns grew up with it and choked it .
42008008	Other seed fell into the good ground , and grew up and yielded a harvest a hundred fold . " When he said this , he called out , " Let him who has ears to hear , hear . "
42008009	His disciples kept asking him what the illustration meant .
42008010	He said : " To you it is granted to know the mysteries of the kingdom of God . But to the rest the message comes in figures of speech , so that although they see they may not see , and although they hear they may not understand .
42008011	This is the illustration : The seed is the message of God .
42008012	Those by the roadside are those who hear , and then the Devil comes and takes away the message from their hearts so that they may not believe and be saved .
42008013	Those on the rock are those who , though they receive the message with joy , yet have no root , who for a while believe , but in the time of trial desert .
42008014	That which fell among thorns means those who hear , and as they go on are choked by the cares and riches and pleasures of life and bring nothing to completion .
42008015	That in the good ground means those who with a noble and good heart hear the message and hold it fast and bear fruit in patience .
42008016	" No one lights a lamp and hides it with a bowl or puts it under a bed . No , he puts it on a stand so that all who come in may see the light .
42008017	For there is nothing hidden which will not become manifest , nor secret which will not be known and come to light .
42008018	Be careful , then , how you hear ; for whoever has , to him will be given , and whoever has not , even what he seems to have will be taken away from him . "
42008019	His mother and his brothers came where he was , but could not get to him on account of the crowd .
42008020	It was told him , " Your mother and your brothers are standing outside wishing to see you . "
42008021	He answered , " My mother and my brothers are these who are hearing the word of God and doing it . "
42008022	It happened one day that he got into a boat , and his disciples went with him . He said to them , " Let us cross over to the other side of the lake . " They put out .
42008023	While they were sailing he fell asleep . A gale of wind came down on the lake and the boat was filling and in peril .
42008024	Coming to him , they awoke him , saying , " Master , Master , we are going down ! " He awoke and rebuked the wind and the waves . They grew quiet and there was a calm .
42008025	He said to the disciples , " Where is your faith ? " They were awed and amazed , and said to one another , " Who then is this man who commands the winds and the water and they obey him ? "
42008026	They sailed to the land of the Gerasenes , which is across from Galilee .
42008027	When he got out on to the land , there met him a certain man from that city who had demons . For a long time he had not worn clothes and had not lived in a house , but in the tombs .
42008028	When he saw Jesus , he screamed and fell down before him , and in a loud voice said , " What have I to do with you , Jesus , Son of God Most High ? I pray you , do not torment me . "
42008029	For he had commanded the impure spirit to come out of the man . Many times it had seized him , and , though he was bound with chains and fetters and kept under guard , yet bursting his chains he would be driven by the demon off into the wilds .

42008031	They begged him not to bid them go away into the abyss .
42008032	There was near by a herd of many swine feeding on the mountain . The demons begged him to permit them to go into the swine . He gave them leave .
42008033	The demons left the man and entered the swine , and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and were drowned .
42008034	The herdsmen , seeing what had happened , fled and told it in the city and on the farms .
42008035	The people came out to see what had happened . When they came to Jesus , they found the man from whom the demons had gone out sitting at the feet of Jesus , clothed and in his right mind , and they were struck with awe .
42008036	Those who had seen it told them how the demoniac had been cured .
42008037	Whereupon all the crowd from the region of the Gerasenes asked him to go away from them , for they were seized with great fear . So he got into a boat and returned .
42008038	The man from whom the demons had gone out begged him to let him be with him . But he sent him away , saying ,

42008040	As Jesus came back , a crowd welcomed him , for all were expecting him .
42008041	There came a man by the name of Jairus â he was a synagogue director . Falling at the feet of Jesus , he begged him to come to his house
42008042	because he had an only daughter , about twelve years old , and she was dying . As he was going the crowds pressed around him .

42008045	Jesus said , " Who is it that touched me ? " All denied , and Peter said , " Master , the crowd is pressing upon you on every side . "
42008046	Jesus said , " Some one touched me , for I know that power has gone forth from me . "
42008047	The woman , seeing that she had not escaped notice , came trembling and fell before him , and told before all the people why she had touched him and how she was instantly cured .
42008048	He said to her , " Daughter , your faith has healed you . Go in peace . "
42008049	While he was still speaking some one came from the Director's house , saying , " Your daughter is dead . Do not trouble the teacher any longer . "
42008050	Jesus heard it and said to him , " Never fear . Only believe and she will be saved . "

42008053	They laughed at him , knowing that she was dead .
42008054	But he took hold of her hand and said to her , " Little girl , rise up . "
42008055	Her spirit returned and at once she stood up . He told them to give her something to eat .
42008056	Her parents were amazed , but he told them not to tell any one of what had happened .
42009001	JESUS called together the twelve and gave them power and authority over all demons and to cure diseases .

42010001	AFTER this , the Master appointed seventy others and sent them out two and two before him into every city and place where he was soon to come .

42010004	Carry no purse , no bag , no shoes , and salute no one by the way .
42010005	Whatever house you enter , first say , ' Peace be to this house . '

42010023	Turning to his disciples , he said privately , " Blessed are your eyes that see what you see !
42010024	I tell you , many prophets and kings wished to see the things that you see and did not see them , and to hear the things that you hear and did not hear them . "
42010025	Then a certain lawyer stood up to test him , and said , " Teacher , what must I do to inherit life eternal ? "
42010026	He said to him , " What is written in the Law ? How do you read it ? "
42010027	He answered , " ' Thou shalt love the Lord thy God with all thy heart and with all thy soul and with all thy strength and with all thy mind , and thy neighbor as thyself . '
42010028	Jesus said to him , " You have answered correctly ; do this and you will live . "
42010029	But he , wishing to justify himself , said to Jesus , " And who is my neighbor ? "
42010030	Jesus rejoined , " A certain man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho and fell among robbers , who stripped him and beat him and went away leaving him half dead .
42010031	By chance a certain priest was going down that road . When he saw him , he went by on the other side .
42010032	In the same way a Levite came to the place and saw him , and passed by on the other side .
42010033	But a certain Samaritan as he traveled came near him , and saw him and pitied him ,
42010034	and went to him and bandaged his wounds , pouring on them oil and wine . Then placing him on his own beast he took him to the inn and cared for him .
42010035	The next morning he took out two shillings and gave them to the inn-keeper and said , ' Care for him , and what evermore you spend , I will pay in full when I come back . '
42010036	Which of these three seems to you to have become neighbor to the man who fell among the robbers ? "
42010037	He said , " He who did kindness to him . " Jesus said to him , " Go and act in the same way yourself . "
42010038	As they journeyed , he entered a certain village . There a woman named Martha welcomed him to her house .
42010039	She had a sister called Mary who seated herself at the feet of the Master and was listening to his words .
42010040	But Martha was busy and worried over a great deal of service . Coming to him she said , " Master , do you not care that my sister has left me to do the work alone ? Tell her to take hold with me . "
42010041	But the Master answered her , " Martha , Martha , you are anxious and worried about many things ,
42010042	but there is need only of a few , or one . Mary has chosen the good part and it shall not be taken from her . "
42011001	ONCE he was in a certain place praying . When he ceased , one of his disciples said to him , " Master , teach us to pray , as John taught his disciples . "
42011002	He said to them , " When you pray say : Father , thy name be kept holy ; Thy kingdom come ;
42011003	Our bread for the coming day Give us day by day ;
42011004	And forgive us our sins ; For we ourselves forgive every one who fails toward us . And bring us not into trial . "
42011005	He said to them , " Suppose one of you has a friend and goes to him at midnight and says to him , ' Friend , lend me three loaves ,
42011006	for a friend of mine has come to my house after a journey and I have nothing to set before him ' ;
42011007	and he from within answers , ' Do not trouble me ; the door is locked , and my children and I are in bed ; I cannot get up and give you anything . '
42011008	I tell you , even if he will not rise and give them to him because he is his friend , yet because of his persistence he will rise and give him all that he needs .
42011009	So I tell you , ask and it will be given to you ; seek and you will find ; knock and the door will be opened to you .
42011010	For every one who asks obtains , and he who seeks finds , and to him who knocks the door will be opened .
42011011	What father is there among you who if his son asks for bread will give him a stone ? Or if he asks for a fish , will he give him a serpent instead ?
42011012	Or if he asks for an egg , will he give him a scorpion ?
42011013	If then you , evil though you are , know how to give good gifts to your children , how much more will your Heavenly Father give a holy spirit to those who ask him . "
42011014	He was casting out a demon and it was dumb . After the demon had gone out , the dumb man spoke and the crowds wondered .
42011015	But some of them said , " By Beelzebul , the chief of the demons , he casts out the demons . "
42011016	Others , by way of test , demanded of him a sign from heaven .
42011017	But he , knowing their reasonings , said to them , " Every kingdom divided against itself comes to desolation , and a house divided against itself falls .
42011018	If Satan is divided against himself , how will his kingdom stand ? You say that I am casting out demons by Beelzebul ;
42011019	but if I am casting out demons by Beelzebul , by whom do your sons cast them out ? Therefore let them be your judges .
42011020	But if I am casting out demons by the finger of God , then the kingdom of God has already reached you .
42011021	" When a strong man fully armed guards his castle , his possessions are in peace .
42011022	But when a stronger than he comes upon him and conquers him , he takes all the armor in which he trusted and divides the spoils .
42011023	He who is not with me is against me , and he who does not gather with me is scattering .
42011024	" When the impure spirit comes out from a man , he goes through waterless places , seeking rest . Not finding it , he says , ' I will return to my house from which I came out . '
42011025	When he comes , he finds it empty , swept , and put in order .
42011026	Then he goes and takes along seven spirits worse than himself , and they enter and settle down there , and the last state of that man becomes worse than the first . "
42011027	While he was saying this a woman in the crowd raised her voice and said , " Blessed was the womb that carried you and the breasts that you sucked ! "
42011028	He said , " Blessed are they who hear the word of God and keep it ! "
42011029	As the crowds were thronging about him , he began and said , " This generation is an evil generation . It seeks for a sign , but no sign will be given to it except the sign of Jonah .
42011030	For just as Jonah became a sign to the Ninevites so the Son of Man will be to this generation .
42011031	The queen of the South will rise in the judgment with the men of this generation and will condemn them . For she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon , and more than a Solomon is here .
42011032	The men of Nineveh will stand up in the judgment with this generation and will condemn it . For they repented at the proclamation of Jonah , and indeed more than a Jonah is here .
42011033	" No one lights a lamp and places it in a cellar or under the peck-measure , but on the stand , so that those who come in may see the light .
42011034	The lamp of the body is the eye . When your eye is clear the whole body is lighted . But when it is bad , your body is dark .
42011035	Make sure that the light that is in you is not darkness .
42011036	If your body is all lighted up , not having any part dark , it will be all lighted as when the lamp lights you by its brilliance . "
42011037	During his talk a Pharisee kept asking him to dine with him . He went in and reclined at table .
42011038	The Pharisee , seeing this , wondered that he had not first washed before dinner .
42011039	The Master said to him , " Now you Pharisees cleanse the outside of the cup and the platter , but the inside of you is full of rapacity and wickedness .
42011040	You foolish men , did not he who made the outside make the inside too ?
42011041	But give the things inside as gifts of mercy and at once all will be clean for you .
42011042	But alas for you , Pharisees ! Because you tithe mint , and rue , and every herb , and pass by justice and the love of God . These things you ought to have practiced , without omitting the others .
42011043	Alas for you , Pharisees ! for you love the first seats in the synagogues and greetings in the market-places .
42011044	Alas for you ! for you are like unmarked graves . The men who walk over them do not know it . "
42011045	One of the lawyers answered him , " Teacher , in saying this you treat us roughly too . "
42011046	He said , " Alas for you lawyers also ! for you burden men with burdens hard to bear , and you yourselves do not touch the burdens with one of your fingers .
42011047	Alas for you ! for you build the tombs of the prophets , but your fathers killed them .
42011048	So you are witnesses and consent to the deeds of your fathers , for they killed them and you build their tombs .
42011049	Therefore also the Wisdom of God said , ' I will send to them prophets and apostles , and some of them they will kill and some they will persecute . '
42011050	So the blood of all the prophets which has been shed from the foundation of the world will be required of this generation â
42011051	from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zachariah who perished between the altar and the House . Yes , I tell you , it will be required of this generation .
42011052	Alas for you lawyers ! because you have taken away the key of knowledge . You yourselves have not entered and you have prevented those who were entering . "
42011053	After he went away from there , the scribes and the Pharisees began to press upon him angrily and cross-question him on many points ,
42011054	laying traps to catch something from his mouth .
42012001	MEANWHILE , as the myriads of the crowd were thronging together so that they trod down one another , he began and said to his disciples first , " Beware of the yeast of the Pharisees , that is , their hypocrisy .
42012002	For nothing is covered up which will not be revealed , nor secret which will not be known .
42012003	Whatever you have said in darkness will , on the contrary , be heard in the light , and what you have spoken into the ear in inner moms will be proclaimed on the housetops .
42012004	I tell you , my friends , never fear those who kill the body and after that have nothing more that they can do .
42012005	But I will show you whom you should fear . Fear him who , after he has killed , has power to cast into Gehenna . Yes , I say , fear him .
42012006	Are not five sparrows sold for two pennies ? Yet not one of them is forgotten before God .
42012007	But even the hairs of your head are all numbered . Never fear ; you are worth more than many sparrows .
42012008	But I tell you every one who confesses me before men , him will the Son of Man confess before the angels of God .
42012009	And he who disowns me before men will be disowned before the angels of God .
42012010	Every one who speaks a word against the Son of Man , it will be forgiven him ; but he who says profane words against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven .
42012011	When they bring you in before synagogues and magistrates and authorities , do not be anxious about how to defend yourselves or what to say .
42012012	For the Holy Spirit will teach you in that hour what you must say . "
42012013	One out of the crowd said to him , " Teacher , bid my brother to divide the inheritance with me . "
42012014	But he said , " Man , who appointed me judge or divider over you ? "
42012015	He said to them , " See to it and be on your guard against every form of covetousness , for not even when one has a superabundance is his life from the things he owns . "
42012016	He gave them an illustration , saying , " The ground of a certain rich man yielded abundantly .
42012017	He debated within himself , saying , ' What shall I do ? for I have no place to store my crops . '
42012018	Then he said , ' I will do this : I will pull down my barns and will build larger ones , and there I will store all my wheat and my goods ;
42012019	and I will say to my soul , Soul , you have many goods laid up for many years , take your ease , eat , drink , be merry ! '
42012020	But God said to him , ' Foolish man , this night your soul will be required of you ; and the things that you have prepared â whose will they be ? '
42012021	So is he who lays up treasure for himself and is not rich toward God . "
42012022	He said to his disciples , " Therefore I tell you , never worry about your life , what you are to eat , nor about your body , what you are to put on .
42012023	For the life is more than the food and the body is more than the clothing .
42012024	Consider the ravens , for they neither sow nor reap ; they have neither granary nor barn ; yet God feeds them . How much more you are worth than the birds !
42012025	Which of you can by worrying add a foot to his height ?
42012026	If you cannot do the least , why do you worry about the rest ?
42012027	Consider the lilies , how they neither spin nor weave . Yet I tell you even Solomon in all his splendor was not arrayed like one of these .
42012028	But if God so clothes the herbage which to-day is in the field and to-morrow is thrown into the oven , how much more will he clothe you , O men of little faith !
42012029	Do not seek after something to eat and something to drink , and do not be agitated by cares .
42012030	For these things all the nations of the world are seeking after .
42012031	But strive for his kingdom and these things will be provided for you .
42012032	Never fear , little flock ! For it is your Father's good pleasure to give you the kingdom .
42012033	Sell what you have and give gifts of mercy . Make for yourselves purses that never grow old , an unfailing treasure in heaven where no thief approaches nor moth consumes ;
42012034	for where your treasure is there your heart will be .
42012035	Let your loins be girded and your lamps burning ;
42012036	and be like men expecting their Master when he returns from the wedding , so that when he comes and knocks they may open to him immediately .
42012037	Blessed are those servants whom the Master , when he comes , will find watching ! Truly I tell you he will gird himself and make them recline at the table and will come and wait on them .
42012038	If he comes in the second watch or in the third watch and finds them so , blessed are they !
42012039	But know this , if the householder had known in what hour the thief was coming , he would not have let his house be broken into .
42012040	And you be ready , for in an hour that you do not think the Son of Man is coming . "
42012041	Peter said , " Master , do you intend this illustration for us or for all ? "
42012042	The Master said , " Who then is the faithful , the wise , manager whom the master will appoint over his establishment to give out rations at the proper time ?
42012043	Blessed is that servant whom his master , when he comes , will find so doing !
42012044	I tell you truly he will appoint him over all his possessions .
42012045	But if that servant says in his heart , ' My master will be long in coming , ' and begins to strike the men servants and the maids and to eat and drink and get drunk ,
42012046	the master of that servant will come on a day when he is not expecting and at an hour that he does not know , and will cut him in two and appoint his portion with the unfaithful .
42012047	That servant who knew his master's will and is not ready , and has not done according to his will , will be beaten with many lashes .
42012048	But he who did not know and yet has done things worthy of lashes will be beaten with few . From every one to whom much was given , much will be required , and from him to whom they have committed much , men will ask the more .
42012049	" I came to cast fire on the earth , and what will I , if it is already kindled ?
42012050	I have a baptism to be baptized with , and how am I distressed until it is accomplished !
42012051	Do you think that I came to give peace on the earth ? No , I tell you , but dissension .
42012052	There will be from now on five in one house split into parties , three against two and two against three ,
42012053	father against son , and son against father , mother against daughter , and daughter against her mother , mother-in-law against her daughter-in-law , and daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law . "
42012054	He said also to the crowds , " When you see a cloud rising in the west , at once you say , ' A shower is coming , ' and so it happens .
42012055	And when you see the south wind blowing , you say , ' There will be burning heat , ' and so it happens .
42012056	Hypocrites , you know how to interpret the face of the earth and the sky , why do you not interpret this crisis ?
42012057	Why do you not of yourselves judge correctly ?
42012058	As you are going with your opponent to the magistrate , take pains on the road to get free from him , so that he may not drag you before the judge and the judge deliver you to the officer and the officer cast you into prison .
42012059	I tell you you will not come out until you pay in full to the last penny . "
42013001	AT that time some were present telling him about the Galilaeans whose blood Pilate had mingled with their sacrifices .
42013002	He answered them , " Do you think that these Galilaeans were sinners above all the Galilaeans because they suffered this ?
42013003	No , I tell you , but unless you have a change of heart , you will all perish in the same way .
42013004	Or those eighteen upon whom the tower in Siloam fell and killed them , do you think that they were deserving of punishment beyond all the people that dwell at Jerusalem ?
42013005	No , I tell you , but unless you have a change of heart , you will all perish just the same . "
42013006	He gave this illustration : " A man had a fig tree planted in his vineyard and came looking for fruit on it and found none .
42013007	He said to the gardener , ' See , three years I have been coming , looking for fruit on this fig tree , and I do not find any . Gut it down . Why should we waste land for it ? '
42013008	But he answered him , ' Leave it this year too , Sir , until I dig around it and throw on manure .
42013009	Then , if it yields fruit in the future , all right . But if not , then you shall cut it down . '
42013010	He was teaching in one of the synagogues on the Sabbath .
42013011	And a woman was there who had had a spirit of weakness eighteen years , and was bent together and could not stand up straight .
42013012	When Jesus saw her he called to her and said , " Woman , you have been freed from your weakness , "
42013013	and he laid his hands on her . Immediately she was straightened and gave glory to God .
42013014	But the synagogue Director , angry because Jesus was healing on the Sabbath , said to the crowd , " There are six days in which work should be done . On those days come and be healed , but not on the Sabbath day . "
42013015	The Master answered him , " Hypocrite , does not each of you on the Sabbath loose his ox or his ass from the manger and lead him away and water him ?
42013016	And ought not this woman , a daughter of Abraham , whom Satan had bound for eighteen years , to have been freed from this bond on the Sabbath day ? "
42013017	As he said this , all his opposers were ashamed , and all the crowd rejoiced at all the glorious things that he did .
42013018	He said , " To what is the kingdom of God like ? To what shall I compare it ?
42013019	It is like a mustard seed which a man took and cast into his garden . It grew and became a tree and the birds of heaven lodged in its branches . "
42013020	Again he said , " To what shall I compare the kingdom of God ?
42013021	It is like yeast which a woman took and hid in three pecks of flour until the whole was leavened . "
42013022	He was journeying through the cities and villages teaching and making his way toward Jerusalem .
42013023	A man said to him , " Master , are there few that are saved ? " He said to them ,
42013024	" Try hard to enter through the narrow door ; for many , I tell you , will try to enter and will not be able .
42013025	After the house-holder has arisen and has shut the door , then you will begin to stand outside and knock at the door , and say , ' Master , open to us . ' And he will answer you , ' I do not know you or where you come from . '
42013026	Then you will begin and say , ' We have eaten and drunk before you and you have taught in our streets . '
42013027	And he will say to you , ' I do not know where you come from . Go away from me , all you workers of wickedness . '
42013028	There will be wailing and gnashing of teeth , when you see Abraham and Isaac and Jacob and all the prophets in the kingdom of God and yourselves thrust outside .
42013029	People will come from the east and the west and from the north and the south and recline at the table in the kingdom of God .
42013030	Indeed , there are last who will be first and there are first who will be last . "
42013031	At that time there came to him some Pharisees , saying , " Go out and leave this place , for Herod purposes to kill you . "
42013032	He said to them , " Go tell that fox , ' See , I am casting out demons and performing cures to-day and to-morrow , and on the third day I will finish . '
42013033	But I must journey to-day , and to-morrow and the next day , for it cannot be that a prophet should perish outside of Jerusalem .
42013034	Jerusalem , Jerusalem , you who kill the prophets and stone those who are sent to you , how often would I have gathered your children as a bird gathers her brood under her wings , and you would not have it !
42013035	See , your house is left to you ! I tell you , you will not see me until the day when you say , ' Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord ! ' "
42014001	ONCE , when he went into the house of one of the leaders of the Pharisees on the Sabbath to eat bread , they were watching him closely .
42014002	And there before him was a man who had dropsy .
42014003	Jesus said to the lawyers and Pharisees , " Is it allowable to heal on the Sabbath or is it not ? "
42014004	They kept quiet . Then taking hold of him he cured him and dismissed him .
42014005	He said to them , " If the son or the ox of any one of you falls into a well on the Sabbath day , will he not at once draw him out ? "
42014006	They could not say anything in answer to this .
42014007	Observing how the guests were choosing the best couches , he gave them an illustration :
42014008	" When you are invited by any one to a wedding , do not recline on the best couch , for some one more honored than you may have been invited ,
42014009	and when he who invited you and him comes he may say to you , ' Give place to this man , ' and then you will with shame begin and take the humblest place .
42014010	But when you are invited , go and recline in the humblest place , so that when he who has invited you comes he may say , ' Friend , come up higher . ' Then you will have honor before all your fellow guests .
42014011	For every one who exalts himself will be humbled and he who humbles himself will be exalted . "
42014012	He said , too , to the man who had invited him , " When you make a breakfast or a dinner , do not call your friends or your brothers or your relatives , or your rich neighbors , for they may invite you in return and you may be repaid .
42014013	But when you hold a reception , invite poor men , maimed men , lame men , blind men .
42014014	And you will be blessed , because they cannot repay you , and you will be repaid at the resurrection of the just . "
42014015	On hearing this , one of his fellow guests said to him , " Blessed will he be who eats bread in the kingdom of God ! "
42014016	Jesus said to him , " A certain man made a great dinner and invited many ,
42014017	and sent his servant at the hour of the dinner to tell the guests , ' Come , for things are now ready . '
42014018	But they all began with one mind to make excuse . The first said to him , ' I have bought a field and must go and see it . I beg of you to have me excused . '
42014019	Another said , ' I have bought five yoke of oxen and I am going to try them . I beg of you , have me excused . '
42014020	Another said , ' I have married a wife and on that account I cannot come . '
42014021	The servant came back and told his master these things . Then the householder , becoming angry , said to his servant , ' Go out quickly into the streets and lanes of the city and lead in here the poor and maimed and blind and lame . '
42014022	The servant said , ' Master , what you ordered has been done and still there is room . '
42014023	The master said to the servant , ' Go out into the roads and hedges and make them come in , so that my house may be filled .
42014024	I tell you not one of those men that were invited shall taste of my dinner . ' "
42014025	Great crowds were traveling along with him , and he turned and said to them ,
42014026	" If any one comes to me and does not hate his father and his mother and his wife and his children and his brothers and his sisters , yes , and his own life also , he cannot be a disciple of mine .
42014027	Whoever does not take up his own cross and come after me cannot be a disciple of mine .
42014028	For which of you wishing to build a tower does not first sit down and compute the cost , whether he has enough to complete it ,
42014029	for fear that , after he has laid the foundation and cannot finish it , all the onlookers may begin to ridicule him ,
42014030	saying , ' This man began to build and could not finish . '
42014031	Or what king going to meet another king in war does not first sit down and deliberate whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who is coming against him with twenty thousand ?
42014032	If not , while the other is still far off he sends an embassy and asks for conditions of peace .
42014033	Just so no one of you who does not renounce all that he has can be a disciple of mine .
42014034	Salt is good , but if the salt becomes tasteless , with what shall it be seasoned ?
42014035	It is fit neither for the land nor for the manure heap . They throw it away . Let him who has ears to hear , hear . "
42015001	ALL the tax collectors and sinners were drawing near to him in order to hear him .
42015002	The Pharisees and the scribes grumbled to one another , " This man welcomes sinners and eats with them . "
42015003	He gave them this illustration :
42015004	" What man of you , if he has a hundred sheep and has lost one of them , does not leave the ninety-nine in the wilderness and go after the lost one until he has found it ?
42015005	And when he has found it he lays it on his shoulders with joy ,
42015006	and when he comes home he calls together his friends and neighbors and says , ' Rejoice with me , for I have found my sheep that was lost ! '
42015007	I tell you there will be more joy in heaven over one sinner whose heart is changed than over ninety-nine righteous men who have no need to change .
42015008	" Or what woman who has ten shillings , if she loses one shilling , does not light a lamp and sweep the house and look for it carefully until she finds it ?
42015009	And when she finds it , she calls together her friends and neighbors and says , ' Rejoice with me , for I have found the shilling that I lost . '
42015010	So I tell you there springs joy in the presence of the angels of God over one sinner whose heart is changed . "
42015011	He said further , " A certain man had two sons .
42015012	And the younger of them said to his father , ' Father , give me the portion of the property that is coming to me . ' So he divided his wealth between them .
42015013	Not many days later , the younger son got everything together and went away to a far country and there squandered his property in a dissolute life .
42015014	When he had spent everything , there came a terrible famine in that land and he began to be in want .
42015015	So he went and attached himself to one of the citizens of that country who sent him into his fields to feed swine .
42015016	And he would fain have filled his stomach with the pods the swine were eating , but no one gave him anything .
42015017	Then , coming to himself , he said , ' How many hired men of my father have bread more than enough , and here I am perishing with famine .
42015018	I will arise and go to my father and will say to him , Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you .
42015019	I am no longer worthy to be called your son . Make me as one of your hired men . '
42015020	And he arose and came to his father . But while he was still far off , his father saw him and pitied him , and ran and fell on his neck and kissed him tenderly .
42015021	The son said to him , ' Father , I have sinned against heaven and before you . I am no longer worthy to be called your son ' â
42015022	But the father said to his servants , ' Bring out quickly the best robe and put it on him , and put a ring on his hand , and shoes on his feet ;
42015023	and bring the fattened calf and kill it , and let us eat and make merry .
42015024	For this , my son , was dead and has come to life ; he was lost and has been found . ' And they began to be merry .
42015025	Now his older son was in the field , and when on returning he drew near the house he heard music and dancing .
42015026	Calling to him one of the servants , he inquired what this was . The servant said to him ,
42015027	' Your brother has come and your father has killed the fattened calf because he has received him back in health . '
42015028	But he grew angry , and would not go in . Then his father came out and begged him .
42015029	But he answered his father , ' See , all these years I have been serving you , and I never broke a command of yours , yet you have never given me a kid to make merry with my friends .
42015030	But when this son of yours , who has wasted your property with bad women , came , you have killed for him the fattened calf . '
42015031	But the father said to him , ' Child , you are always with me and all that I have is yours .
42015032	We could not but make merry and rejoice , for your brother here was dead and has come to life ; he was lost and is found . '
42016001	HE said to his disciples , " A certain rich man had a manager who was accused to him of wasting his property .
42016002	Calling him to him , he said , ' What is this that I hear about you ? Give an account of your management ; for you cannot longer be manager . '
42016003	The manager said to himself , ' What shall I do ? for my master is going to take the management away from me . I have not strength to dig ; I am ashamed to beg .
42016004	I know what I will do , so that when I am dismissed from the management they may welcome me into their houses . '
42016005	So , calling to him all of the debtors of his master , he said to the first , ' How much do you owe to my master ? '
42016006	He replied , ' A hundred measures of oil . ' He said , ' Take your account and sit down quickly and write fifty . '
42016007	Then to another he said , ' And you , how much do you owe ? ' He replied , ' A hundred measures of wheat . ' He said to him , ' Take your account and write eighty . '
42016008	The master praised the wicked manager because he had done prudently . For the sons of this world are with reference to their own generation wiser than the sons of light .
42016009	I tell you , make for yourselves friends with the Mammon of unrighteousness , so that when it fails they may welcome you into the eternal tents .
42016010	He who is faithful in the least is faithful also in much , and he who is dishonest in the least is also dishonest in much .
42016011	If , then , you have not been faithful in the dishonest Mammon , who will entrust to you the true ?
42016012	And if you were not faithful in what was another's , who will give you what is your own ?
42016013	No house servant can serve two masters . For either he will hate one and love the other or he will hold to one and despise the other . You cannot serve God and Mammon . "
42016014	The Pharisees , who were lovers of money , were listening to all this and they were sneering at him .
42016015	He said to them , " You are those who justify yourselves before men , but God knows your hearts . For what is highly esteemed among men is an abomination before God .
42016016	" The Law and the Prophets were until John . From that time the good news of the kingdom of God is proclaimed and every one is forcing his way into it .
42016017	" It is easier for heaven and earth to pass away than for one stroke of a letter of the Law to fail .
42016018	" Every one who divorces his wife and marries another commits adultery , and he who marries a divorced woman commits adultery .
42016019	" A certain man was rich and was clothed in purple and fine linen and lived merrily every day in splendor .
42016020	And a certain poor man by the name of Lazarus had been laid at his gate , full of sores
42016021	and longing to be fed from what fell from the rich man's table . Even the dogs came and licked his sores .
42016022	It happened that the poor man died and was carried by the angels to Abraham's bosom . The rich man also died and was buried .
42016023	And in Hades he lifted up his eyes , being in torments , and saw Abraham far off and Lazarus in his bosom .
42016024	He called and said , ' Father Abraham , have compassion on me and send Lazarus to dip the tip of his finger in water and cool my tongue ; for I am in anguish in this flame . '
42016025	But Abraham said , ' Child , remember that you had your good things in full in your lifetime , and Lazarus likewise had his evil things . Now he is here receiving comfort and you are in anguish .
42016026	Moreover , between us and you a great chasm has been fixed , so that those who wish to cross from here to you cannot , nor can any cross from there to us . '
42016027	But he said , ' I beg you , then , Father , to send him to my father's house ,
42016028	for I have five brothers , in order to testify to them , so that they may not come also to this place of torment . '
42016029	Abraham said , ' They have Moses and the prophets . Let them listen to them . '
42016030	But he said , ' No , father Abraham , but if one goes to them from the dead , they will have a change of heart . '
42016031	Abraham replied , ' If they do not listen to Moses and the prophets , neither will they be persuaded , though one rises from the dead . '
42017001	HE said to his disciples , " It cannot be but that occasions of stumbling will arise , but alas for him through whom they come !
42017002	It would be better for him if , with a millstone hung around his neck , he had been flung into the sea than to cause one of these little ones to stumble .
42017003	" Be on your guard . If your brother sins against you , reprove him , and if he changes his mind , forgive him .
42017004	Even if seven times in the day he sins against you and seven times turns to you , saying , ' I repent , ' forgive him . "
42017005	The apostles said to the Master , " Increase our faith . "
42017006	The Master said , " If you had faith like a mustard seed , you would say to this mulberry tree , ' Be uprooted and planted in the sea , ' and it would obey you .
42017007	" Who is there of you , having a servant plowing or keeping sheep , that will say to him when he comes in from the field , ' Come quickly and recline at table ' ?
42017008	On the contrary , will he not say to him , ' Make ready something for my dinner and gird yourself and wait on me while I eat and drink , and after that you may eat and drink yourself ' ?
42017009	Does he thank the servant because he did what he was told ?
42017010	Just so you , when you have done all that has been commanded you , say , ' We are useless servants ; we have done merely what we ought to have done . ' "
42017011	It happened that on his journey toward Jerusalem he was going through Samaria and Galilee .
42017012	As he was approaching a certain village , ten leprous men met him . They stood at a distance ,
42017013	and , raising their voices , called , " Jesus , Master , have compassion on us . "
42017014	When Jesus saw them , he said , " Go and show yourselves to the priests . " While they were going , they became clean .
42017015	One of them , seeing that he had been cured , turned back with a loud shout giving glory to God ,
42017016	and he fell on his face at the feet of Jesus , thanking him . He was a Samaritan .
42017017	Jesus said , " Were not ten cleansed ? But the nine â where are they ?
42017018	Was there none found returning to give glory to God except this foreigner ? "
42017019	He said to him , " Rise and go . Your faith has healed you . "
42017020	On being asked by the Pharisees when the kingdom of God was coming , Jesus answered them , " The kingdom of God will not come in a way that can be observed ,
42017021	nor will they say , ' Here it is ! ' or , ' There it is ! ' For indeed the kingdom of God is among you . "
42017022	He said to the disciples , " There will come days when you will wish to see one of the days of the Son of Man and you will not see it .
42017023	They will say to you , ' See here ! ' or , ' See there ! ' but do not start off or go in pursuit .
42017024	For as the lightning when it flashes shines from one part of the heavens to the other , so will the Son of Man be in his day .
42017025	But first he must suffer many things , and be rejected by this generation .
42017026	As it happened in the days of Noah , so will it be in the days of the Son of Man .
42017027	They were eating and drinking , marrying and being given in marriage , until the day that Noah went into the ark and the flood came and destroyed them all .
42017028	Just so it was in the days of Lot ; they were eating and drinking , buying and selling , planting and building .
42017029	But on the day that Lot went out of Sodom it rained fire and brimstone from heaven and destroyed them all .
42017030	So will the Son of Man be on the day that he is revealed .
42017031	On that day , if a man is on the housetop and his things in the house , he must not come down to get them , and for the same reason if he is in the field he must not turn back .
42017032	Remember Lot's wife .
42017033	Whoever seeks to save his life will lose it , and whoever loses it will save it .
42017034	I tell you that night there will be two men in one bed ; one will be taken with him and the other will be left .
42017035	There will be two women grinding at the same mill , one will be taken with him and the other will be left . "
42017037	They said to him , " Where , Master ? " He said to them , " Where the carcass is , there will the vultures come flocking together . "
42018001	HE gave them an illustration that they ought always to pray and not to lose courage .
42018002	He said , " There was in a certain city a judge who did not fear God or regard man .
42018003	And there was a widow in that city who kept coming to him and saying , ' Give me justice against my adversary . '
42018004	For a time he would not . Later he said to himself , ' Even though I do not fear God nor regard man ,
42018005	yet because this widow is annoying me I will do her justice so that she may not keep coming and mauling me forever . '
42018006	The Master said , " Hear what the wicked judge says ;
42018007	and will not God do justice for his elect , who are calling to him day and night , even though he is long-suffering with their adversaries ?
42018008	I tell you , he will do justice for them speedily . But when the Son of Man comes , will he find faith on the earth ? "
42018009	He gave also this illustration to some who trusted in themselves as being righteous and despised others :
42018010	" Two men went up to the Temple courts to pray . One was a Pharisee and the other was a tax collector .
42018011	The Pharisee stood and prayed thus with himself , ' God , I thank thee that I am not like the rest of men , extortioners , cheats , adulterers , or even like this tax collector .
42018012	I fast twice a week . I give tithes of all I get . '
42018013	But the tax collector stood far off and would not even lift his eyes to heaven , but beat his breast , saying , ' God be merciful to me , the sinner ! '
42018014	I tell you this man went down to his house justified rather than the other . For every one who exalts himself will be humbled , and he who humbles himself will be exalted . "
42018015	They were bringing to him babes for him to touch . The disciples on seeing this rebuked them .
42018016	But Jesus called the children to him , saying , " Let the little children come to me , and do not hinder them ; for of such is the kingdom of God .
42018017	Truly , I tell you , whoever does not receive the kingdom of God as a little child will not enter it . "

42018021	He said , " All these I have kept from my boyhood up . "
42018022	On hearing that , Jesus said to him , " You lack still one thing . Sell all that you have and distribute to the poor and you will have treasure in heaven , and then come and follow me . "
42018023	But he , on hearing this , became deeply sorrowful , for he was very rich .
42018024	Jesus looked at him and said , " With how much difficulty do those who have riches enter the kingdom of God !

42018026	Those who heard it said , " Then who can be saved ? "

42018033	and they will scourge him and kill him , and on the third day he will rise . "
42018034	But they understood none of these things , and what he said was hidden from them . They did not grasp the meaning of his words .
42018035	As he approached Jericho , a blind man was sitting by the roadside begging .
42018036	Hearing a crowd passing , he inquired what this was .
42018037	They told him , " Jesus , the Nazarene , is passing by . "
42018038	Then he shouted , " Jesus , son of David , have pity on me ! "
42018039	Those who were in front rebuked him and told him to be still . But he kept crying out much louder , " Son of David , have pity on me ! "

42019006	He hurriedly descended and welcomed him joyfully .
42019007	All who saw it grumbled , saying that Jesus was going in to stay with a sinner .

42019012	He said , " A certain nobleman went into a far country to get for himself a kingdom and return .
42019013	Calling his ten servants , he gave them each an equal sum of money and said to them , ' Do business until I come . '
42019014	But his citizens hated him and sent an embassy after him to say , ' We do not want this man to be king over us . '
42019015	When he returned , having secured the royal power , he ordered those servants to whom he had given the silver to be called to him that he might know what each had gained in trading .
42019016	The first came saying , ' Sir , your money has gained tenfold . '
42019017	He said , ' Well done , good servant , because you were faithful in the least you shall be ruler over ten cities . '
42019018	Then came the second , saying , ' Your money , Sir , has made fivefold . '
42019019	He said to this one , ' And you shall be over five cities . '
42019020	Another one came , saying , ' Sir , here is your silver , which I kept laid away in a napkin .

42019022	He said to him , ' Out of your own mouth I will judge you , you wicked servant . Did you know that I was an austere man , taking up what I did not lay down and reaping where I did not sow ?
42019023	Then why did you not put my silver into the bank , so that when I came I could have exacted it with interest ? '

42020001	ON one of those days , as he was teaching the people in the Temple courts and proclaiming the good news , the high priests and the scribes came up with the elders
42020002	and said to him , " Tell us by what authority you are doing these things or who it is that gave you this authority . "
42020003	He answered them , " I too will ask you a question and you must tell me :
42020004	the baptism of John , was it from heaven or from men ? "
42020005	They conferred among themselves , saying , " If we say , ' From heaven , ' he will say , ' Why then did you not believe him ? '
42020006	and if we say , ' From men , ' all the people will stone us ; for they are persuaded that John was a prophet . "
42020007	So they answered that they did not know where it came from .
42020008	Jesus said to them , " Neither will I tell you by what authority I am doing these things . "
42020009	He began and gave the people this illustration : " A man planted a vineyard and let it out to grape-growers and went abroad for a long time .
42020010	At the proper season he sent to the grape-growers a servant for them to give him a part of the fruit of the vineyard . But the grape-growers beat him , and sent him away empty-handed .
42020011	He afterwards sent another servant . That one , too , they beat and insulted and sent away empty-handed .
42020012	Then he sent a third . But this one , too , they wounded and threw out .
42020013	The owner of the vineyard said , ' I will send my son , my beloved . Perhaps they will reverence him . '
42020014	But when the grape-growers saw him , they conferred with one another and said , ' This is the heir . Let us kill him so that the inheritance may be ours . '
42020015	So they threw him outside of the vineyard and killed him . What now will the owner of the vineyard do ?
42020016	He will come and destroy those grape-growers and will give the vineyard to others . " When they heard this , they exclaimed , " May it never be ! "

42022001	THE Feast of Unleavened Bread , which is called the Passover , was approaching .

43021007	That disciple whom Jesus loved said to Peter , " It is the Master ! " Simon Peter , on hearing that it was the Master , girded around him his blouse , for he was naked , and threw himself into the lake .
43021008	The other disciples came in the small boat , for they were not far from land â about a hundred yards â dragging the netful of fish .
43021009	When they had gotten out on land , they saw a fire of coals and fish laid on it and bread .
43021010	Jesus said to them , " Bring some of the fish that you have just caught . "
43021011	Simon Peter got into the boat and drew the net to land full of big fishes â a hundred and fifty-three â and though there were so many the net was not torn .
43021012	Jesus said , " Come , take break-fast . " No one of the disciples dared to ask him who he was , knowing that it was the Master .
43021013	Jesus came and took bread and gave to them , and fish in the same manner .
43021014	This is now the third time that Jesus showed himself to the disciples after rising from the dead .
43021015	When they had breakfasted , Jesus said to Simon Peter , " Simon , son of John , do you love me more than these ? " He said to him , " Yes , Master , you know that I love you . " He said to him , " Feed my lambs . "
43021016	He said to him a second time , " Simon , son of John , do you love me ? " He said to him , " Yes , Master , you know that I love you . " He said to him , " Shepherd my sheep . "
43021017	He said to him the third time , " Simon , son of John , do you love me ? " Peter was grieved because he said to him the third time , " Do you love me ? " and he said to him , " Master , you know all things . You know that I love you . " Jesus said to him , " Feed my sheep .
43021018	Truly , truly , I tell you , when you were young , you girded yourself and walked about wherever you wished . When you are old , you will stretch out your hands and another will gird you and carry you where you do not wish . "
43021019	This he said , indicating the kind of death by which he would glorify God . After saying this he said to him , " Follow me . "
43021020	Peter turned and saw the disciple whom Jesus loved , following .
43021021	Peter , seeing him , said to Jesus , " Master , what shall this man do ? "
43021022	Jesus said to him , " If I choose to have him stay until I come , what is that to you ? You must follow me . "
43021023	So the report went out among the brethren that that disciple was not to die . But Jesus did not say to Peter that he would not die , but , " If I choose to have him stay until I come , what is that to you ? "
43021024	This is the disciple who witnesses to these things and who wrote these things , and we know that his testimony is true .
43021025	There are also many other things that Jesus did , but if these are written , every one , I do not think that the world itself will have room for the books when written .
44001001	IN my first book , Theophilus , I told of all that Jesus did and taught from the beginning

44003001	PETER and John were going up into the Temple courts at the hour of prayer , three o'clock ,

44007001	THE High Priest said , " Are these things true ? "

44007026	On the next day Moses appeared when two of them were fighting , and tried to make peace between them , saying , ' Men , you are brethren . Why are you injuring each other ? '

44007030	" When forty years had passed , an angel appeared to him in the desert of Mount Sinai in the flames of a burning bush .
44007031	When Moses saw the sight he was astonished , but as he was approaching to look closely , the voice of the Lord was heard ,
44007032	' I am the God of your fathers , the God of Abraham and of Isaac and of Jacob . ' Then Moses trembled and did not dare to look closely .
44007033	The Lord said to him , ' Loose your sandals from your feet , for the place on which you are standing is holy ground .

44007046	He found favor with God and prayed that he might provide a temple for the house of Israel .

44007048	Yet the Most High does not dwell in buildings made by hands ; as the prophet says ,
44007049	' Heaven is my throne and the earth is my footstool . What sort of house will you build for me , says the Lord , or what is my place of rest ?

44008001	SAUL also approved of their putting him to death . On that day arose a great persecution of the church in Jerusalem . All except the apostles were scattered through Judaea and Samaria .
44008002	Pious men carried Stephen away for burial and made great lamentation over him .

44008008	There was great rejoicing in that city .
44008009	A certain man named Simon had previously been practicing magic in the city and astonishing the people of Samaria , giving out that he was some great one .
44008010	They had all given attention to him , from the least to the greatest , saying , " This man is the power of God which is called great . "

44010002	He was a pious man , reverencing God with all his household , doing many acts of charity to the people and praying to God constantly .

44010006	He is the guest of a certain Simon , a tanner , whose house is by the seaside . "

44012001	ABOUT that time King Herod laid hands on some members of the church in order to maltreat them .

44012021	On an appointed day Herod in his royal robes sat on a platform and made an address to them .

44013017	The God of this people Israel chose our fathers and made the people great during their sojourn in the land of Egypt , and with an uplifted arm brought them out .

44013023	" Of this man's descendants God , according to his promise , brought to Israel a savior â Jesus ,
44013024	before whose coming John had proclaimed to all the people of Israel baptism for a change of heart .
44013025	As John was finishing his career he used to say , ' What do you think that I am ? I am not he . But one is coming after me the sandals of whose feet I am not worthy to unfasten . '
44013026	" Brethren , sons of Abraham's race and those among you who reverence God , the message of this salvation has been sent to you .
44013027	For the inhabitants of Jerusalem and their rulers , neither understanding him nor the utterances of the prophets which are read every Sabbath , fulfilled those utterances by condemning him .
44013028	Although they found no ground for putting him to death they begged Pilate to have him killed .
44013029	When they had completely done all that had been predicted about him , they took him down from the cross and laid him in a tomb .
44013030	But God raised him from the dead
44013031	and he appeared for many days to those who had gone up with him from Galilee to Jerusalem . They are now his witnesses to all the people .
44013032	" We tell you the good news that the promise to our fathers has been kept ;
44013033	for God has fulfilled it for our children in raising up Jesus , as it is written in the second psalm , ' Thou art my son ; to-day I have become thy father . '
44013034	And as to his raising him from the dead , never to return to decay , he spoke thus ; ' I will give you the holy and sure promises made to David . '
44013035	Therefore he says also in another psalm , ' Thou wilt not let thy holy one see decay . '
44013036	For David after serving the will of God in his own generation fell asleep and was laid with his fathers and saw decay .
44013037	But he whom God raised up saw no decay .
44013038	" Therefore let it be known to you , brethren , that through him forgiveness of sins is proclaimed to you .
44013039	Yes , every one who believes in him is cleared from all the sins from which you could not be cleared by the Law of Moses .
44013040	Take care then that what was said in the Prophets does not come on you ,
44013041	' See , you disdainful ones , and wonder and perish ; for I am working a work in your days â a work which you will not believe even if some one fully explains it to you . ' "
44013042	As Paul and Barnabas were going out , the people begged that these words might be spoken to them on the next Sabbath .
44013043	After the synagogue was dismissed , many of the Jews and of the pious converts to Judaism followed Paul and Barnabas , who talked to them and endeavored to persuade them to hold fast to the grace of God .
44013044	On the next Sabbath almost the whole city came together to hear the message of God .
44013045	But the Jews , seeing the crowds , were filled with anger and kept speaking in abusive language against what was said by Paul .
44013046	Then Paul and Barnabas said with fearless plainness , " The message of God had to be spoken first to you . But since you thrust it away and do not judge yourselves worthy of life eternal â now , we turn to the Gentiles .
44013047	For so the Lord has commanded us , ' I have set you for a light of the Gentiles , that you may be for salvation to the ends of the earth . '
44013048	When the Gentiles heard this , they rejoiced and glorified the message of the Lord , and all who were predestined to life eternal believed .
44013049	The message of the Lord was carried abroad through the whole country .
44013050	But the Jews stirred up the pious women of high standing and the leading men of the city , and started a persecution against Paul and Barnabas and expelled them from their boundaries .
44013051	They shook off the dust of their feet as a protest against them , and came to Iconium .
44013052	The disciples were filled with joy and with the Holy Spirit .
44014001	IN Iconium Paul and Barnabas went in the same way into the synagogue and spoke so that a large number both of Jews and of Greeks believed .
44014002	But the unbelieving Jews excited and embittered the minds of the Gentiles against the brethren .
44014003	Therefore the apostles spent considerable time speaking freely and fearlessly in reliance upon the Lord , who bore witness to his gracious message by permitting signs and wonders to be done by their hands .
44014004	The people of the city became divided ; some were with the Jews and some with the apostles .
44014005	But when there was a rush made by the Gentiles and the Jews , along with their rulers , to hustle them and stone them ,
44014006	the apostles learned of it and fled to the cities of Lycaonia , Lystra and Derbe , and the surrounding country ,
44014007	and there they went on telling the good news .
44014008	In Lystra there was a man sitting who was powerless in his feet . He had been lame from his mother's womb and never had walked .
44014009	He was listening to Paul as he was speaking . Paul fixed his eyes on him , and , seeing that he had faith to be healed ,
44014010	said in a loud voice , " Stand up straight on your feet . " He sprang up and walked about .
44014011	When the crowds saw what Paul had done , they raised their voices , saying in Lycaonian , " The gods have taken human form and come down to us . "
44014012	They called Barnabas Zeus and Paul Hermes , because he was the principal speaker .
44014013	Then the priest of Zeus , whose temple was in front of the city , brought bulls and garlands to the gates , followed by the crowds , and intended to offer sacrifice .
44014014	But when the apostles Barnabas and Paul heard of it , they rent their garments and sprang into the crowd , crying out ,
44014015	" Men , why are you doing this ? We too are men with the same weaknesses that you have . We are bringing you the good news that you are to turn from these foolish things to the living God , who made the heavens and the earth and the sea and all things that are in them .
44014016	In past generations he permitted all the nations to go their own ways ,
44014017	though he did not leave himself without evidence , for he did you good and gave rains from heaven and fruitful seasons , filling your hearts with food and gladness . "
44014018	Even by saying this they with difficulty kept the crowds from offering sacrifice to them .
44014019	But Jews arrived from Antioch and Iconium and won over the crowds , and they stoned Paul and dragged him outside of the city , thinking that he was dead .
44014020	But when the disciples gathered around him he rose up and reentered the city . On the next day he left with Barnabas for Derbe .
44014021	Telling the good news in that city they made a number of disciples . Then they returned to Lystra and Iconium and Antioch ,
44014022	reassuring the minds of the disciples and encouraging them to be steadfast in the faith , saying , " Through many trials we must enter into the kingdom of God . "
44014023	They appointed elders for them in every church , and after prayer and fasting committed them to the Lord in whom they had believed .
44014024	They passed through Pisidia and came into Pamphylia .
44014025	After telling the message in Perga , they came down to Attalia .
44014026	From there they sailed for Antioch , where they had been committed to the grace of God for the work which they had now completed .
44014027	Upon their arrival they assembled the church and narrated all that God , working with them , had done , and how he had opened the door of faith to the Gentiles .
44014028	There they passed no little time with the disciples .
44015001	BUT certain men came down from Judaea and undertook to teach the brethren , " Unless you are circumcised according to the custom of Moses , you cannot be saved . "
44015002	Since no little dissension and controversy arose between Paul and Barnabas and these men , it was arranged that Paul and Barnabas and some others of them should go up to Jerusalem to the apostles and elders about this question .
44015003	So they were sent on by the church and passed through Phoenicia and Samaria , relating the conversion of the Gentiles , which caused great joy to all the brethren .
44015004	On their arrival in Jerusalem they were welcomed by the church and the apostles and the elders , and they narrated all that God , working with them , had done .
44015005	Then some of the party of the Pharisees , who had become believers , rose and said , " We must circumcise them and tell them to keep the Law of Moses . "
44015006	The apostles and elders met to confer about this matter .
44015007	After there had been much debate , Peter rose and said to them , " Brethren , you know that in early days God chose among you that through my mouth the Gentiles should hear the message of good news and should believe .
44015008	And God , who knows all hearts , bore witness to them by giving them the Holy Spirit , just as he did to us .
44015009	He made no difference between us and them in cleansing their hearts by faith .
44015010	Now , therefore , why are you testing God by putting on the neck of the disciples a yoke which neither our fathers nor we have been able to bear ?
44015011	On the contrary we believe that we are saved through the grace of the Lord Jesus just as they are . "
