45005004	and endurance develops a tested character , and a tested character develops hope ,
45005005	and hope does not disappoint , for the love of God has been poured out in our hearts through the Holy Spirit granted to us .
45005006	For while we were still without strength Christ , at the due time , died for the unrighteous .
45005007	Hardly for a righteous man will any one die . For a good man some one perhaps may dare to die .
45005008	But God shows his own love to us in that while we were still sinners Christ died for us .
45005009	Much more then , now that we have been pronounced righteous through his blood , shall we be saved from wrath by him .
45005010	For if while enemies we were reconciled to God through the death of his Son , much more , now that we are reconciled , shall we be saved by his life .
45005011	And not only so , but we exult in God through our Lord Jesus Christ , through whom we have now obtained the reconciliation .
45005012	Therefore as through one man sin entered the world , and through sin death entered , and so death spread to all men , since all sinned â
45005013	for down to the time of the Law sin was in the world , and yet sin is not charged where there is no law ;
45005014	but death reigned from Adam to Moses even over those who had not sinned like Adam , who is the type of him who was coming .
45005015	But the gracious gift is not like the fall . For if by the fall of the one the many sinned , much more did the grace of God and the free gift by the grace of the one man Jesus Christ abound to the many .
45005016	And the free gift was not like the sentence that came through one who sinned ; for the sentence came from one fall for condemnation , but the free gift was that men should be called righteous in spite of many falls .
45005017	For if by the fall of one man death reigned through that one , much more those who receive the abounding grace and the free gift of righteousness will reign in life through one , that is , through Jesus Christ .
45005018	As then through one fall sentence came upon all men and they were condemned ; so through one righteous act the free gift came to all men so that they are pronounced righteous and live .
45005019	For as by the disobedience of the one man the many were set down as sinners , so by the obedience of the one the many will be set down as righteous .
45005020	But law came in alongside that the fall might be greater ; but where sin became greater grace became greater still ,
45005021	in order that as sin reigned in death grace might reign through righteousness and issue in life eternal through Jesus Christ our Lord .
45006001	WHAT shall we say then ? Shall we remain in sin so that grace may be great ?
45006002	Never . How shall we who died to sin still live in it ?
45006003	Are you ignorant that all of us who have been baptized into Christ Jesus were baptized into his death ?
45006004	We were buried with him by baptism into death , in order that as Christ was raised from the dead through the glory of the Father , so we too might walk in newness of life .
45006005	For if we have grown into union with him by the likeness of his death , surely we shall be united with him by the likeness of his resurrection .
45006006	For we know this , that our old-time humanity was crucified with him , in order that the sinful body might be made powerless , that we might no longer be slaves of sin .
45006007	For one who has died has been pronounced righteous and free from sin .
45006008	But if we died with Christ we believe that we shall live with him ,
45006009	knowing that Christ , after being raised from the dead , dies no more ; death no more reigns over him .
45006010	For the death that he died , he died to sin once for all ; but the life that he lives , he lives to God .
45006011	So you must think yourselves dead to sin , but living to God in Christ Jesus .
45006012	Do not let sin reign in your mortal body so that you will obey its lusts ,
45006013	and do not yield your members to sin as the instruments of wickedness ; but present yourselves to God as men once dead , but now living , and yield your members to God as the instruments of righteousness .
45006014	For sin shall not be king over you ; for you are not under law , but under grace .
45006015	What then ? May we sin because we are not under law , but under grace ? Never .
45006016	Do you not know that to whom you present yourselves as servants intending obedience , you are the servants of the one you obey , whether of sin , resulting in death , or of obedience , resulting in righteousness ?
45006017	Thanks be to God that though you were slaves of sin you became obedient from the heart to the type of teaching in which you were instructed .
45006018	You were made free from sin and made servants to righteousness .
45006019	I am speaking humanly on account of the weakness of your human nature . As you did present your members as servants to impurity and to lawlessness to do lawlessness , so now you have presented your members as servants to righteousness for holy living .
45006020	When you were servants of sin you were free from righteousness .
45006021	What fruit did you have then ? Fruit of which you are now ashamed ; for the end of those things is death .
45006022	But now freed from sin and having become servants of God you have your fruit in holy living and its outcome , life eternal .
45006023	For the wages of sin is death , but the gracious gift of God is life eternal in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45007001	ARE you ignorant , brethren , for I am speaking to those who know law , that the Law rules over a person while he is living ?
45007002	For a married woman is by law bound to her husband while he is living . But if the husband dies , she is freed from the law of her husband .
45007003	Therefore while her husband is living she is called an adulteress if she becomes another man's . But if her husband dies she is free from the law , so that she is not an adulteress when she becomes another man's .
45007004	So , my brethren , you were made dead to the Law through the body of Christ , that you might become wedded to another , to him who was raised from the dead , that we might bear fruit to God .
45007005	For when we were in the flesh the sinful passions that arise through the Law were active in our members , so that we bore fruit to death .
45007006	But now the Law has been made inoperative on us , since we have died to that by which we were held , so that we serve in newness of the spirit and not in oldness of the letter .
45007007	What shall we say then ? Is the Law sin ? Never . But I should not have come to know sin except through the Law . I should not have known lust if the Law had not said , " Thou shalt not lust . "
45007008	Sin , taking occasion through the commandment , worked in me every lust . For apart from the Law sin is dead .
45007009	I was living once , apart from law . But when the commandment came , sin began to live and I died ,
45007010	and the commandment which meant life was found to mean death .
45007011	For sin , taking occasion through the commandment , deceived me and by it killed me .
45007012	So the Law is holy and the commandment is holy and just and good .
45007013	Did then what is good become death to me ? Never . But sin , that it might appear sin , worked death in me through the good , in order that it might become beyond measure sinful .
45007014	For we know that the Law is spiritual ; but I am fleshly , sold under sin .
45007015	For what I am doing I do not understand . For not what I choose is what I practice , but what I hate , this I do .
45007016	But if I do what I do not choose , I agree with the law that it is right .
45007017	And now it is no longer I that do it , but the Sin that dwells in me .
45007021	I find then this rule , when I choose to do the right , that evil is present with me .
45007022	I delight in the Law in my inner man ,
45007023	but I see another law in my members , warring with the law of my mind and leading me captive under the law of sin which is in my members .
45007024	Wretched man that I am ! who will deliver me from this body of death ?
45007025	Thanks be to God through Jesus Christ our Lord ! So then I myself with my mind serve the Law of God , but with my flesh the law of sin .
45008001	THERE is therefore now no condemnation to those who are in Christ Jesus .
45008002	For the law of the Spirit of life in Christ Jesus has freed you from the Law of sin and death .
45008003	For , what was impossible for the Law , because it was weak through the flesh â God , sending his own Son in the form of sinful flesh and for sin , condemned the sin that is in the flesh ,
45008004	so that the righteousness required by the Law might be fulfilled in us who live not according to the flesh , but according to the spirit .
45008005	For those who are living according to the flesh have their minds on the things of the flesh , but those who are living according to the spirit have their minds on the things of the spirit .
45008006	Fleshly mindedness is death , but spiritual mindedness is life and peace .
45008007	Therefore fleshly mindedness is hostile to God ; for it is not subject to the Law of God , nor can it be .
45008008	Those who are in the flesh cannot please God .
45008009	But you are not in the flesh , but in the spirit , if the Spirit of God dwells in you . If any one has not the Spirit of Christ , that man is not his .
45008010	If Christ is in you the body is dead because of sin , but the spirit is life because of righteousness .
45008011	If the Spirit of him who raised up Jesus from the dead dwells in you , he who raised up Christ Jesus from the dead gives life even to your mortal bodies , through his indwelling Spirit in you .
45008012	So then , brethren , we are debtors , not to the flesh to live according to the flesh ;
45008013	for if you live according to the flesh , you will die ; but if by the Spirit you put to death the practices of the body , you will live .
45008014	For as many as are led by the Spirit of God , they are the sons of God .
45008015	For you did not receive a spirit of bondage leading again to fear , but you received a spirit of sonship , in which we cry , Abba , Father .
45008016	The Spirit itself witnesses with our spirits that we are children of God .
45008017	And if children , we are also heirs â heirs of God , joint heirs with Christ , since we suffer with him that we may also be glorified with him .
45008018	For I estimate that the sufferings of this present time amount to nothing in comparison with the glory that is to be revealed for us .
45008019	For the earnest expectation of the creation is waiting for the revelation of the sons of God .
45008020	For the creation was made subject to folly not willingly , but for the sake of him who subjected it , in hope ,
45008021	because the creation itself will be freed from the slavery of decay into the glorious freedom of the children of God .
45008022	For we know that all the creation groans in the pangs of childbirth until now .
45008023	And not the creation alone , but we ourselves also who have the first-fruits of the Spirit , groan within ourselves in expectation of the sonship , the liberation of our bodies .
45008024	For we are saved by hope ; but hope that is seen is not hope , for what any one sees , why does he hope for ?
45008025	But if we hope for what we do not see , we patiently wait for it .
45008026	Thus also the Spirit helps us in our weakness . For we do not know what to pray for as we ought , but the Spirit itself intercedes for us with sighs beyond words .
45008027	And he who searches hearts knows what is the mind of the Spirit , because he intercedes for the holy according to the will of God .
45008028	We know that all things work together for good to those who love God , to those who are called according to his purpose .
45008029	For those whom he foreknew he also predetermined to be conformed to the image of his Son , that he might be the first-born among many brethren .
45008030	And those whom he predetermined he also called , and those whom he called he also pronounced righteous , and those whom he pronounced righteous he also glorified .
45008031	What then shall we say to this ? If God is for us , who is against us ?
45008032	He who did not spare his own Son , but gave him up for us all , how shall he not with him graciously give us all things ?
45008033	Who shall bring a charge against God's elect ? God pronounces them righteous .
45008034	Who is there to condemn ? Christ Jesus died , or rather was raised , and he is on the right hand of God interceding for us .
45008035	Who shall separate us from Christ's love ? Shall trial or distress or persecution or famine or nakedness or danger or sword ?
45008037	On the contrary , in all these we more than conquer through him who loved us .
45008038	For I am persuaded that neither death nor life nor angels nor archangels , nor things present nor things to come , nor powers ,
45008039	nor height nor depth nor any other created thing will be able to separate us from God's love in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45009001	I AM speaking the truth in Christ ; I am saying nothing false ; my conscience bears witness with me in the Holy Spirit
45009002	that I have great grief and unceasing pain in my heart .
45009003	For I could wish myself to be accursed and cast away from Christ for the sake of my brethren , my kinsmen according to the flesh ,
45009004	who are Israelites , whose is the sonship and the glory and the covenants and the reception of the law and the worship and the promises ;
45009005	whose are the fathers and from whom by physical descent the Christ came . God who is over all be blessed through the ages ! Amen .
45009006	Not that God's word has failed . For not all who are of Israel are Israel ;
45009007	nor because they are descendants of Abraham are they all children ; but " through Isaac shall your descendants be named . "
45009008	That is , not the physical descendants are children , but the children of the promise are counted for descendants .
45009009	For the wording of the promise was , " At this time next year I will come and Sarah shall have a son . "
45009010	And not only so , but when Rebecca was about to bear children to our father Isaac ,
45009011	though the same man was father of both children and they were not yet born and had done nothing good or bad , in order that the purpose of God according to his choice might stand , not according to their works , but according to his call ,
45009012	it was said to her , " The older shall serve the younger . "
45009013	In the same way it is written , " Jacob I loved , but Esau I hated . "
45009014	What shall we say then ? Is there unrighteousness on God's part ? Never .
45009015	For he says to Moses , " I will have mercy on whom I have mercy and I will have compassion on whom I have compassion . "
45009016	So then it is not a question of the man who wills or who runs , but of God who shows mercy .
45009017	For the Scripture says to Pharaoh , " For this very purpose I raised you up in order to show my power upon you and to have my name proclaimed in all the earth . "
45009018	So then he has mercy on whom he chooses and he hardens whom he chooses .
45009019	You will say to me then , " Why does he still find fault ? For who has opposed his will ? "
45009020	But who are you , O man , who are answering back to God ? Does the thing that is moulded say to the moulder , " Why have you made me so ? "
45009021	Has not the potter the right to make from the same lump of clay one vessel for honor and another for dishonor ?
45009022	What if God , choosing to exhibit his wrath and to make known what he can do , bore in long patience the vessels of wrath made for destruction ,
45009023	and in order to make known the richness of his glory upon the vessels of mercy which he had prepared for glory
45009024	called us not only from the Jews but also from the Gentiles ?
45009025	As also he says in Hosea , " Those who are not my people I will call my people , and her who has not been beloved I will call beloved ,
45009026	and in the place where it was said to them , ' You are not my people , ' there they shall be called sons of the living God . "
45009027	Isaiah cried aloud regarding Israel , " Though the number of the sons of Israel is as the sand of the sea , only a remnant will be saved .
45009028	For the Lord will execute his sentence on the earth completely and speedily . "
45009029	Even as Isaiah predicted , " Unless the Lord of armies had left us some descendants , we should have become like Sodom and should have been made to resemble Gomorrah . "
45009030	What shall we say then ? That Gentiles who did not pursue righteousness obtained righteousness , the righteousness of faith ,
45009031	but Israel pursuing after the Law of righteousness did not attain to the Law .
45009032	Why ? Because they pursued it not by faith , but as it were by works . They stumbled over that stumbling stone ,
45009033	as it is written , " See , I am laying in Zion a stumbling stone , a rock to trip over , but he who has faith in him will never be put to shame . "
45010001	BRETHREN , the desire of my heart and my prayer to God for them is for their salvation .
45010002	For I bear them witness that they have a zeal for God , but not an intelligent one .
45010003	For , ignorant of God's righteousness and seeking to establish their own , they have not submitted to God's righteousness .
45010004	For Christ is the end of the Law for righteousness to every believer .
45010005	For Moses writes that he who does the righteousness of the Law shall live by it .
45010006	But the righteousness of faith says , " Do not say in your heart , ' Who shall ascend into heaven ? ' that is , to bring Christ down â "
45010007	or , ' Who shall descend into the abyss ? ' " â that is , to bring up Christ from the dead .
45010008	But what does it say ? " The word is near you , in your mouth and in your heart " â that is , the word of faith which we are proclaiming ,
45010009	that if you confess with your mouth the Lord Jesus and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead you will be saved .
45010010	For with the heart a man believes and becomes righteous , and with the mouth he confesses and attains salvation .
45010011	For the Scripture says , " No one who believes in him will be put to shame . "
45010012	For there is no difference between Jew and Greek . For there is the same Lord of all , rich toward all who call upon him .
45010013	For " Every one who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved . "
45010014	How then shall they call on him in whom they have not believed ? How shall they believe in him of whom they have not heard ? How shall they hear without some one to proclaim him ?
45010015	How shall they proclaim him unless they are sent ? As it is written , " How beautiful are the feet of those who bring good news ! "
45010016	But have not all heard the good news ? For Isaiah says , " Lord , who has believed our report ? "
45010017	So then faith comes from the report and report comes through the word of Christ .
45010018	But I say , it cannot be true that they have not heard , can it ? On the contrary , " Their sound has gone out into all the earth and their words to the ends of the world . "
45010019	I say , it cannot be that Israel did not know , can it ? First Moses says , " I will excite you to jealousy by what is not a nation and by a foolish nation I will provoke you to anger . "
45010020	And Isaiah makes bold to say , " I was found by those who were not seeking me : I became manifest to those who were not inquiring for me . "
45010021	But to Israel he says , " All day long I stretched forth my hands to a people who disobey and answer back . "
45011001	I SAY then , can it be that God has repudiated his people ? Never . For I am an Israelite , a descendant of Abraham , of the tribe of Benjamin .
45011002	God has not repudiated his people whom he foreknew . Do you not know what the Scripture says in the story of Elijah , how he prays to God against Israel ?
45011003	" Lord , they have killed thy prophets : they have demolished thy altars , and I only am left and they are seeking my life . "
45011004	But what was the divine response ? " I have left to myself seven thousand men who have not knelt to Baal . "
45011005	So at this present time there is a remnant according to a gracious selection .
45011006	But if it is by grace it is no longer because of works , for then grace would be no longer grace .
45011007	What then ? Israel has not found what it is seeking , but the chosen have found it . And the rest have been made dull ,
45011008	as it is written , " God gave them a stupid spirit , eyes not for seeing and ears not for hearing until this day . "
45011009	And David says , " Let their table become a snare and a trap , a stumbling block and a retribution .
45011010	Let their eyes be darkened so as not to see , and bow down their backs always . "
45011011	I say , then , have they stumbled just in order that they may fall ? Never . But by their fall salvation comes to the Gentiles so as to arouse the emulation of the Jews .
45011012	If their fall is the riches of the world and their loss the riches of the Gentiles , how much more will their full restoration be !
45011013	But I say to you Gentiles â since I am an apostle to Gentiles I glory in my office ,
45011014	if in any way I may arouse to emulation my own kindred and save some of them â
45011015	if their rejection is the reconciliation of the world , what will their welcome back be but life from the dead ?
45011016	If the first fruit was holy , so will the mass be ; and if the root was holy , so will be the branches .
45011017	If some of the branches were broken off and you , who are a wild olive , were grafted in among them and became a sharer in the root and rich sap of the olive ,
45011018	do not exult over the branches . Even though you exult , it is not you who are supporting the root , but the root is supporting you .
45011019	You will say then , " Branches were broken off so that I might be grafted in . "
45011020	Certainly , for lack of faith they were broken off , and you are standing by faith . Do not be proud , but be afraid .
45011021	For if God did not spare the natural branches , neither will he spare you .
45011022	See the kindness and the rigor of God , toward those who fell rigor , but toward you God's kindness , if you continue in his kindness , else you too will be cut off .
45011023	And they if they do not continue in their unbelief will be grafted in .
45011024	For God is able to graft them back . For if you were cut from your natural stock , a wild olive tree , and were grafted , contrary to nature , into a good olive tree , how much more will the natural branches be grafted into their own olive tree !
45011025	I would not have you ignorant , brethren , of this mystery , that you may not be self-conceited , because stupidity in a measure has come upon Israel until the full number of Gentiles comes in ,
45011026	and thus all Israel will be saved , as it is written , " From Zion will come the deliverer . He will remove ungodliness from Jacob .
45011027	And this is my covenant with them when I take away their sins . "
45011028	According to the good news they are enemies for your sake , but according to the promise they are beloved for their fathers ' sake .
45011029	God never changes his mind about his gifts and his call .
45011030	For as you were once disobedient to God , but now have found mercy through their disobedience ,
45011031	so they have now been disobedient in your time of mercy , that they too may now obtain mercy .
45011032	For God has shut up all in unbelief in order that he may have mercy on all .
45011033	O the depth of the wealth both of the wisdom and the knowledge of God ! How unsearchable are his judgments , how untraceable his ways !
45011034	For who has known the mind of the Lord ? Or who became his counsellor ?
45011035	Who first gave to him so as to receive repayment ?
45011036	For from him and through him and to him are all things . To him be glory through the ages ! Amen .
45012001	I BEG you therefore , brethren , by the mercies of God , to present your bodies as a living and holy sacrifice , pleasing to God â your rational worship .
45012002	Do not follow the fashions of this world , but be transformed by the renewal of your minds so as to recognize what is the good and pleasing and perfect will of God .
45012003	Through the grace given to me I say to every one among you not to think of himself more highly than he ought , but to think so as to become wise , as God has allotted to each a measure of faith .
45012004	For as in one body we have many members and the members do not all have the same function ,
45012005	so we who are many are one body in Christ and individually members of one another .
45012006	Having gifts differing according to the grace given to us , if it is prophecy , let us use it according to the proportion of our faith ;
45012007	if it is service , let us use it in service . Let the teacher use his gift in teaching .
45012008	Let the exhorter use his gift in exhorting . Let him who gives do it in simplicity . Let him who manages do it earnestly . Let him who helps the needy do it cheerfully .
45012009	Let your love be without pretense . Abhor what is evil ; cling to the good .
45012010	Have brotherly love toward one another like family affection , in honor preferring one another ,
45012011	never flagging in zeal , fervent in spirit , serving the Lord ,
45012012	rejoicing in hope , patient in trial , constant in prayer ,
45012013	contributing to the needs of the holy , devoted to hospitality .
45012014	Pray for blessings on your persecutors , blessings , not curses .
45012015	Rejoice with those who rejoice , weep with those who weep .
45012016	Be in harmony with one another . Do not be thinking of high things , but be content with humble things . Do not become conceited .
45012017	Repay to no one evil for evil . Aim at what is honorable in the sight of all men .
45012018	If possible , so far as depends on you , live at peace with all men .
45012019	Do not revenge yourselves , beloved , but give place to God's wrath . For it is written , " Vengeance is mine ; I will repay , says the Lord . "
45012020	But , " if your enemy is hungry , feed him ; if he is thirsty , give him drink ; for in so doing you will heap coals of fire on his head . "
45012021	Do not be overcome by evil , but overcome evil with good .
45013001	LET every person be obedient to the superior authorities . For there is no authority except from God and the actual authorities have been appointed by God .
45013002	So he who resists the authority opposes the arrangement of God . Those who resist will bring on themselves condemnation .
45013003	For rulers are not a terror to good deeds , but to bad . Do you wish not to fear the authority ? Do what is good and you will have praise from it .
45013004	For he is a servant of God to promote your good . But if you are doing evil , be afraid ; for he does not bear the sword to no purpose . For he is God's servant to inflict his wrath on him who practices evil .
45013005	Therefore we must be obedient , not only because of the punishment but as a matter of conscience .
45013006	For this reason also you pay tribute . For they are God's officers attending to this very thing .
45013007	Pay to all their dues , tribute to whom tribute is due , custom to whom custom is due , respect to whom respect is due , honor to whom honor is due .
45013008	Owe no one anything , except to love one another . He who loves the other has fulfilled the Law .
45013009	For the commandments , " Thou shalt not commit adultery , " " Thou shalt not commit murder , " " Thou shalt not steal , " " Thou shalt not covet , " and any other that there may be , are summed up in this : " Thou shalt love thy neighbor as thyself . "
45013010	Love works no evil to a neighbor . Love therefore is full obedience to the Law .
45013011	Live thus because you know this crisis , for it is already time for you to awake from sleep . For now our salvation is nearer than when we became believers .
45013012	The night is far spent , the day draws near . Let us put away the deeds of darkness , let us put on the weapons of light .
45013013	Let us live becomingly as in the day , not in revelry and drunkenness , not in sensuality and licentiousness , not in quarrelling and jealousy .
45013014	But put on the Lord Jesus Christ and make no provision for gratifying physical passions .
45014001	WELCOME him who is weak in the faith , but not in order to decide disputed questions .
45014002	One man believes in eating all things . The weak man eats vegetables .
45014003	The man who eats is not to despise the one who does not eat , and he who does not eat is not to judge the one who eats . For God has accepted him .
45014004	Who are you to judge the servant of another ? To his own master he stands or falls , and stand he will , for God is able to make him stand .
45014005	One man esteems one day above another , another man esteems every day . Let each be fully persuaded in his own mind .
45014006	He who regards the day regards it to the Lord and he who eats eats to the Lord , for he gives thanks to God . And he who does not eat abstains for the Lord and gives thanks to God .
45014007	For no one of us is living for himself and no one dies for himself .
45014008	If we live we live for the Lord and if we die we die for the Lord . So whether we live or die we are the Lord's .
45014009	For to this end Christ died and lived again , in order that he might be Lord both of the dead and of the living .
45014010	But you , why do you judge your brother ? Or you , why do you treat your brother with contempt ? For we shall all stand before the judgment seat of God .
45014011	For it is written , " As I live , says the Lord , every knee shall bend to me and every tongue shall confess to God . "
45014012	So then each one of us shall give account for himself to God .
45014013	Therefore let us no longer judge one another , but let us rather decide not to put a stumbling block in a brother's way , or anything to trip him up .
45014014	I know and am persuaded in the Lord Jesus that nothing is defiling in itself . But to one who thinks anything to be defiling it is defiling .
45014015	If because of your food your brother is grieved , you are no longer walking in love . Do not with your food destroy him for whom Christ died .
45014016	Do not let what is good to you be spoken of as evil .
45014017	For the kingdom of God is not food and drink , but righteousness and peace and joy in the Holy Spirit .
45014018	For he who thus serves Christ is pleasing to God and esteemed by men .
45014019	Therefore , let us seek for what makes for peace and our mutual upbuilding .
45014020	Do not for the sake of food break down the work of God . All things are pure , but anything is evil to the man who eats it with a feeling of doing wrong .
45014021	It is noble not to eat meat or to drink wine or to do anything over which your brother stumbles .
45014022	The faith that you have , have to yourself before God . Blessed is the man who does not condemn himself for what he allows himself .
45014023	He who has doubts and still eats stands condemned , because he is not acting from faith . But whatever does not spring from faith is sin .
45015001	WE who are strong ought to bear the infirmities of the weak , and not to please ourselves .
45015002	Each of us should please his neighbor for his good so as to build him up .
45015003	For Christ did not please himself , but , as it is written , " The reproaches of those who were reproaching thee fell on me . "
45015004	All that was written of old was written for our instruction , in order that by patience and by the encouragement of the Scriptures we may have hope .
45015005	May the God of patience and encouragement grant to you to have harmony with one another , in the manner of Christ Jesus ,
45015006	so that with one mind and one voice you may glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
45015007	Therefore , welcome one another as Christ welcomed us , to the glory of God .
45015008	For I say that Christ became a servant of circumcision for the sake of God's truth , in order to confirm the promises given to the fathers
45015009	and that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy , as it is written , " For this will I confess thee among the Gentiles and sing to thy name . "
45015010	And again Scripture says , " Rejoice , Gentiles , with his people . "
45015011	And again , " Sing to the Lord , all Gentiles , and let all the peoples praise him . "
45015012	And again Isaiah says , " There will be a root of Jesse , and one who rises to rule Gentiles : in him Gentiles will hope . "
45015013	May the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing , so that you may abound in hope through the power of the Holy Spirit !
45015014	I am persuaded , my brethren â yes , I myself â regarding you , that you are full of goodness , filled with all knowledge , able to instruct one another .
45015015	But I have written rather boldly to you , partly to remind you , because of the grace given to me from God ,
45015016	that I may be a minister of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles , in priestly service of the good news of God , in order that the offering of the Gentiles may be acceptable , sanctified by the Holy Spirit .
45015017	I do boast in Christ Jesus of my work for God .
45015018	For I will not venture to speak except of what Christ has done through me to promote obedience of Gentiles , by word and deed ,
45015019	through the power of signs and wonders , by the power of the Holy Spirit , so that from Jerusalem around to Illyricum , I have fully proclaimed the good news of Christ ,
45015020	being ambitious to tell the good news where Christ has not been named , so that I might not build on any other man's foundation ,
45015021	but as it is written , " They who have had no message of him shall see and they who have not heard shall understand . "
45015022	This is why I have been so much hindered in coming to you .
45015023	But now having no more territory in these regions and having for many years had a strong desire to come to you
45015024	while making a journey to Spain , I hope to see you as I pass through and to be furthered on my journey by you , after first partially satisfying my desire of being with you .
45015025	But now I am on my way to Jerusalem to render service to the holy .
45015026	For Macedonia and Achaia have been pleased to make a contribution for the poor among the holy in Jerusalem .
45015027	They have been pleased to do this and indeed they are indebted to them . For if the Gentiles have shared their things of the spirit , they owe them sacred service in things of the body .
45015028	So after completing this and sealing to them this fruit , I shall come away and pass by you to Spain .
45015029	And I know that when I come to you it will be in the fullness of the blessing of Christ .
45015030	I beg you , brethren , for the sake of our Lord Jesus and the love of the Spirit to join me in wrestling in prayer to God on my behalf ,
45015031	that I may be delivered from the unbelievers in Judaea and that my service in Jerusalem may be pleasing to the holy ,
45015032	that I may come to you with joy by the will of God and be refreshed with you .
45015033	The God of peace be with all of you ! Amen .
45016001	I COMMEND to you our sister Phoebe , a servant of the church in Cenchreae ,
45016002	that you may receive her in the Lord in a way worthy of the holy , and help her in any matter in which she may need you . For she has been a provider for many , myself included .
45016003	Give my greetings to Prisca and Aquila , my fellow workers in Christ Jesus ,
45016004	who for my life risked their own necks , to whom not I alone give thanks , but also all the churches of the Gentiles .
45016005	Give my greetings also to the church in their house . Give my greetings to Epaenetus my beloved , who is the first-fruit of Asia for Christ .
45016006	Give my greetings to Mary , who has worked hard for you .
45016007	Give my greetings to Andronicus and Junias , men of my race and my companions in prison , who are eminent among the apostles , who also were in Christ before me .
45016008	Give my greetings to Ampliatus my beloved in the Lord .
45016009	Give my greetings to Urbanus our fellow worker in Christ , and to Stachys my beloved .
45016010	Give my greetings to Apelles , that tested man in Christ . Give my greetings to the household of Aristobulus .
45016011	Give my greetings to Herodion , who is of my race . Give my greetings to those of the household of Narcissus who are in the Lord .
