47001001	PAUL , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and Timothy the brother , to the church of God that is in Corinth with all the holy that are in all Achaia :
47001002	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ !
47001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , the Father of loving kindness and the God of all encouragement ,
47001004	who encourages us in every distress so that we may be able to encourage those who are in every distress by the encouragement by which we ourselves have been encouraged by God .
47001005	Because as the sufferings of Christ are abundant in our case , so through Christ our encouragement is abundant .
47001006	But if we are in distress , it is for your encouragement and salvation . If we are encouraged , it is for your encouragement which is effective in the endurance of the same sufferings that we suffer .
47001007	Our hope is strong regarding you , since we know that as you are partakers of the sufferings so you are of the encouragement .
47001008	For we do not wish you to be ignorant , brethren , regarding the distress that came on us in Asia â that we were exceedingly weighed down , beyond our strength , so that we despaired even of life .
47001009	Indeed we have the sentence of death within ourselves , that our trust may not rest on ourselves , but on God who raises the dead .
47001010	He delivered us from such a death and will deliver , and we have hope in him that he will go on delivering ,
47001011	while you help by your prayers for us , so that from many persons thanksgiving may arise for the gift granted to us through the prayers of many for us .
47001012	For this is what we boast of , the witness of our conscience that in holiness , and sincerity before God , not in fleshly wisdom , but in the grace of God , we have lived in the world and especially toward you .
47001013	For we are not writing to you anything but what you read and acknowledge and I hope you will acknowledge to the end ,
47001014	as you have partly acknowledged it about us , that we are your ground of boasting and you are ours on the day of our Lord Jesus .
47001015	With this confidence I intended to come to you first , so that you might have a second favor ,
47001016	by my visiting you on the way to Macedonia and again coming back from Macedonia to you and being sped by you on my way toward Juda .
47001017	When I was intending this , did I show fickleness ? Or do I plan what I plan according to the flesh , so that I may say yes , yes , and no , no ?
47001018	As God is faithful , my word to you is not yes and no .
47001019	For the Son of God , Christ Jesus , who was proclaimed among you by us â myself and Silvanus and Timothy â was not yes and no , but in him was yes .
47001020	For all the promises of God , however many , have their yes in him . Therefore also through him is the Amen to the glory of God through us .
47001021	It is God who makes us and you steadfast to Christ , and has anointed us
47001022	and sealed us and has given the pledge of the Spirit in our hearts .
47001023	I call God as a witness against my soul that in order to spare you I have not yet come to Corinth .
47001024	Not that we are lords over your faith , but fellow workers sharing your joy , for you are standing firm in the faith .
47002001	BUT I decided this in my own mind , not to come again to you in sorrow .
47002002	For if I grieve you , who is there to cheer me except those who are grieved by me ?
47002003	I am writing this very thing so that I may not come and have grief from those who ought to make me glad , for I am confident in regard to all of you that my joy is yours .
47002004	For out of great distress and pain of heart I am writing with many tears , not that you may be grieved , but that you may know the love that I have beyond measure for you .
47002005	But if any one has caused grief , he has grieved not me , but to some extent â not to be too severe â all of you .
47002006	Sufficient for such a one is this punishment by the majority ,
47002007	so that on the contrary you should rather forgive him and encourage him , that such a one may not be swallowed up in excessive grief .
47002008	Therefore I beg you to assure him of your love .
47002009	Because for this purpose I am writing , that I may know your tested character , whether you are obedient in everything .
47002010	To whomever you forgive anything I also forgive it , and what I have forgiven , if I have forgiven anything , it was for your sake in the sight of Christ ,
47002011	that Satan may not take advantage of us , for we are not ignorant of his purposes .
47002012	When I came to Troas for the good news of Christ and a door had been opened for me in the Lord ,
47002013	I had no rest in my spirit because I did not find Titus my brother , but bidding them farewell I came away to Macedonia .
47002014	Thanks be to God who always leads us in his triumph in Christ and spreads through us the sweet odor of the knowledge of him in every place .
47002015	For we are for God a sweet odor of Christ â in the saved and in the perishing .
47002016	To the latter an odor from death to death , to the former an odor from life to life . And who is competent for this ?
47002017	For we are not , like the most , adulterating the message of God for gain , but in sincerity , as from God , in the presence of God , we speak in Christ .
47003001	ARE we beginning again to recommend ourselves ? Do we need , as some do , letters of recommendation to you or from you ?
47003002	You are our letter , written in our hearts , known and read by all men ,
47003003	evidently a letter of Christ delivered by us , written not with ink , but with the Spirit of the living God , not on stone tablets , but on tablets that are hearts of flesh .
47003004	We have such confidence through Christ toward God .
47003005	Not that of ourselves we are fit to reason out anything as from ourselves , but our fitness is from God ,
47003006	who has fitted us to be servants of a new covenant , not of the letter , but of the spirit . For the letter kills , but the spirit gives life .
47003007	If the service that brought death , engraved in letters on stones , came in glory , so that the children of Israel could not look steadily at the face of Moses because of the glory of his face â that fading glory â
47003008	how much more glorious will not the service of the Spirit be ?
47003009	For if the service that brought condemnation was glory , much more will the service that brings righteousness surpass in glory .
47003010	For what was made so glorious is in a way no longer glorious compared with the glory that surpasses it .
47003011	For if what was to be ended came in glory , much more glorious must be that which is enduring .
47003012	With such a hope then we speak with great frankness ,
47003013	and are not like Moses , who used to put a veil over his face so that the children of Israel might not see when the vanishing glory ended ;
47003014	but their thinking was dulled . For to this day the same veil remains unlifted when the old covenant is read ; because it is done away only in Christ .
47003015	To this day when Moses is read the veil lies on their hearts ;
47003016	" but when they turn to the Lord the veil is taken away . "
47003017	The Lord is the Spirit , and where the Spirit of the Lord is there is liberty .
47003018	And we all , with unveiled face , reflecting the glory of the Lord , are changed into the same likeness from glory to glory as by the Spirit of the Lord .
47004001	THEREFORE , having this service through God's mercy , we are not downhearted ,
47004002	but we have renounced shameful secret things , not living in craftiness nor adulterating God's message , but by the openness of truth commending ourselves to every man's conscience in the sight of God .
47004003	If our good news is veiled , it is veiled to those who are going to ruin ,
47004004	in whom the god of this world has blinded the thinking of the unbelieving so that the light of the glorious good news of Christ , who is the image of God , may not shine in .
47004005	For we are not proclaiming ourselves but Christ Jesus as Lord , and ourselves as your servants for Jesus ' sake .
47004006	Because it is the God who said , " Light shall shine out of darkness , " who has shone in our hearts bringing the light of the glorious knowledge of God in the face of Christ .
47004007	But we have this treasure in earthen jars , that the surpassing power may be God's and not ours â
47004008	in every way distressed , but not reduced to straits , perplexed , but not in despair ,
47004009	persecuted , but not forsaken , cast down , but not destroyed ,
47004010	always bearing about in our bodies the death of Jesus that the life also of Jesus may be manifest in our bodies .
47004011	For we , though living , are always delivered up to death for Jesus ' sake , that also the life of Jesus may be manifested in our mortal flesh .
47004012	So death works in us , but life in you .
47004013	Having the same spirit of faith , as it is written , " I believed , therefore I spoke , " we too believe and therefore speak ,
47004014	knowing that he who raised up Jesus will also raise us up with Jesus and place us in his presence with you .
47004015	For all things are for your sake , that grace abounding through many may overflow in thanksgiving to the glory of God .
47004016	Therefore we are not downhearted , but even if our outward man is wasting away , yet our inward man is renewed day by day .
47004017	For our momentary and light distress is working out for us a far surpassing and eternal weight of glory
47004018	while we contemplate not the things that are seen , but the things unseen . For the things that are seen are transient , but the things unseen are eternal .
47005001	FOR we know that if this tent , our earthly home , is thrown down , we have a building of God , a home not made by hands , eternal in the heavens .
47005002	For in this we sigh in earnest desire to put on our dwelling that comes from heaven ,
47005003	since if we put that on we shall not be found naked .
47005004	For while we are in this tent we sigh being burdened , not that we wish to be unclothed , but to put on the other , that what is mortal may be swallowed up in life .
47005005	He who has prepared us for this very thing is God , and he has given to us the pledge of the Spirit .
47005006	So being always of good courage and knowing that while living at home in the body we are living in a foreign land away from the Lord â
47005007	for we walk by faith , not by sight â
47005008	I say we are of good courage and wish rather to live in the land foreign to the body and be at home with the Lord .
47005009	Therefore also we are ambitious to be pleasing to him , whether at home with him or in this foreign land .
47005010	For we must all appear as we truly are before the judgment seat of Christ , that each may receive the award for what he has done with his body , according to his actions , whether good or bad .
47005011	Knowing , therefore , the fear of the Lord , we are persuading men . What we are is plain to God , and I hope that it is also plain to your consciences .
47005012	We are not recommending ourselves again to you , but giving occasion to you for boasting on our behalf , that you may have it to use against those who boast of appearances and not of heart .
47005013	For if we were out of our minds it was for God , and if we are sane it is for you .
47005014	For the love of Christ impels us , convinced of this , that if one died for all , then all died ,
47005015	and he died for all that the living may no longer live for themselves , but for him who died for them and was raised again .
47005016	So we , from now on , know no man according to the flesh . Even if we have known Christ according to the flesh , yet now we know him so no more .
47005017	So if any one is in Christ he is a new creature . The old things have passed away , they have become new .
47005018	And all things are from God , who has reconciled us to himself through Christ and given to us the service of reconciliation â
47005019	to proclaim that God was in Christ reconciling the world to himself , not counting against men their sins , and that he has committed to us the message of reconciliation .
47005020	So we are ambassadors for Christ , as if God were appealing to you through us . We pray you on Christ's behalf to be reconciled to God .
47005021	Him who knew no sin God made sin for our sake that we might become the righteousness of God in him .
47006001	AS God's fellow workers we also beg you not to receive his grace fruitlessly .
47006002	For he says , " At a favorable time I heard you and on a day of salvation I helped you . " Now is a particularly favorable time , now is a day of salvation .
47006003	We give no occasion for stumbling to any one that our service may not be blamed ,
47006004	but in everything we commend ourselves as God's servants in great patience , in distresses , in necessities , in hardships ,
47006005	in floggings , in prisons , in riots , in toils , in sleepless nights , in fastings ,
47006006	with purity , with knowledge , with long-suffering , with kindness , with the Holy Spirit , with sincere love ,
47006007	with the message of truth , with the power of God ; by the weapons of righteousness in the right hand and the left ,
47006008	by honor and shame , by slander and praise ; as deceivers yet true ,
47006009	as unknown yet well known , as dying and yet we are living , as chastised yet not put to death ,
47006010	as sorrowful yet always rejoicing , as poor yet making many rich , as having nothing yet owning all things .
47006011	Our mouth is open to you , Corinthians , our heart expands itself .
47006012	You find no narrowness in us , the narrowness is in your own sympathies .
47006013	As a fair return , I am speaking as to my children , let your hearts expand .
47006014	Do not be yoked up , like unmatched animals , with unbelievers . For what partnership have righteousness and lawlessness , or what fellowship has light with darkness ,
47006015	or what harmony has Christ with Belial , or what share has a believer with an unbeliever ?
47006016	What agreement has the Temple of God with idols ? For we are the Temple of the living God , as God said , " I will dwell in them and walk among them , and I will be their God and they shall be my people .
47006017	Therefore come out from the midst of them and be separate , says the Lord , and do not touch an unclean thing , and I will receive you
47006018	and will be a Father to you and you shall be sons and daughters to me , says the Lord , the Ruler of all . "
47007001	HAVING then these promises , beloved , let us purify ourselves from every defilement of flesh or spirit , in reverence for God making our holiness complete .
47007002	Make room for us in your hearts . We have wronged no one ; we have injured no one ; we have taken advantage of no one .
47007003	I am not saying this to condemn you , for I have already said that you have such a place in our hearts that we are ready to die with you or to live with you .
47007004	Great is my frankness in speaking to you ; great is my boasting of you ; I am filled with encouragement , running over with joy at every distress of ours .
47007005	For since we came to Macedonia our flesh has had no rest , but we have been distressed in every way , conflicts without , fears within .
47007006	But God , who encourages the depressed , encouraged us by the coming of Titus ,
47007007	and not by his coming only , but also by the encouragement by which he was encouraged about you . He told us of your longing for me , your lamentation , your zeal in my behalf , so that I rejoice the more .
47007008	For if I grieved you in my letter I do not regret it , though I did regret it , seeing that that letter grieved you even for a time ,
47007009	but I am glad now , not that you were grieved , but that your grief led to a change of heart . You were grieved as God approves so that you should in nothing suffer loss from us .
47007010	For such grief as God approves works a change of heart leading to salvation and is never to be regretted . But the grief of the world results in death .
47007011	Notice this very grieving as God approves , how great earnestness resulted from it in your case , what effort to defend yourselves , what indignation , what fear , what longing , what zeal , what just punishment ! In everything you showed yourselves blameless in the matter .
47007012	So although I wrote to you , I did it not for the sake of him who did the wrong , nor for the sake of him who suffered wrong , but that your earnestness for us might be made plain to you before God .
47007013	On this account we have been encouraged . In addition to this encouragement of ours , we rejoiced very much more over the joy of Titus because his spirit has been refreshed by you all ,
47007014	for if I have made any boast regarding you I have not been put to shame , but as we spoke everything in truth to you so our boasting over Titus turned out the truth .
47007015	And his affections go out more strongly to you when he remembers the obedience of you all , how with reverence and trembling you received him .
47007016	I am glad to be in every respect of good courage regarding you .
47008001	I MUST tell you , brethren , of the grace of God that has been given to the churches of Macedonia ,
47008002	that in a great trial of distress their abundant joy and their deep poverty have abounded in the wealth of their liberality .
47008003	For according to their ability , I bear witness , and beyond their ability , of their own accord ,
47008004	with great urgency they begged of us the favor of fellowship in the service for the holy ,
47008005	and this not as we had hoped , but first they gave themselves to the Lord and to us through the will of God .
47008006	Therefore we encouraged Titus that as he had begun so he should complete this grace among you .
47008007	But as you excel in every way , in faith and speech and knowledge and in all earnestness and in the love you learned from us , be sure to excel in this grace also .
47008008	I speak not by way of command , but testing the genuineness of your love by the earnestness of others .
47008009	For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ , that though he was rich yet for your sake he became poor , that you by his poverty might become rich .
47008010	In this I give my opinion , for this is advantageous for you , since a year ago you were first to begin not only the doing but the wanting to do anything .
47008011	But now complete the doing , that as there was a readiness in willing so there may be a completion according to your means .
47008012	For if there is first the readiness , a gift is acceptable according to what a man has , not according to what he has not .
47008013	I do not mean that others shall have relief and you shall have trouble ,
47008014	but by equality at the present time your abundance may supply their need so that their abundance may come at your need â that there may be equality ,
47008015	as it is written , " He who gathered much had nothing over and he who gathered little had no lack . "
47008016	Thanks be to God who puts into the heart of Titus the same interest in you .
47008017	For he welcomed our appeal , but being unusually interested comes to you of his own choice .
47008018	With him we are sending the brother whose praise for service to the good news has spread through all the churches ,
47008019	and not only that , but he was appointed by the churches as our fellow traveler in this gracious errand carried out by us to the glory of the Lord himself and by our own eager desire .
47008020	We are taking care that no one shall blame us for our administration of this bountiful fund ,
47008021	for we are providing arrangements honorable , not only in the sight of the Lord , but also in the sight of men .
47008022	We are sending along with them also our brother whose earnestness we have tested many times in many ways , and who is now especially earnest because of his great confidence in you .
47008023	If any one asks about Titus , he is my intimate friend and fellow worker for you . If it is our brethren , they are the messengers of the churches , the glory of Christ .
47008024	Show them in the sight of the churches your love and the ground of our boasting to them about you .
47009001	REGARDING the service to the holy , it is superfluous for me to write to you .
47009002	For I know your readiness and I am boasting about you to the Macedonians , that Achaia was ready a year ago , and your zeal has stimulated the most of them .
47009003	I am sending the brethren that our boasting about you may not be proved in this matter an empty boast , so that you may be ready as I have said ,
47009004	and if any Macedonians come with me and find you unprepared , we , not to say you , may not be made ashamed of this confidence .
47009005	So I think it necessary to urge the brethren to go on in advance to you and prepare before-hand your promised gift , that it may be ready as a gift and not as if extorted .
47009006	Remember this , he who sows sparingly will reap sparingly and he who sows bountifully will reap bountifully .
47009007	Let each give as he has purposed in his heart , not grudgingly nor of necessity , for God loves a cheerful giver .
47009008	God is able to make every blessing abound for you so that having in everything always all that you need , you may abound in every good work ,
47009009	as it is written , " He scattered , he gave to the poor , his righteousness endures forever . "
47009010	He who supplies seed to the sower and bread for food will supply and make abundant your seed and will increase the fruits of your righteousness .
47009011	You will be enriched in everything so that you will have all liberality which through our agency causes thanksgiving to God .
47009012	For the performance of this sacred service not only supplies the needs of the holy , but also overflows to God in many thanksgivings .
47009013	By the proof afforded by this service men are led to glorify God for your fidelity to your profession of faith in the good news of Christ , and for the liberality of your contributions toward them and toward all .
47009014	In their prayers in your behalf they pour out their longing love for you because of the surpassing grace of God that is upon you .
47009015	Thanks be to God for his unspeakable gift !
47010001	I MYSELF , Paul , beg you by the gentleness and sweet reasonableness of Christ â I who " to your face am humble when among you , but when absent am bold toward you " â
47010002	I pray that I may not when present have to be bold with the confidence with which I expect to show my courage against some who think of us as living according to the flesh .
47010003	For although living in the flesh we do not carry on our warfare according to the flesh ,
47010004	for the weapons of our warfare are not weapons of the flesh , but powerful under God for the destruction of fortresses .
47010005	We overthrow reasonings and every high thing that exalts itself against the knowledge of God , and take captive every thought into obedience to Christ
47010006	and are ready to take vengeance upon every disobedience when your obedience is complete .
47010007	Look at what is right before your eyes . If any one is confident that he belongs to Christ , let him again consider this regarding himself , that just as he belongs to Christ so also do we .
47010008	For if I boast somewhat excessively of our authority , which the Lord gave for building you up and not for pulling you down , I shall not be ashamed .
47010009	Let me not seem as if meaning to frighten you by letters .
47010010	Because , " His letters , " they say , " are mighty and strong , but his bodily presence is weak and his speaking amounts to nothing . "
47010011	Let such a person consider this , that what we are in words by letters when absent such we will be in deeds when present .
47010012	We do not venture to class ourselves or compare ourselves with some of those who are commending themselves . But they , measuring themselves among themselves and comparing themselves with themselves , do not understand .
47010013	We will not boast beyond measure , but according to the measure of the measuring rod which God assigned to us , and that reaches as far as you .
47010014	For we are not stretching ourselves , as if we did not reach to you , for we were the first to reach you with the good news of Christ .
47010015	We are not boasting beyond measure in the labors of others , but we have hope that as your faith grows we may have larger influence among you according to our measure and beyond ,
47010016	so that we may tell the good news to the regions lying beyond you and not boast of things already done in some other man's territory .
47010017	" Let him who boasts boast in the Lord . "
47010018	For it is not he who commends himself that is approved , but whom the Lord commends .
47011001	O THAT you would bear with me in a little foolishness . Yes , bear with me .
47011002	For I am jealous over you with the jealousy of God , for I betrothed you to one husband to present you as a pure virgin to Christ .
47011003	But I fear that , as the serpent deceived Eve by his cunning , your thoughts may be led away from sincerity and purity toward Christ .
47011004	For if some newcomer proclaims another Jesus whom we did not proclaim , or if you receive a different kind of spirit which you did not receive , or a different good news which you did not welcome , you bear with him finely .
47011005	I consider that I am in nothing inferior to the most eminent apostles .
47011006	If I am an ordinary man in speaking , still I am not in knowledge , but in everything we made that altogether clear to you .
47011007	Did I commit a sin when I humbled myself that you might be exalted , because I proclaimed to you the good news of God without pay ?
47011008	I robbed other churches by taking wages for serving you ,
47011009	and when I was with you and in need I was not a burden to any one , for the brethren who came from Macedonia supplied my need . In every way I kept myself from being a burden to you , and shall keep myself so .
47011010	As the truth of Christ is in me , this boast of mine shall not be stopped in the region of Achaia .
47011011	Why ? Because I do not love you ? God knows .
47011012	But what I am doing I shall do so as to cut away all ground of attack from those who wish ground , and that in what they boast of they may be found just like us .
47011013	For such are false apostles , deceitful workers , disguising themselves as apostles of Christ .
47011014	And no wonder , for Satan himself disguises himself as an angel of light .
47011015	So it is no great thing if his servants too disguise themselves as servants of righteousness . Their end will be according to their deeds .
47011016	I say again , let no one think me foolish . But , even if so , receive me as foolish , that I too may boast a little .
47011017	What I am saying I am not saying by the Lord's command , but as it were in foolishness , in this confident boasting .
47011018	Since many are boasting according to the flesh , I too will boast ,
47011019	for you who are wise bear pleasantly with the foolish .
47011020	You bear it if any one enslaves you , if any one devours you , if any one takes possession of you , if any one exalts himself , if any one strikes you in the face .
47011021	I say it with shame as if we had been weak . But in whatever any one is bold I too am bold .
47011022	Are they Hebrews ? So am I . Are they Israelites ? So am I . Are they descended from Abraham ? So am I .
47011023	Are they servants of Christ ? I superlatively â in labors beyond measure , in prisons beyond measure , in floggings excessively , in deaths often .
47011024	From Jews five times I received forty stripes less one ,
47011025	three times I was beaten with rods , once I was stoned , three times I was ship-wrecked , a night and day I have been in the deep ;
47011026	in journeys often , in perils of rivers , in perils of robbers , in perils from my own race , in perils from Gentiles , in perils in the city , in perils in the open country , in perils on the sea , in perils among false brethren ;
47011027	in toil and labor , in many a sleepless night , in hunger and thirst , in fastings often , in cold and nakedness .
47011028	Aside , from other things there is that which weighs on me daily , anxiety for all the churches .
47011029	Who is weak and I am not weak ? Who stumbles and I am not burning ?
47011030	If there must be boasting , I will boast of the things that show my weakness .
47011031	The God and Father of the Lord Jesus knows , he who is blessed forever , that I am not lying .
47011032	In Damascus the Governor under King Aretas was guarding the city of the Damascenes to arrest me ,
47011033	and through a window I was lowered in a basket and escaped from his hands .
47012001	I MUST boast , though it is unprofitable . I will come to visions and revelations of the Lord .
47012002	I know a man in Christ fourteen years ago â whether in the body I know not , or out of the body I know not ; God knows â such a man caught up to the third heaven .
47012003	I know such a man â whether in the body or out of the body I know not ; God knows â
47012004	that he was caught up into Paradise and heard unspeakable words which it is not lawful for man to speak .
47012005	Of such a one I will boast , but of myself I will not boast except of my weaknesses .
47012006	Even if I choose to boast I shall not be foolish , for I shall speak the truth . But I guard myself that no one may think of me beyond what he sees me to be , or hears from me ,
47012007	and because of the surpassing nature of the revelations . For this reason , that I should not be puffed up , there was given to me a thorn in the flesh , an angel of Satan , to torment me , so that I should not be puffed up .
47012008	Regarding this I three times begged the Lord that it might leave me .
47012009	But he has said to me , " My grace is sufficient for you ; for power is made perfect in weakness . " Most gladly then will I boast in my weaknesses , that the power of Christ may abide upon me .
47012010	Therefore I rejoice in weaknesses , in rough treatment , in necessities , in persecutions , in distresses for Christ's sake ; for when I am weak , then I am strong .
47012011	I have become foolish ; you made me . For I ought to have been recommended by you . For in nothing have I been inferior to the most eminent apostles , even though I am nothing .
47012012	The signs of an apostle were performed among you in all patience by miracles and wonders and deeds of power .
47012013	What is there in which you were made inferior to the rest of the churches except that I was not a burden to you ? Forgive me this wrong .
47012014	Now this third time I am ready to come to you , and I shall not be a burden to you . For I am not seeking yours , but you . For the children ought not to lay up money for the parents , but the parents for the children .
47012015	And I will most gladly spend and be spent for your souls . If I love you too much , am I loved the less ?
47012016	Be that as it may , I was not a burden to you . But being crafty I caught you with cunning ?
47012017	Did I take advantage of you through any one of those I sent to you ?
47012018	I begged Titus to go , and I sent along with him the brother . Did Titus take advantage of you ? Did we not act in the same spirit and walk in the same steps ?
47012019	Are you thinking all this while that we are defending ourselves to you ? We are speaking before God in Christ . All this , beloved , is to build you up .
47012020	For I am afraid that when I come I shall not find you such as I wish , and I myself may not be found by you such as you wish . I am afraid that there may be strife , jealousy , anger , rivalry , slanders , whisperings , conceit , disorders .
47012021	I am afraid that when I come again my God may humble me in your presence , and that I shall grieve over many of those who have been long sinning and have not repented of the impurity and unchastity and sensuality which they have practiced .
47013001	THIS third time I am coming to you . " By the evidence of two witnesses , or three , every matter shall be proved . "
47013002	Those who have been long sinning and all the rest I have forewarned and now forewarn , when I was present with you the second time and now when absent , that if I come again I shall not spare ;
47013003	since you are eager to have a test of Christ speaking in me . He is not weak toward you , but powerful among you .
47013004	He was crucified in weakness , but he is living by the power of God . And we are weak in him , but we shall live with him by the power of God for you .
47013005	Test yourselves whether you are in the faith , put yourselves to the proof . Are you not conscious that Jesus Christ is in you ? He is , unless you cannot stand the test .
47013006	I hope that you know that we are not unable to stand the test .
47013007	I pray to God that you may do nothing evil , not in order that we may seem to stand the test , but in order that you may do the right , though we should seem unable to stand the test .
47013008	For we cannot do anything against the truth ; our power is for the truth .
47013009	We rejoice when we are weak and you are strong . This we are praying for , your all-round character .
47013010	For this reason I am writing this while absent , so that when present I may not act with severity in the use of the authority which the Lord gave me for building you up , not for pulling you down .
47013011	Now , brethren , farewell . Be fully equipped ; take courage ; be of one mind ; live in peace ; then the God of love and peace will be with you .
47013012	Greet one another with a holy kiss .
47013013	All the holy send greetings .
47013014	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ , and the love of God , and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all .
48001001	PAUL an apostle â not from men or through men , but through Jesus Christ and God the Father , who raised him from the dead â
48001002	and all the brethren with me , to the churches of Galatia :
48001003	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ ,
48001004	who gave himself for our sins to deliver us from the present wicked world according to the will of our God and Father !
48001005	To him be glory through the ages of the ages ! Amen .
48001006	I am astonished that you are so quickly changing over from him who called you by the grace of Christ to a different kind of good news ,
48001007	though it is not another good news . But there are some who are perplexing you and wishing to pervert the good news of Christ .
48001008	But even if we , or an angel from heaven , should bring you any good news different from what we did bring you , let him be accursed !
48001009	As I said before , I say now again , if any one brings you good news different from what you have received , let him be accursed !
48001010	Am I now trying to please men or God ? If I were still trying to please men I should not be Christ's servant .
48001011	For I assure you , brethren , that the good news which I brought is not of man's devising .
48001012	For neither did I receive it from man nor was I taught it through man , but through a revelation of Jesus Christ .
48001013	You have heard of my former life in Judaism , that I furiously persecuted the church of God and made havoc of it ,
48001014	and I went further in Judaism than many of my own age and race , being intensely zealous for the traditions of my forefathers .
48001015	But when he who had appointed me when I was in my mother's womb , and had called me by his grace ,
48001016	was pleased to reveal his Son in me that I might tell the good news of him among the Gentiles , immediately I did not consult with flesh and blood ,
48001017	nor did I go up to Jerusalem to those who were apostles before me , but I went away into Arabia , and came back to Damascus .
48001018	Then , after three years , I went up to Jerusalem to visit Peter and stayed with him fifteen days .
48001019	But I saw no other one of the apostles , though I did see James the Lord's brother .
48001020	In what I am writing to you , before God I am not lying .
48001021	Then I came into the regions of Syria and Cilicia .
48001022	I was not known by face to the churches of Christ in Judaea .
48001023	Only they had heard that " he who used to persecute us is now telling the good news of the faith of which he once made havoc , "
48001024	and they glorified God on my account .
48002001	THEN after fourteen years I again went up to Jerusalem with Barnabas , taking along Titus .
48002002	I went up by revelation , and I stated to them the good news which I proclaim among the Gentiles . But I did this privately before those who were most esteemed , that I might not be running , or have run , to no Purpose .
48002003	But even Titus , who was with me and was a Greek , was not compelled to be circumcised ,
48002004	though it was suggested on account of false brethren who had been brought in , who had crept in to spy out our liberty which we have in Christ Jesus , in order to enslave us .
48002005	But we did not yield in subjection to them even for an hour , that the truth of the good news might continue with you .
48002006	But from those who were esteemed to be something â whatever they were , it makes no difference to me ; God does not regard the social standing of a man â those who were most esteemed did not impart to me anything additional .
48002007	But , on the contrary , seeing that I was entrusted with the good news for the uncircumcision as Peter was for the circumcision ,
48002008	for he who had worked in Peter for the apostleship to the circumcision had worked in me for the Gentiles ,
48002009	recognizing the grace given to me , James , Cephas , and John , who were regarded as pillars , gave the right hand of fellowship to me and Barnabas , that we should go to the Gentiles and they to the circumcision .
48002010	Only they wished us to remember the poor . This very thing I also was earnest in doing .
48002011	But when Peter came to Antioch , I opposed him to his face , because he had been justly censured .
48002012	For before certain persons came from James , he was eating with the Gentiles . But when they came , he drew back and separated himself , fearing those who were of the circumcision .
48002013	And the rest of the Jews practiced the same hypocrisy with him , so that even Barnabas was led off with them in their hypocrisy .
48002014	But when I saw that they were not walking straight according to the truth of the good news , I said to Cephas before them all , " If you who are a Jew are living like a Gentile and not like a Jew , how can you compel the Gentiles to live like Jews ? "
48002015	We who are Jews by nature and not sinners of the Gentiles ,
48002016	knowing that a man is not declared righteous because of works of law , but through faith in Christ Jesus , we also have put our faith in Christ Jesus that we may be declared righteous because of faith in Christ , and not because of works of law , for because of works of law no human being will be declared righteous .
48002017	If while seeking to be declared righteous in Christ we ourselves are found sinners , is Christ then a servant of sin ? Never .
48002018	For if I am building up again what I pulled down , I show myself as a transgressor .
48002019	For I through law died to law that I might live to God .
48002020	I have been crucified with Christ . I am living , yet no longer I , but Christ is living in me . The life that I am now living in flesh I am living by faith in the Son of God , who loved me and gave himself for me .
48002021	I do not make nothing of the grace of God , for if righteousness is through law , then Christ died for nothing .
48003001	O THOUGHTLESS Galatians , who has bewitched you before whose eyes Jesus Christ was pictured crucified ?
48003002	Only this I wish to learn from you : Was it because of works of law that you received the Spirit , or because of hearing with faith ?
48003003	Are you so thoughtless ? After beginning with spirit are you now finishing with flesh ?
48003004	Have you suffered such things to no purpose ? â if it is to no purpose .
48003005	He who supplies to you the Spirit and works miracles among you , is he doing it because of works of law or because of hearing with faith ,
48003006	just as Abraham had faith in God and it was credited to him for righteousness ?
48003007	You know , then , that those who are of faith â they are children of Abraham .
48003008	For the Scripture , foreseeing that God would declare the Gentiles righteous because of faith , announced the good news in advance to Abraham , " In you all the Gentiles will be blessed . "
48003009	So then those who are of faith are blessed with faithful Abraham .
48003010	For all who are of the works of law are under a curse , for it is written , " Cursed is every one who does not abide by all the precepts of the book of the Law and do them . "
48003011	But that by law no one is declared righteous before God is plain , because , " He who is righteous by faith shall live . "
48003012	But the Law is not of faith , but " He who does these things shall live by them . "
48003013	Christ redeemed us from the curse of the Law by becoming a curse for our sake , for it is written , " Cursed is every one who hangs on a tree , "
48003014	in order that the blessing of Abraham might in Jesus Christ come on the Gentiles , that they might receive through faith the promise of the Spirit .
48003015	Brethren , I am speaking humanly , a ratified covenant , although but a man's , no one can set aside or add to .
48003016	But the promises were spoken to Abraham and to his offspring . It does not say , " and to offsprings , " as meaning many , but as if meaning one , " and to your offspring , " who is Christ .
48003017	I mean this , a covenant ratified by God , the Law that came four hundred and thirty years afterward does not annul , so as to defeat the promise .
48003018	For if the inheritance is by law , it is no longer by promise . But God granted it to Abraham by promise .
48003019	Why then was the Law ? It was added later to make transgressions , until the Offspring should come to whom the promise had been made , and it was arranged through angels by the hand of a mediator .
48003020	A mediator does not belong to one person , but God is one .
48003021	Is the Law then against the promises of God ? Never ! For if a law had been given which could give life , then really righteousness would have come by law .
48003022	But the Scripture has shut up all under sin that the promise based on faith in Jesus Christ may be given to those who have faith .
48003023	Before faith came we were guarded under law , shut up waiting for the faith that was to be revealed .
48003024	Thus the Law became our tutor leading us to Christ , that we might be declared righteous by faith .
48003025	Now that faith has come , we are no longer under a tutor .
48003026	You are all sons of God through faith in Christ Jesus .
48003027	All who have been baptized into Christ have put on Christ .
48003028	There cannot be Jew or Greek , slave or free , male or female : for you all are one in Christ Jesus .
48003029	If you are Christ's , then you are Abraham's offspring and heirs according to the promise .
48004001	I SAY that as long as the heir is under age he differs in nothing from a slave , though he be owner of all .
48004002	But he is under guardians and managers until the day appointed by the father .
48004003	So we , when we were under age , were enslaved under the elementary lessons of the world ;
48004004	but , when the fullness of time came , God sent forth his Son born of a woman , born under the Law ,
48004005	that he might redeem those who were under Law , that we might receive the recognition as sons .
48004006	Because you are sons , God has sent into our hearts the Spirit of his Son crying Abba , Father .
48004007	So you are no longer a slave , but a son , and if a son , then also an heir , through God's act .
48004008	At the time when you did not know God you were enslaved to what by nature are not gods .
48004009	But now that you know God , or rather have been known by God , how are you turning back to the weak and beggarly elementary lessons to which you wish to be slaves again ?
48004010	You observe days and months and seasons and years .
48004011	You make me afraid that I have labored over you uselessly .
48004012	Become like me , brethren , I beg of you , for I became like you . You have not wronged me in anything .
48004013	You know that because of weakness of the flesh I told you the good news at first .
48004014	And you did not despise or spurn what was a trial to you in my bodily condition , but welcomed me as you would an angel of God , as you would Christ Jesus .
48004015	Where now is the blessing you pronounced on me ? For I bear you witness that if it had been possible you would have plucked out your own eyes and given them to me .
48004016	Have I become your enemy because I tell you the truth ?
48004017	They are paying court to you , but not honorably . No , they wish to shut you out , so that you may pay court to them .
48004018	It is honorable to be courted in an honorable matter always , and not only when I am with you ,
48004019	my children , for whom I again am suffering birth pangs until Christ is formed in you .
48004020	Would that I could be present with you now and could change my tone , for I am at a loss about you .
48004021	Tell me , you who wish to be under law , do you not hear the Law ?
48004022	For it is written that Abraham had two sons , one born of the slave girl and one born of the free wife .
48004023	But he who was born of the slave girl was born according to the flesh , while he who was born of the free wife was born by promise .
48004024	This is an allegory . For these women are the two covenants , one from Mount Sinai , bearing children for slavery . This is Hagar .
48004025	Hagar is Mount Sinai in Arabia . She represents the present Jerusalem , for she is in slavery along with her children .
48004026	But the Jerusalem on high is free and she is our mother .
48004027	For it is written , " Rejoice , O barren one , you who do not bear ! Break forth and shout , you who feel no birth pangs ! For many are the children of the desolate â more than those of her who has a husband . "
48004028	But you , brethren , are , as Isaac was , children of promise .
48004029	But just as then he who was born according to the flesh persecuted him who was born according to the Spirit , so it is now .
48004030	But what says the Scripture ? " Cast out the slave girl and her son . For the son of the slave girl shall not inherit along with the son of the free wife . "
48004031	Therefore , brethren , we are not children of a slave girl , but of the free wife .
48005001	STAND firm , therefore , in the freedom with which Christ set us free , and do not wear any yoke of slavery .
48005002	See , I , Paul , tell you that if you receive circumcision , Christ will be of no use to you .
48005003	I testify again to every man who receives circumcision that he is under obligation to carry out the whole Law .
48005004	You have put an end to Christ's work for you , you who are declared righteous by law ; you have fallen away from grace .
48005005	For we in the Spirit because of faith are waiting for the hope of righteousness .
48005006	For in Christ Jesus neither has circumcision any value nor uncircumcision , but faith working through love .
48005007	You were running finely . Who hindered you from obeying the truth ?
48005008	The persuasion was not from him who called you .
48005009	A little yeast sets the whole lump fermenting .
48005010	I am persuaded in regard to you in the Lord that you will have no other mind . He who is troubling you must bear his condemnation , whoever he may be .
48005011	But I , brethren , if I am still proclaiming circumcision , why am I persecuted ? Then the offensiveness of the cross has been done away .
48005012	Would that those who are troubling you would even cut off all !
48005013	For you were called to freedom , brethren ; only do not let your freedom be an opportunity for the flesh , but in love be servants to one another .
48005014	For the whole Law is summed up in one word : " You shall love your neighbor as yourself . "
48005015	But if you bite and devour one another , take care that you are not destroyed by one another .
48005016	I say , walk in the Spirit and you will not carry out the passions of the flesh .
48005017	For the flesh has passions contrary to the Spirit and the Spirit contrary to the flesh , for these are opposed to each other , so that you may not do whatever you wish .
48005018	But if you are led by the Spirit you are not under law .
48005019	The works of the flesh are obvious , such as unchastity , impurity , indecency ,
48005020	idolatry , magic , hatred , strife , jealousy , anger , rivalries , dissensions , factions ,
48005021	envyings , drinking bouts , revelries , and the like . Of these I tell you beforehand , as I have already told you , that those who practice such things will not inherit the kingdom of God .
48005022	But the fruit of the Spirit is love , joy , peace , slowness to anger , kindness , benevolence , faithfulness ,
48005023	gentleness , self-control ; against such there is no law .
48005024	Those who belong to Christ Jesus have crucified the flesh with its emotions and passions .
48005025	If we are living in the Spirit let us direct our lives by the Spirit .
48005026	Let us not be vainglorious , irritating one another , envying one another .
48006001	BRETHREN , if a man is surprised in some sin , you who are spiritual are to restore such a one in a spirit of gentleness , each looking out for himself to avoid being tempted .
48006002	Bear one another's burdens and so fulfill the law of Christ .
48006003	If any one thinks that he is something when he is nothing , he deceives himself .
48006004	Let each one test his own work and then he will have his reason for boasting in himself alone and not in another .
48006005	For each must bear his own load .
48006006	Let him who is taught the message share with his teacher in all good things .
48006007	Do not be deceived ; God is not mocked ; what a man sows that he will also reap .
48006008	For he who sows to his own flesh will from the flesh reap decay ; but he who sows to the Spirit will from the Spirit reap life eternal .
48006009	Let us not grow discouraged in doing what is noble , for in due time we shall reap if we do not grow faint .
48006010	So then as we have opportunity let us work for the good of all men , and especially of those who belong to the household of the faith .
48006011	See with what great letters I write with my own hand .
48006012	All who wish to make a fair show in the flesh are trying to compel you to receive circumcision , but only that they may not be persecuted for the cross of Christ .
48006013	For even those who are circumcised do not themselves keep the Law , but they wish you to be circumcised in order to boast in your flesh .
48006014	But let me never boast except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ , by which the world is crucified to me and I to the world .
48006015	For neither is circumcision anything nor uncircumcision , but a new creation .
48006016	All who walk by this rule â may peace and mercy be on them , and on the Israel of God !
48006017	For the future let no one trouble me ; for I bear on my body the brands of Jesus .
48006018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirits , brethren . Amen .
49001001	PAUL , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , to the Holy who are at Ephesus , faithful in Christ Jesus :
49001002	Grace and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ !
49001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , who has blessed us with every spiritual blessing in the heavenly heights in Christ ,

49001010	for the government of the fullness of the ages , to bring to unity all things in Christ , both things in the heavens and things on the earth .
49001011	In him we were predestined according to the plan of him who works in all things according to the purpose of his will ,

49001020	which he put forth in Christ when he raised him from the dead and made him sit at his own right hand in the heavenly heights ,

49001023	which is his body , the fullness of him who fills all in all .
49002001	YOU also God raised to life when you were dead in misdeeds and sins
49002002	in which you once walked , following the ways of this age of the world , led by the Ruler of the power of the air , the spirit who now works in the sons of disobedience .
49002003	Among these we all lived once in the passions of our flesh and of our thoughts , and we were by nature children of wrath like the rest .
49002004	But God , who is rich in mercy , because of his great love with which he loved us ,
49002005	even when we were dead in misdeeds , made us alive along with Christ â by grace we have been saved â
49002006	and raised us up with him and made us sit with him in the heavenly heights in Christ Jesus ,
49002007	that he might show in the ages to come the surpassing richness of his grace in his kindness to us in Christ Jesus .
49002008	For by grace you have been saved through faith , and that not of yourselves ; it is the gift of God ,
49002009	not of works , that no one may boast .
49002010	For we are his work , formed in Christ Jesus for good works in which God had prepared beforehand to have us live .
49002011	Therefore remember that once you were Gentiles in the flesh and were called uncircumcision by the so-called circumcision in the flesh , made by hands ,
49002012	and that you were then apart from Christ , aliens from the commonwealth of Israel and strangers to the covenants of promise , without hope and without God in the world .
49002013	But now in Christ Jesus you who once were far have become near by the blood of Christ .
49002014	For he is our peace . He has made both Jew and Gentile one and has broken down the dividing wall , the enmity .
49002015	In his own flesh he has ended the force of the law of commandments in ordinances in order to make the two , in himself , into one new man , thus making peace ,
49002016	and in order to reconcile both in one body to God through his cross , by slaying the enmity by it .
49002017	And he came and brought the good news of peace to you who were far and peace to those who were near .
49002018	For through him we , both Jews and Gentiles , have access through one Spirit to the Father .
49002019	So then you are no longer strangers and resident aliens , but fellow citizens with the holy and members of the household of God ,
49002020	built on the foundation of the apostles and prophets , Jesus Christ himself being the corner stone .
49002021	In him all the building , framed together , is growing into a holy temple in the Lord ,
49002022	in whom you also are being built for a dwelling of God in the Spirit .
49003001	FOR this reason I , Paul , the prisoner of Christ Jesus for the sake of you Gentiles , â
49003002	if you have heard of the gracious commission which God has given me to you ,
49003003	that by revelation the mystery has been disclosed to me , as I wrote before briefly ,
49003004	In reading that letter you can learn my understanding in the mystery of Christ ,
49003005	a mystery which was not disclosed in other generations to the sons of men as it has now been revealed to his holy apostles and prophets by the Spirit ,
49003006	namely , that the Gentiles are fellow heirs and fellow members of the body , fellow sharers of the promise in Christ Jesus through the good news ,
49003007	of which I became a servant according to the free grace of God which was given me by the inworking of his power .
49003008	To me , the least of all the holy , has this grace been given , to proclaim to the Gentiles the good news of the unsearchable riches of Christ
49003009	and to show what is the working of the mystery which has been hidden for ages in God , who created all things
49003010	in order to disclose now to the archangels and powers in the heavenly heights , through the church , the varied wisdom of God ,
49003011	according to the eternal purpose which he has accomplished by Christ Jesus our Lord ,
49003012	in whom we have boldness and confident access through faith in him .
49003013	So I beg you not to lose heart because of the distresses that come on me for your sake . They are a high honor to you .
49003014	For this reason I bow my knees to the Father
49003015	from whom every family in heaven and on earth is named ,
49003016	that he may grant to you according to his glorious wealth to be strengthened with might through his Spirit in the inner man ,
49003017	that Christ may dwell in your hearts through faith , and that you , rooted and founded in love ,
49003018	may be able with all the holy to comprehend what is the breadth and length and height and depth â
49003019	yes , to know the love of Christ , which yet surpasses knowledge , and may be filled with all the fullness of God .
49003020	To him who is able to do far beyond all we ask or think by the power that works in us ,
49003021	to him be glory in the church and in Christ Jesus through all the generations of the ages ! Amen .
49004001	I , THE prisoner of the Lord , beg you , then , to live worthily of the calling with which you have been called ,
49004002	with all modesty and gentleness , being slow to anger , bearing with one another in love ,
49004003	earnest in keeping the unity of the Spirit in the bond of peace .
49004004	There is one body and one Spirit , just as you were called with one hope that belongs to your calling ,
49004005	one Lord , one faith , one baptism ,
49004006	one God and Father of all , who is over all and through all and in all .
49004007	To each one of us grace was given according to the measure of the gift of Christ .
49004008	Therefore it says , " He ascended on high ; he led away captives ; he gave gifts to men . "
49004009	What does " he ascended " mean , except that he had descended into the lowest parts of the earth ?
49004010	He who descended is also he who " ascended " high above all the heavens to fill all things .
49004011	And he " gave " to some to be apostles , some prophets , some tellers of the good news , some shepherds and teachers ,
49004012	for the equipment of the saints , for the work of service , for building up the body of Christ ,
49004013	until we all attain oneness in the faith and the knowledge of the Son of God , and the maturity of manhood and the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ .
49004014	Then we shall be no longer children tossed and borne about by every wind of teaching through the trickery of men and craftiness in the devices of deceit ,
49004015	but speaking the truth in love we shall grow wholly into him who is the head , Christ ,
49004016	from whom the whole body framed together and strengthened by what every joint supplies vigorously , in the measure of each , makes growth in building itself up in love .
49004017	This then I say and solemnly protest in the Lord : that you are no longer to live as the Gentiles live in vacancy of mind ,
49004018	having their understanding darkened , aliens from the life of God because of the ignorance that is in them , and because of the hardness of their hearts .
49004019	Lost to any sense of shame they have abandoned themselves to sensuality for the practice of every kind of impurity with greediness .
49004020	But you have not so learned Christ ,
49004021	if you have heard him and have been taught in him as the truth is in Jesus ,
49004022	that you should put away the old man who belonged to your former way of life and was perishing in deluding passions ,
49004023	and that you should be made new in the spirit of your minds
49004024	and put on the new man formed as God approves in the righteousness and holiness of truth .
49004025	Therefore put aside lying and speak truth every one to his neighbor , for we are members one of another .
49004026	" Be angry and do not sin . " Do not let the sun go down on your wrath ,
49004027	neither give place for the Devil .
49004028	He who steals must steal no longer , but rather he must labor , working with his own hands something good , so as to have something to share with any one in need .
49004029	Let no vile word come out of your mouth , but , if anything , a good word for needed upbuilding of character to give grace to those who hear .
49004030	Do not grieve the Holy Spirit of God by whom you have been sealed for the day of redemption .
49004031	Let all bitterness and anger and wrath and clamor and abusive language be put away from you with every kind of malice .
49004032	Be kind to one another , sympathetic , forgiving one another just as God in Christ has forgiven you .
49005001	BE imitators of God as beloved children
49005002	and live in love , as Christ loved us and gave himself for us , an offering and sacrifice to God yielding a fragrant odor .
49005003	Unchastity or any kind of impurity or greediness must not be mentioned among you , as befits holy people ;
49005004	nor should there be indecent and foolish talk or jesting , which are unbecoming , but rather thanksgiving .
49005005	For you know well that no unchaste or impure person , no greedy person â who is an idolater â has any inheritance in the kingdom of Christ and God .
49005006	Let no one deceive you with empty words ; for because of these things the wrath of God comes on the sons of disobedience .
49005007	Do not , then , be partakers with them .
49005008	For you were once darkness , but now you are light in the Lord . Live like children of light â
49005009	for the fruit of light appears in all generosity and righteousness and truth â
49005010	testing what is pleasing to the Lord ,
49005011	and have no fellowship with the unfruitful works of darkness , but rather reprove them ,
49005012	for the things that they do in secret it is shameful even to speak of .
49005013	But all things when reproved are shown truly by the light , for everything shown truly is light .
49005014	Therefore it says , " Wake , O sleeper , and rise from the dead and Christ will give you light . "
49005015	Be strictly careful , then , how you live , not as unwise but as wise .
49005016	Buy up the opportunity , because these are evil days .
49005017	Therefore do not be thoughtless , but understand what is the Lord's will .
49005018	Do not be drunk with wine , in which there is profligacy , but be full of the Spirit ,
49005019	speaking to one another in psalms and hymns and spiritual songs , singing and playing the harp heartily to the Lord ,
49005020	giving thanks always for all things in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ to God the Father .
49005021	Be subject to one another in reverence for Christ ,
49005022	wives to their own husbands as in the Lord ,
49005023	because a man is the head of his wife as Christ is the head of the church and he is the savior of the body .
49005024	But as the church is subject to Christ , so wives are to their husbands in everything .
49005025	Husbands , love your wives , as Christ also loved the church and gave himself for it ,
49005026	that he might make it holy , cleansing it by the washing with water according to his word ,
49005027	that he might present to himself the church glorious , without spot or wrinkle or any such thing , but holy and faultless .
49005028	Thus ought men to love their own wives as their own bodies . He who loves his own wife loves himself ,
49005029	for no one ever hates his own flesh , but nourishes and cherishes it , just as Christ does the church ,
49005030	for we are members of his body .
49005031	" Therefore shall a man leave his father and his mother and shall cleave to his wife and the two shall become one flesh .
49005032	" This mystery is great , but I am speaking of Christ and the church .
49005033	But each one of you must love his own wife as himself , and the wife must reverence her husband .
49006001	CHILDREN , obey your parents in the Lord , for this is right .
49006002	" Honor your father and your mother . " This is the first commandment with a promise ,
49006003	" That it may go well with you and you may be long-lived in the land . "
49006004	And you , fathers , do not irritate your children , but bring them up in the education and admonition of the Lord .
49006005	Slaves , obey those who according to the flesh are your masters , with reverence and awe in singleness of your hearts as to Christ ,
49006006	not with eye service as pleasers of men , but as Christ's slaves , doing the will of God in a whole-souled way ,
49006007	giving service with cheerfulness as to the Lord and not to men ,

49006011	Put on the complete armor of God so that you may be able to stand against the cunning arts of the Devil .

49006013	Therefore take the complete armor of God , that you may be able to withstand in the evil day and , after going through everything , to stand .

49006020	for which I am an ambassador in chains , that I may tell it fearlessly as I ought .

49006022	whom I am sending to you for this very purpose , will tell you everything , so that you may know the news of me and he may encourage your hearts .

50001001	PAUL and Timothy , servants of Christ Jesus , to all the Holy in Christ Jesus who are in Philippi , with Bishops and Deacons :
