50001008	For God is my witness how much I long for you all in the affections of Christ Jesus .
50001009	And this is my prayer that your love may abound more and more in knowledge and all insight ,
50001010	so that you may discriminate between the things that differ , that you may be pure and blameless in the day of Christ ,
50001011	filled with the fruit of knowledge through Jesus Christ to the glory and praise of God .
50001012	I wish you to know , brethren , that my affairs have turned out rather to the furtherance of the good news ,
50001013	so that my chains have become well known as for Christ to the whole Praetorian Guard and to all the rest ,
50001014	and the most of the brethren in the Lord , made confident by my chains , are unusually brave in speaking the message fearlessly .
50001015	Some indeed proclaim Christ because of envy and rivalry , some also because of good will .
50001016	Some announce Christ from love , knowing that I am placed for the defense of the good news ,
50001017	but others out of partisanship , thinking to add distress to my chains .
50001018	What then ? Still in every way , whether in pretense or in truth , Christ is proclaimed and in that I rejoice , yes , and will rejoice .
50001019	For I know that this will make for my salvation through your prayer and the supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ ,
50001020	according to my earnest expectation and hope that I may be put to shame in nothing , but with all courage , as always , so now Christ may be honored in my body , whether by my life or by my death .
50001021	For to me to live is Christ and to die is gain .
50001022	If it is to be life in the flesh , that means fruitful work for me . I know not which to choose .
50001023	I am under pressure both ways , having the desire to depart and be with Christ , for it is far better ,
50001024	yet that I should stay in the flesh is more needful on your account .
50001025	And this I confidently know , that I shall stay and stay near you all for your advancement and joy of faith ,
50001026	that your exultation in Christ Jesus may overflow on my account , because of my presence again with you .
50001027	Only exercise your citizenship in a manner worthy of the good news of Christ , so that , whether I come and see you or in absence hear news of you , I may know that you are standing in one spirit , with one mind wrestling in the faith of the good news
50001028	and not frightened in anything by your adversaries , which for them is a sign of ruin , but for you of salvation , and that from God ;
50001029	because it has been graciously allowed you not only to believe in Christ but also to suffer for his sake ,
50001030	and you have the same struggle that you saw in me and now hear of in me .
50002001	IF there is any encouragement in Christ , any persuasive power in love , any fellowship in the Spirit , any sympathies and compassions ,
50002002	fill up my joy by having the same love , being of the same mind , thinking the same thing ,
50002003	doing nothing in a partisan or vainglorious way , but each modestly regarding the others as of more account than himself .
50002004	Do not be each intent on his own interests , but also on the interests of others .
50002005	Let this mind be in you which was also in Christ Jesus ,
50002006	who , though he was in the form of God , did not think that equality with God was something to be grasped ,
50002007	but emptied himself , taking the form of a servant and coming into the likeness of men ,
50002008	and when found in the condition of a man he humbled himself by becoming obedient even to death â death on the cross .
50002009	Therefore , God has highly exalted him and has graciously given him the name which is above every name ,
50002010	that at the name of Jesus every knee may bow , of beings in heaven and those on earth and those under the earth ,
50002011	and every tongue confess that Jesus Christ is Lord , to the glory of God the Father .
50002012	So then , my beloved , as you have always obeyed , not in my presence only , but now much more in my absence , work out your own salvation with reverence and awe .
50002013	For it is God who is working in you both the willing and the doing because of his kindness .
50002014	Do everything without murmurings or disputings
50002015	that you may be blameless and pure , children of God , spotless in the midst of a crooked and perverse generation among whom you shine as lights in the world ,
50002016	holding forth the message of life , so that on the day of Christ I can boast that I did not run in vain or labor in vain .
50002017	But if I am poured out as a libation on your sacrificial offering of faith , I rejoice and share the joy of you all .
50002018	In the same way you must rejoice and share my joy .
50002019	But I hope in the Lord Jesus to send Timothy to you soon , that I may be cheered by knowing about you .
50002020	For I have no one likeminded with him who will so sincerely care for your interests .
50002021	For all pursue their own aims , not those of Christ Jesus .
50002022	But you know how he has been tested and how like a child with a father he has served with me in spreading the good news .
50002023	So I hope to send him at once when I see how my affairs are going .
50002024	And I trust in the Lord that I myself shall come quickly .
50002025	I think it necessary to send to you Epaphroditus , my brother and fellow worker and fellow soldier , and your messenger and minister to my needs ,
50002026	since he longs for you all and is troubled because you have heard that he was sick .
50002027	Indeed he was sick and near to death . But God had mercy on him , and not on him alone , but also on me , that I might not have sorrow upon sorrow .
50002028	I send him the more readily that you may see him and rejoice again and I be less sorrowful .
50002029	Receive him in the Lord with all joy and hold such men in honor ,
50002030	because for the work of Christ he was near to death , hazarding his life to complete the service you were not here to do for me .
50003001	TO conclude , my brethren : rejoice in the Lord . To repeat to you the same things is not tiresome to me and it is safe for you .
50003002	Beware of the dogs , beware of the bad workmen , beware of the excision .
50003003	For we are the circumcision , we who worship in the Spirit of God and exult in Christ Jesus , and have no confidence in the flesh ,
50003004	though I have ground for confidence even in the flesh . If any other man thinks that he has ground for confidence in the flesh , I have more â
50003005	circumcised the eighth day , of the race of Israel , of the tribe of Benjamin , a Hebrew of Hebrews , as to the Law a Pharisee ,
50003006	as to zeal persecuting the church , as to the righteousness of the Law blameless .
50003007	But the things that were gain to me , those I have counted loss for Christ .
50003008	Yes , I count all to be loss because of the surpassing worth of the knowledge of Christ Jesus my Lord , for whom I have suffered the loss of all things and count them but refuse , that I may gain Christ
50003009	and be found in him , not having my own righteousness that was from the Law , but that which is through faith in Christ , the righteousness which comes from God and rests on faith ,
50003010	that I may know him and the power of his resurrection and the fellowship of his sufferings , becoming like him in death ,
50003011	if possibly I may attain to the resurrection from the dead .
50003012	Not that I have already obtained it or have already been made perfect , but I press on to lay hold of that for which I was laid hold of by Christ Jesus .
50003013	Brethren , I do not consider myself yet to have laid hold of it . But one thing I do : forgetting what is behind and stretching forward to what is in front
50003014	I press toward the goal for the prize of the heavenly call of God in Christ Jesus .
50003015	Let us all who are full grown think in this way . If in anything you think differently , even that God will reveal to you ,
50003016	but so far as we have attained let us walk in the same path .
50003017	Unite in imitating me , brethren , and watch those who are living according to our example .
50003018	For many are living as I used often to tell you and now say even weeping that they are enemies of the cross of Christ .
50003019	Their end is ruin , their God is their stomach , their glory is in their shame , they think earthly thoughts .
50003020	For the state of which we are citizens is in the heavens and from there we are expecting a Savior , the Lord Jesus Christ .
50003021	He will transform the body we have in our low estate into the likeness of the body he has in glory by the power by which he can subject all things to himself .
50004001	SO , my brethren beloved and longed for , my joy and crown , stand firm thus in the Lord , beloved .
50004002	I beg Euodia and I beg Syntyche to be of the same mind in the Lord .
50004003	Yes , I ask you , true yokefellow , help them , since they struggled in spreading the good news along with me and Clement and the rest of my fellow workers whose names are in the book of life .
50004004	Rejoice in the Lord always . Again I say rejoice .
50004005	Let your fairness be known to all men . The Lord is near .
50004006	Do not worry , but in everything by prayer and entreaty with thanksgiving let your requests be made known to God .
50004007	And the peace of God which passes all understanding will guard your hearts and your thoughts in Christ Jesus .
50004008	To conclude , brethren , whatever is true , whatever is dignified , whatever is just , whatever is pure , whatever is lovable , whatever is highly spoken of â if there is any virtue or any praise â think of that .
50004009	What you learned and accepted and heard and saw in me â practice that . And the God of peace will be with you .
50004010	I rejoiced in the Lord greatly that now at length your thoughtfulness for me had revived . You were thoughtful for me all along , but lacked opportunity .
50004011	Not that I am speaking because of want ; for I have learned how to be content in whatever circumstances I am .
50004012	I know how to live humbly and I know how to enjoy abundance . In each and every situation I have been initiated into the secret both of being well fed and of going hungry , both of having abundance and of bearing want .
50004013	I can do all things through him who gives me strength .
50004014	Yet you did nobly in sharing with me in my distress .
50004015	You Philippians know that at the beginning of the good news , when I came away from Macedonia , no church shared with me in the matter of giving and receiving except you only ,
50004016	and that in Thessalonica you sent once , yes , twice , for my need .
50004017	Not that I am seeking for the gift , but I am seeking for the fruit that increases to your credit .
50004018	I have enough of everything and more than enough . I am fully supplied since receiving from Epaphroditus the things from you , a fragrant odor , an acceptable sacrifice , pleasing to God .
50004019	My God will supply every need of yours according to his wealth in glory in Christ Jesus .
50004020	To God our Father be glory for the ages of the ages ! Amen .
50004021	Greet every holy one in Christ Jesus . The brethren with me send greetings to you .
50004022	All the holy send greetings to you , especially those of Caesar's household .
50004023	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirits !
51001001	PAUL , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and Timothy our brother ,
51001002	to the holy and faithful brethren in Christ in Colossae : Grace be to you and peace from God our Father !
51001003	We always thank God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , in praying for you ,
51001004	because we have heard of your faith in Christ Jesus and the love that you have to all the holy
51001005	because of the hope laid up for us in heaven . Of this you have already heard in the true message of the good news
51001006	which has come to you . Just as in all the world it is bearing fruit and growing , so also it is among you since the day that you heard and learned of the grace of God in truth .
51001007	So you learned it from Epaphras , our beloved fellow servant , who is a faithful servant of Christ in your behalf ,
51001008	and who has told us of your love in the Spirit .
51001009	For this reason we also , from the day we heard it , never cease praying for you and asking that you may have full knowledge of his will in all wisdom and spiritual insight ,
51001010	and that you may live lives worthy of the Lord and please him in every way . May you bear fruit in every good work and grow in the knowledge of God .
51001011	May you be strengthened with all strength according to his glorious power , so as to have all patience and endurance .
51001012	May you joyfully give thanks to the Father who has made you fit to share in the inheritance of the holy in light .
51001013	He has saved us from the power of darkness and transferred us into the kingdom of his beloved Son ,
51001014	in whom we have redemption , the forgiveness of our sins .
51001015	He is the image of the invisible God , the first born of all creation ;
51001016	for in him were created all things in heaven and on earth , both visible and invisible , whether thrones or lordships or archangels or powers â all things have been created through him and for him ,
51001017	and he is before all things and in him all things unite .
51001018	And he is the head of the body , the church . He is the beginning , the firstborn from the dead , that he may be first in all things ,
51001019	because it pleased God to have all his fullness dwell in him
51001020	and to reconcile all things to himself through him , making peace through the blood of his cross â all things , I say , whether on earth or in heaven .
51001021	And you who were once alienated and enemies in your minds , living in wicked works , he has reconciled
51001022	by his body of flesh through death , to present you holy and spotless and blameless before him ,
51001023	if you remain in the faith , firm and steadfast , never moving from the hope of the good news which you have heard and which has been proclaimed in all the creation under heaven , and of which I , Paul , became a servant .
51001024	Now I rejoice in what I suffer for your sake , and in my turn am filling up in my flesh what was lacking in the afflictions of Christ for the sake of his body , that is , the church .
51001025	I became a servant of the church according to the commission from God given to me for you , to deliver fully God's message ,
51001026	the mystery hidden for ages and generations but now made plain to his holy ones ,
51001027	to whom God willed to make known what is the glorious wealth of this mystery among the Gentiles , which is Christ in you the hope of glory .
51001028	And we are announcing him , warning every man and teaching every man in all wisdom in order that we may present every man complete in Christ .
51001029	For this also I labor , wrestling with the energy of him who works powerfully within me .
51002001	FOR I wish you to know how I am wrestling for you and for those in Laodicea and for all who have not seen my face in the flesh ,
51002002	that your hearts may be encouraged and that joined together in love you may reach all the wealth of the full assurance of insight into the knowledge of the mystery of God , which is Christ .
51002003	In him all the treasures of wisdom and knowledge lie hidden .
51002004	I say this that no one may deceive you by plausible arguments .
51002005	For even though I am absent in the flesh , yet in the spirit I am with you , rejoicing to see your good order and the firmness of your faith in Christ .
51002006	Since , then , you have received Christ Jesus as Lord , live in him ,
51002007	rooted and built up in him , growing strong in the faith as you have been taught , and overflowing with thanksgiving .
51002008	Beware that no one carries you away captive by his philosophy and empty deceit according to the tradition of men , according to the elementary teachings of the world and not according to Christ .
51002009	For in him dwells all the fullness of God in bodily form ,
51002010	and you have been filled in him . He is the head of every archangel and authority .
51002011	In him you were circumcised with a circumcision not done by hands , by laying aside your fleshly body in the circumcision of Christ .
51002012	You were buried with him in baptism and raised again through faith in the inworking of God who raised him from the dead .
51002013	You who were dead in your sins and in the uncircumcision of your flesh God has made alive with him , and has forgiven us all our sins .
51002014	He erased the writing that was against us in the rules , the writing that was opposed to us . He has taken it out of the way by nailing it to his cross .
51002015	He despoiled the archangels and authorities and fearlessly made an example of them when he triumphed over them on the cross .
51002016	Let no one then judge you in the matter of food or drink or in regard to a festival or new moon or Sabbath .
51002017	These were a shadow of coming things , but the body is Christ's .
51002018	Let no one as umpire defraud you of your prize , if he delights in excessive humility and ceremonial worship of the angels , searching into his own visions , emptily puffed up by his fleshly mind
51002019	and not holding to the Head , from whom the whole body , supplied and held together by joints and bands , grows as God gives it growth .
51002020	If you died with Christ to the elementary teachings of the world , why do you , as if still living in the world , have such rules as ,
51002021	" Do not touch , " " Do not taste , " " Do not handle "
51002022	referring to things that perish when used ?
51002023	These rules follow the commandments and teachings of men . They have an appearance of wisdom in self-imposed ceremonial and excessive humility and severity to the body , but have no value against the indulgence of the flesh .
51003001	IF then you have been raised with Christ , seek the things above , where Christ is sitting at the right hand of God .
51003002	Have your minds on the things above and not on the things on the earth .
51003003	For you have died and your life is hidden with Christ in God .
51003004	When Christ , our life , appears , then you also will appear with him in glory .
51003005	Treat the members of your earthly bodies as dead â dead to unchastity , impurity , passion , evil desire , and avarice , which is idolatry .
51003006	On account of these things comes the wrath of God .
51003007	To them you also were once habituated when you lived in them .
51003008	But now you also must put away all wrath , anger , malice , abusive language . Vile talk must not be in your mouths .
51003009	Do not lie to one another . You have stripped off the old self with his practices
51003010	and have clothed yourselves with the new self , which is being renewed into knowledge in the image of its Creator .
51003011	Here there is no Greek or Jew , circumcision or uncircumcision , barbarian , Scythian , slave or freeman , but Christ is all and in all .
51003012	Put on , then , as the chosen of God , holy and beloved , sympathies , compassions , kindness , humility , gentleness , slowness to anger ,
51003013	bearing with one another and forgiving one another , if any one has a grievance against any . Just as the Lord forgave you , so must you forgive .
51003014	Above all these , clothe yourselves with love , which is the perfect bond of union .
51003015	Let the peace of Christ be umpire in your hearts . For this you were called into one body . And be thankful .
51003016	The message of Christ must dwell in you richly , as you teach in all wisdom and admonish one another with psalms and hymns and spiritual songs and sing with grace in your hearts to God .
51003017	And whatever you do in word or deed , do all in the name of the Lord Jesus , giving thanks to God the Father through him .
51003018	Wives , be in subjection to your husbands , as is fitting in the Lord .
51003019	Husbands , love your wives and do not be harsh toward them .
51003020	Children , obey your parents in everything , for this is pleasing in the Lord .
51003021	Fathers , do not irritate your children , for they may lose heart .
51003022	Slaves , obey in everything your masters in the flesh , not with eye-service as men-pleasers , but in sincerity of heart , because you reverence the Lord .
51003023	Whatever you do , do it heartily as for the Lord and not for men ,
51003024	for you know that from the Lord you will receive the reward of the inheritance . You are slaves to the Lord Christ .
51003025	He who does wrong will be repaid for the wrong he has done , and there is no partiality .
51004001	MASTERS , give to your slaves what is just and equal , for you know that you have a Master in heaven .
51004002	Be earnest and constant in prayer . Be thankfully watchful in it .
51004003	Pray along with us and for us that God may open for us a door for the message , so that I may tell the mystery of Christ for the sake of which I am in chains â
51004004	so that I may make it clear , as I ought .
51004005	Behave wisely towards outsiders , buying up the opportunity .
51004006	Let what you say be always with grace , seasoned with salt . Know how you should answer each one .

51004008	I am sending him to you for this very purpose , that you may know my situation and that he may encourage your hearts .

52001001	PAUL and Silvanus and Timothy , to the Church of the Thessalonians in God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ : Grace to you and peace .
52001002	We thank God always for you all when we mention you in our prayers ,
52001003	unceasingly remembering your work of faith and labor of love and patience of hope in our Lord Jesus Christ before God our Father .
52001004	We know , brethren beloved by God , that he has chosen you
52001005	and that our good news came to you not in word only but in power and in the Holy Spirit and in great assurance , just as you know we acted among you for your benefit .
52001006	You became imitators of us and of the Lord , receiving the message in great affliction with joy which the Holy Spirit gave ,
52001007	so that you became a pattern for all believers in Macedonia and in Achaia .
52001008	For the message of the Lord sounded forth from you not only in Macedonia and Achaia , but in every place your faith toward God has gone abroad , so that there is no need for us to speak a word .
52001009	For the people themselves are telling about us , what a reception we had with you , and how you turned to God from idols , to serve the living and true God

52002001	YOU yourselves know , brethren , what a reception we had from you , that it was not without result ,
52002002	but after we had suffered and been roughly treated , as you know , in Philippi , we made bold in our God to speak to you the good news of God with great wrestling .
52002003	For our appeal springs not from deception , nor from impure motives , nor from cunning ,
52002004	but as we have been approved by God to be entrusted with the good news , so we speak , not as if we were pleasing men , but God , who tests our hearts .
52002005	Nor did we ever fall into flattering talk , as you know , nor use any pretext for self-enrichment â God is witness â
52002006	nor did we seek glory from men , either from you or others , although we could have claimed the dignity of Christ's apostles .
52002007	But we became gentle in the midst of you like a nursing mother cherishing her own children .
52002008	Yearning over you so , we would gladly have imparted to you not only God's good news but our own lives as well , because you had become dear to us .
52002009	For you remember , brethren , our toil and labor as we worked night and day so as not to burden any one of you while we proclaimed to you the good news of God .
52002010	You are witnesses â and God is witness â how purely and justly and blamelessly we acted toward you who believe .
52002011	You know that just like a father toward his own children we encouraged each one of you , and warned and conjured you
52002012	to live lives worthy of the God who is calling you into his own kingdom and glory .
52002013	For this reason we unceasingly give thanks to God that when you received from us the report of the message of God you accepted it not as the message of men , but , as it truly is , the message of God , which also is doing its work in you who believe .
52002014	For you became imitators , brethren , of the churches of God that are in Judaea in Christ Jesus , because you too suffered the same things from your fellow countrymen that they did from the Jews ,
52002015	who killed both the Lord Jesus and the prophets , and drove us out and do not please God and are enemies to all men ,
52002016	trying to prevent us from speaking to the Gentiles so that they may be saved . All this goes always to fill up the measure of their sins . But God's fiercest wrath has overtaken them .
52002017	But we , brethren , when bereft of you for a little while , out of sight not out of mind , endeavored more earnestly to see your faces , with great longing .
52002018	For that reason we determined to come to you , yes , I , Paul , more than once : but Satan hindered us .
52002019	For what is our hope or joy or crown to boast of before our Lord Jesus at his coming ? Is it not you ?
52002020	You are our glory and joy .
52003001	SO when we could no longer endure the anxiety , we chose to be left at Athens alone
52003002	and sent Timothy , our brother and God's servant in the good news of Christ , to strengthen and encourage you in your faith ,
52003003	that no one might be disturbed in these trials . For you yourselves know that we are destined to this .
52003004	For when we were with you we told you in advance , " We shall soon have trouble . " And so it came to pass , as you know .
52003005	Therefore , when I could no longer endure the anxiety , I sent to know about your faith for fear that the tempter had tempted you and our labor had gone for nothing .
52003006	But now that Timothy has come to us from you and has brought us good news of your faith and love , and that you always keep us well in mind and long to see us , just as we long to see you ,
52003007	we have been cheered , brethren , in regard to you , in all our straits and distresses by your faith .
52003008	Now we are living , since you are standing firm in the Lord .
52003009	For how can we be grateful enough to God for you in view of all the joy we have because of you ,
52003010	while we pray beyond measure night and day that we may see your faces and make good whatever lacks there may be in your faith ?
52003011	May our God and Father himself and our Lord Jesus Christ open the way for us to come to you .
52003012	The Lord make you to abound and overflow in love toward one another and toward all men , just as we do toward you ,
52003013	that your hearts may be made firm and you may be blameless in holiness before our God and Father at the coming of our Lord Jesus with all his holy ones .
52004001	TO conclude , brethren , we beg of you and urge you in the Lord Jesus that , as you learned from us how you ought to live to please God , and are living , you will excel still more .
52004002	For you know what directions we have given you through the Lord Jesus .
52004003	For this is the will of God : to have you become holy and have you shun unchastity ;
52004004	to have each of you know how to take a wife for himself in holiness and honor ,
52004005	not in the passion of lust , as the Gentiles do who know not God ;
52004006	to have no one trespass or take advantage of his brother in this matter ; for the Lord is the punisher of all such , as we have already told you and solemnly warned you .
52004007	God has not called us to live in impurity , but in holiness .
52004008	Therefore he who disregards this disregards not man , but God , who gives his Holy Spirit to you .
52004009	Regarding brotherly love you have no need for me to write to you . For you yourselves have been taught by God to love one another ,
52004010	and you do the same to all the brethren in the whole of Macedonia . But we urge you , brethren , to excel still further
52004011	and to be ambitious to lead a quiet life and to mind each his own business and to work with your hands , as we instructed you .
52004012	Thus you will live becomingly in the sight of outsiders and will have need of nothing .
52004013	We do not wish you to be ignorant , brethren , regarding those who are sleeping , that you may not sorrow as the rest of men who have no hope .
52004014	For since , as we believe , Jesus died and rose , so too God will through Jesus bring with him those who have fallen asleep .
52004015	This we tell you by the word of the Lord : We , the living , who have been left until the coming of the Lord , will not have the start of those who have fallen asleep .
52004016	For the Lord himself will descend from heaven with a shout , with the voice of an archangel and with God's trumpet-call , and first the dead in Christ will rise .
52004017	Then we , the living , who are left , will be caught up along with them into the clouds to meet the Lord in the air . And thus we shall forever be with the Lord .
52004018	So encourage one another with these words .
52005001	BUT regarding times and dates , brethren , you do not need to have me write to you .
52005002	For you yourselves know perfectly that the day of the Lord will come like a thief in the night .
52005003	When they are saying , " Peace and safety , " then sudden destruction is upon them , like the pangs upon a woman with child , and they will not escape .
52005004	But you , brethren , are not in darkness so that the day can take you like a thief .
52005005	You are all sons of light and sons of day . We do not belong to night or to darkness .
52005006	Then let us not be sleeping like the rest of men , but let us watch and be sober .
52005007	For those who sleep sleep in the night and those who drink drink in the night .
52005008	But let us who are of the day be sober . Let us put on the breastplate of faith and love and for a helmet the hope of salvation .
52005009	For God has not destined us to wrath , but to the winning of salvation through our Lord Jesus Christ ,
52005010	who died for us that whether we are waking or sleeping we may live in company with him .
52005011	Therefore encourage one another and build up one another , as indeed you are doing .
52005012	We beg you , brethren , to regard those who are laboring among you and who preside over you in the Lord and give you counsel ,
52005013	and to esteem them very highly in love on account of their work . Be at peace among yourselves .
52005014	We urge you , brethren , to warn the disorderly , encourage the faint-hearted , help the weak , be patient with all .
52005015	Take care that no one repays evil with evil , but always seek eagerly what is good in dealing with one another and with every one .
52005016	Always be joyful .
52005017	Pray without ceasing .
52005018	In everything give thanks , for this is God's will in Christ for you .
52005019	Do not quench the Spirit .
52005020	Do not despise prophecies .
52005021	Test all things ; hold fast the good .
52005022	Avoid every kind of evil .
52005023	May the God of peace himself make you completely holy , and may your spirits and souls and bodies be kept faultless and blameless for the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ .
52005024	He is faithful who calls you and he will do it .
52005025	Brethren , pray for us .
52005026	Greet all the brethren with a holy kiss .
52005027	I solemnly charge you in the Lord's name to have this letter read to all the brethren .
52005028	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you .
53001001	PAUL and Silvanus and Timothy to the Church of the Thessalonians in God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ :
53001002	Grace to you and peace from God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
53001003	We ought always to thank God for you , brethren , as is fitting , since your faith is growing greatly and the love of each and all of you toward one another is increasing ,
53001004	so that we ourselves glory in you among the churches of God because of your endurance and faith in all of your persecutions and in the distresses you are bearing .
53001005	This is a proof of God's righteous judgment . It is to make you worthy of God's kingdom , on behalf of which you are suffering ,
53001006	since it is just on God's part to repay with trouble those who are troubling you ,
53001007	and to repay to you , who are being troubled , rest with us at the revelation of the Lord Jesus from heaven with his mighty angels .
53001008	With flaming fire he will inflict vengeance on those who do not know God and do not obey the good news of our Lord Jesus .
53001009	They will suffer the penalty of eternal destruction and be sent away from the face of the Lord and from his glorious power ,
53001010	when he comes to be glorified among his holy ones and to be wondered at on that day among all believers â for our testimony to you was believed .
53001011	To this end we are always praying for you that our God will make you worthy of the call , and will by his power bring to completion every one of your kind purposes and works of faith ,
53001012	that the name of our Lord Jesus may be glorified in you , according to the grace of our God and of the Lord Jesus Christ .
53002001	WITH regard to the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ and our being gathered to meet him , I beg you , brethren ,
53002002	not to be quickly unsettled in mind nor excited by either a revelation or by a message or a letter supposed to be from us , to the effect that the day of the Lord is close at hand .
53002003	Let no one lead you astray in any way , because it will not come until the Apostasy has first come and the Man of Lawlessness has been revealed â the Son of Perdition ,
53002004	who opposes and exalts himself above everything called God and every object of worship , so that he enters the Temple of God and seats himself there , declaring that he himself is God .
53002005	Do you not remember that while I was still with you I used to tell you this ?
53002006	And now you know what is restraining him until he is revealed at his appointed time .
53002007	For the mystery of lawlessness is already working , only there is just now one who is restraining it until he passes out of the way .
53002008	And then the Lawless One will be revealed . But the Lord Jesus will sweep him away with the breath of his mouth and will make him powerless by the splendor of his coming .
53002009	For his coming will be when Satan is active in every sort of power and in false signs and wonders
53002010	and in every kind of wicked deception of those who are perishing , because they did not receive the love of the truth so that they might be saved .
53002011	For this reason God sends to them a deceptive influence so that they believe a lie ,
53002012	that all who have not believed the truth but have delighted in wickedness may be condemned .
53002013	We ought always to thank God for you , brethren , beloved by the Lord , because God chose you from the beginning for salvation through the Spirit's making you holy and your own faith in the truth .
53002014	To this he called you through the good news that we brought , so that you may share the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ .
53002015	Now then , brethren , stand firm and hold fast the teachings that you have been taught whether by our words or by our letter .
53002016	May our Lord Jesus Christ himself and God our Father , who loved us and gave us eternal encouragement and good hope through grace ,
53002017	encourage your hearts and make you strong in every good word and work .
53003001	IN conclusion , brethren , pray for us , that the Lord's message may run and be glorified , as among you ,
53003002	and that we may be saved from the unreasonable and wicked men , for faith does not belong to all .
53003003	But the Lord is faithful and he will strengthen you and guard you from evil .
53003004	We are persuaded in the Lord in regard to you that you are doing and will do what we direct .
53003005	The Lord guide your hearts in the love of God and the patience of Christ .
53003006	We charge you , brethren , in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ , to stand aloof from every brother who is living in a disorderly way and not according to the teaching that you received from us .
53003007	For you yourselves know that you should imitate us , for we were not disorderly when among you ,
53003008	nor did we eat bread with any one without paying , but with labor and toil night and day we worked in order not to burden any one of you .
53003009	Not that we have not the authority , but in order to give you ourselves as an example for you to imitate .
53003010	For when we were with you we gave you this command , " If any one will not work , neither is he to eat . "
53003011	For we hear that some among you are leading disorderly lives , busy about nothing and yet busybodies .
53003012	Such we command and urge in the Lord Jesus Christ to work quietly and eat their own bread .
53003013	But you , brethren , must not become discouraged in doing well .
53003014	If any one does not obey our words in this letter , mark that man and do not associate with him , so that he may be ashamed .
53003015	Yet do not regard him as an enemy , but warn him as a brother .
53003016	The Lord of peace himself give you peace at all times in all ways . The Lord be with you all .
53003017	The greeting of Paul by my own hand , which is the sign in every letter . This is my handwriting .
53003018	The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with all of you .
54001001	PAUL , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the appointment of God , our Savior , and Christ Jesus our hope ,
54001002	to Timothy my true child in faith : Grace , mercy and peace from God the Father and Christ Jesus our Lord .
54001003	As I begged you to stay in Ephesus when I was leaving for Macedonia , that you might charge some not to teach new and strange doctrines
54001004	nor give attention to myths and endless genealogies , which promote disputes rather than God's plan in the faith , so I beg you now .
54001005	The aim of the commandment is love out of a pure heart and a good conscience and a sincere faith .
54001006	Some missing these have turned aside to empty talk ,
54001007	wishing to be teachers of the Law , but not understanding either what they are saying or what the things are that they are so positive about .
54001008	We know that the Law is excellent , if any one uses it lawfully .
54001009	But we know this : that law is not laid down for a righteous man , but for the lawless and the insubordinate , the ungodly and sinners , the unholy and profane , for murderers of fathers and murderers of mothers , for manslayers ,
54001010	for the unchaste , for those who practice unnatural vices , for slave-dealers , liars , perjurers , and for whatever else is contrary to wholesome teaching
54001011	such as accords with the glorious good news of the blessed God , with which I have been entrusted .
54001012	I thank Christ Jesus our Lord who has given me strength , because he thought me faithful and put me into his service ,
54001013	though before that I spoke profanely and was a persecutor and insolent in outrages . But I received mercy because I did it ignorantly in unbelief .
54001014	And the grace of our Lord overflowed in me with faith and love in Christ Jesus .
54001015	The saying is trust-worthy and deserving of full acceptance that " Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners , " of whom I am the foremost .
54001016	But I received mercy for this reason , that in me , as the foremost , Jesus Christ might show all of his long-suffering for an example for those who are to believe in him and gain life eternal .
54001017	To the King of the ages , the immortal , invisible , only God , be honor and glory for the ages of the ages ! Amen .
54001018	This command I lay down for you , my child Timothy , in accordance with the prophecies that came in advance regarding you , in order that armed with them you may wage the noble war ,
54001019	holding to faith and a good conscience , which some have cast aside and thus made shipwreck of their faith .
54001020	Among these are Hymenaeus and Alexander , whom I have handed over to Satan , that they may learn not to speak profanely .
54002001	I BEG , then , first of all , that petitions , prayers , supplications , and thanksgivings be made in behalf of all men ,
54002002	in behalf of kings and all who are in authority , that we may lead a quiet and peaceful life in all piety and sobriety .
54002003	This is excellent and pleasing in the sight of God , our Savior ,
54002004	who wishes all men to be saved and to come to the knowledge of the truth .
54002005	For there is one God and one Mediator between God and men , himself man , Christ Jesus ,
54002006	who gave himself as a ransom for all , a fact to be witnessed to at the fitting time .
54002007	To this I was appointed a herald and an apostle â I am telling the truth , I am not lying â a teacher of Gentiles in faith and truth .
54002008	I wish , then , that the men offer prayer in every place , lifting up holy hands without wrath or debate .
54002009	Also that the women adorn themselves in becoming dress modestly and discreetly , not with braided hair or gold or pearls or costly clothes ,
54002010	but â as is becoming for women professing piety â with good deeds .
54002011	A woman is to learn in all subjection .
54002012	I do not permit a woman to teach or to usurp authority over a man , but she must remain silent .
54002013	Adam was first formed , then Eve .
54002014	And Adam was not deceived ; the woman was deceived and fell into sin .
54002015	But they will be saved through child-bearing , if they continue in faith and love and holiness with self-control .
54003001	THE saying is trustworthy : " If any one aspires to the office of a bishop , he desires a noble work . "
54003002	A bishop , then , should be above reproach , true to one woman , temperate , self-controlled , dignified , hospitable , with a gift for teaching ,
54003003	not given to wine or to blows , but fair-minded , averse to strife , not a lover of money ,
54003004	presiding well over his own house , with children obedient and respectful .
54003005	But if any one does not know how to preside over his own house , how will he take care of the church of God ?
54003006	He must not be a new convert , for fear he may be blinded by pride and fall into the condemnation of the Devil .
54003007	He must have a good reputation with outsiders so as not to fall into reproach and the snare of the Devil .
54003008	Deacons , in the same way , must be dignified , not double-tongued , not given to much wine , not eager for base gain ,
54003009	holding the mystery of the faith with a pure conscience .
54003010	They must first be tested , and then let them fill the office of deacon if there is nothing against them .
54003011	Women , in the same way , must be dignified , not slanderers , temperate , trustworthy in everything .
54003012	Deacons must be men true to one woman , presiding well over their children and their own houses .
54003013	Those who have filled the office of deacon well win for themselves a high standing and great boldness in the faith in Christ Jesus .
54003014	I am writing these things to you , although I hope to come to you soon ,
54003015	but so that if I am delayed you may know how people should conduct themselves in the household of God , which is the church of the living God , the pillar and base of the truth .
54003016	Confessedly great is the mystery of godliness : " Who was manifested in flesh , declared righteous in spirit , seen by angels , proclaimed among Gentiles , believed on in the world , received up in glory . "
54004001	THE Spirit says distinctly that in later times some will desert from the faith , giving attention to deceiving spirits and teachings of demons ,
54004002	through the hypocrisy of men who teach falsely , branded in their own consciences ,
54004003	forbidding marriage , and insisting on abstinence from certain kinds of food which God made to be partaken of with thanksgiving by those who are faithful and know the truth .
54004004	For everything made by God is excellent and nothing is to be rejected if taken with thanksgiving .
54004005	For it is made holy through God's message and through prayer .
54004006	In teaching this to the brethren you will be a noble servant of Christ Jesus , nourished by the words of the faith and of the excellent teaching which you have followed .
54004007	But avoid profane and old-womanish myths . Exercise yourself in godliness .
54004008	Bodily exercise is useful to a small degree , but godliness is useful for everything . " It has the promise of the present life and of the life that is to come . "
54004009	This saying is trustworthy and deserving of full acceptance .
54004010	For to this end we are laboring and wrestling , because we have set our hope on the living God , who is the Savior of all men , especially of believers .
54004011	Command and teach these things .
54004012	Let no one look down on you because you are young , but be an example to believers in speech , in the life you lead , in love , in faith , in purity .
54004013	Until I come give attention to reading , to exhortation , to teaching .
54004014	Do not neglect the gift that is in you , which was given to you through prophecy with the laying on of the hands of the eldership .
54004015	Be careful about these things , be fully occupied with them , that your progress may be plain to all .
54004016	Be thoughtful about yourself and your teaching . Persevere in this ; for in doing so you will save yourself and those who hear you .
54005001	Do not rebuke an older man , but entreat him as a father , the younger men as brothers ,
54005002	the older women as mothers and the younger women as sisters , in all purity .
54005003	Honor widows if they are really widows .
54005004	If any widow has children or grandchildren , let them learn first to act piously toward their own family and to repay what they owe to their parents and grandparents . For this is pleasing in the sight of God .
54005005	A real widow who is left alone has set her hope on God and devotes herself to prayers and supplications night and day .
54005006	But the pleasure-loving widow , though living , is already dead .
54005007	Give these commands that they may be free from reproach .
54005008	If any one does not provide for his own , and especially those of his own household , he has disowned the faith and is worse than an unbeliever .
54005009	A widow is to be put on the list if she has reached the age of not less than sixty years , if she has been true to one husband ,
54005010	has a reputation for good deeds , has brought up children , has entertained strangers , has washed the feet of the holy , has ministered to people in distress , has been active in every good work .
54005011	But younger widows refuse , for when wanton desires lead them away from Christ they wish to marry
54005012	and thus they incur condemnation for breaking their first promise .
54005013	At the same time they learn to be idle , going around from house to house , and not only idle , but gossips , and busybodies , saying what they should not .
54005014	I would , therefore , have the younger widows marry , bear children , keep house , give no occasion to our enemies for slander .
54005015	For already some have turned aside after Satan .
54005016	If any woman who is a believer has widows , she must provide for them and the church must not be burdened , so that it may provide for those who are really widows .
54005017	The elders who preside well should be thought worthy of double salary , especially those who labor in speaking and teaching .
54005018	For the Scripture says , " You shall not muzzle the ox while he is treading out the grain , " and the workman deserves his wages .
54005019	Against an elder do not receive an accusation unless on the testimony of two or three witnesses .
54005020	Those who are going on in sin rebuke before all , that the rest may fear .
54005021	I charge you before God and Christ Jesus and the chosen angels to observe these directions without prejudice , doing nothing through partiality .
54005022	Do not lay hands of ordination upon any one hastily . Have no share in the sins of other men . Keep yourself pure .
54005023	Do not keep on being a water-drinker , but use a little wine for the sake of your stomach and because of your frequent ailments .
54005024	Some men's sins are conspicuous and go on before to condemnation , but the sins of some men follow after them .
54005025	Just so noble deeds are conspicuous and those that are otherwise cannot be hid .
54006001	ALL who are slaves under the yoke must regard their own masters as worthy of all honor , so that the name of God and the teaching may not be profanely slandered .
54006002	Those who have believing masters must not despise them because they are brothers , but rather work as slaves for them because those who are benefited by their good work are believers and beloved . Teach and urge these things .
54006003	If any one teaches otherwise and does not agree to wholesome words , those of our Lord Jesus Christ , and to religious teaching ,
54006004	he is conceited , knowing nothing , but morbidly fond of disputes and controversies from which come envy , strife , abusive language , wicked suspicions ,
54006005	and wranglings of men of depraved minds who are destitute of the truth . They think of religion as a source of gain .
54006006	Religion with contentment is a great source of gain .
54006007	For we brought nothing into the world and we cannot carry anything out .
54006008	If we have food and clothing we will be content with these .
54006009	But those who are determined to be rich fall into temptation and a snare and many foolish and injurious passions which plunge men into destruction and ruin .
54006010	For the love of money is a root of all kinds of evil . Some men grasping for it have strayed from the faith and have pierced themselves with many pangs .
54006011	But you , O man of God , must shun this . Pursue righteousness , piety , faith , love , endurance , gentleness .
54006012	Play the grand hard game of the faith . Lay hold on life eternal , to which you have been called and have made the noble confession before many witnesses .
54006013	I charge you in the presence of God who gives life to all , and Christ Jesus who before Pontius Pilate made the noble confession ,
54006014	to keep the commandment stainless and free from reproach until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
54006015	which in due time he will show , who is the blessed and only Potentate , the King of kings and Lord of lords ,
54006016	who alone has immortality , who dwells in light unapproachable , whom no man has seen or can see . To him be honor and power eternal ! Amen .
54006017	Command those who are rich in this world not to be haughty nor to fix their hope on uncertain wealth , but on God who provides all things richly for our enjoyment .
54006018	They must do good work , be rich in noble deeds , be generous , ready to share ,
54006019	treasuring up for themselves a good fund for the future , that they may lay hold on the life that is real .
54006020	O Timothy , guard what has been entrusted to you , turning away from profane and empty talk and contradictions of what is falsely called " knowledge . "
54006021	Some while professing it have gone astray as regards the faith . Grace be with you all .
55001001	PAUL , an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God according to the promise of life in Christ Jesus ,
55001002	to Timothy my beloved child : Grace , mercy , and peace from God the Father and from Christ Jesus our Lord .
55001003	I thank God whom , I serve , following in the steps of my forefathers , with a pure conscience , while I constantly mention you in my prayers night and day ,
55001004	remembering your tears and longing to see you , that I may be filled with joy .
55001005	I remember the sincere faith that is in you , which lived first in your grandmother Lois and then in your mother Eunice , and I am confident that it lives in you also .
55001006	For this reason let me remind you to kindle anew the gift of God that is in you by the laying on of my hands .
55001007	For God has not given us a spirit of fear , but of power and love and self-control .
55001008	Do not be ashamed to testify for our Lord or for me his prisoner , but join in suffering hardships for the good news as God gives power .
55001009	It is he who saved us and called us with a holy calling , not according to our deeds but according to his own purpose and grace , given to us in Christ Jesus ages ago
55001010	but now manifested by the appearance of our Savior Christ Jesus , who has defeated death and brought to light life and immortality by the good news .
55001011	For this I was made a herald and an apostle and a teacher ,
55001012	and for this reason I am suffering these things . But I am not ashamed , for I know in whom I have put my faith , and am confident that he is able to guard what I have entrusted to him until that day .
55001013	Hold to the example of wholesome words which you heard from me in faith and love in Christ Jesus .
55001014	Guard through the Holy Spirit which dwells in us the precious trust committed to you .
55001015	You know that all of those in Asia have deserted me . Among them are Phygelus and Hermogenes .
55001016	The Lord grant mercy to the family of Onesiphorus , for he often cheered me and was not ashamed of my chain ;
55001017	but when he came to Rome he looked me up eagerly and found me .
55001018	The Lord grant to him to find mercy from the Lord on that day ! And in how many ways he served me in Ephesus you know better still .
55002001	YOU , therefore , my child , must be strong in the grace that is in Christ Jesus ,
55002002	and the things you heard from me , which came through many witnesses , you must commit to trustworthy men who will be able to teach others also .
55002003	Take your share of hardship as a good soldier of Christ Jesus .
55002004	No one while serving as a soldier entangles himself in the affairs of life , for the soldier must please him who enlisted him .
55002005	And if any one enters an athletic contest , he is not crowned unless he competes according to the rules .
55002006	The farmer who does the labor ought first to have his share of the fruits .
55002007	Think over what I am saying , for the Lord will give you insight in all things .
55002008	Remember Jesus Christ , raised from the dead , a descendant of David , as my good news teaches .
55002009	In telling it I am suffering hardships even to chains , as if I were an evildoer , but God's message is not chained .
55002010	For this reason I am enduring all for the sake of the chosen , that they may gain the salvation that is in Christ Jesus with eternal glory .
55002011	Trustworthy is the saying , " For if we have died with him we shall also live with him ;
55002012	if we endure we shall also be kings with him ; if we disown him , he will disown us ;
55002013	if we are faithless , he remains faithful ; for he cannot disown himself . "
55002014	Remind them of these things , charging them before God not to engage in controversy to no profit , but to the ruin of the hearers .
55002015	Be earnest in presenting yourself to God as a tested man , a workman who has no cause to be ashamed , rightly handling the message of truth .
55002016	But shun profane and empty talk . It will grow into greater impiety ,
55002017	and its teachings will spread like a gangrene . Hymenaeus and Philetus are of this sort .
55002018	They have gone astray as to the truth , saying that the resurrection has already taken place , and they are overthrowing the faith of some .
55002019	However , God's solid foundation stands , with this inscription , " The Lord knows his own , " and , " Let every one who names the Lord's name turn from wickedness . "
55002020	In a great house there are not only utensils of gold and silver , but also of wood and earthenware , and some are for honorable and others for dishonorable uses .
55002021	If any one keeps himself pure from these errors , he will be ready for honorable use , holy , fit for the master's service , prepared for every good work .
55002022	But flee the passions of youth and pursue righteousness , faith , love , peace , in the company of those who call on the Lord out of a pure heart .
55002023	Avoid foolish disputes of the uneducated , knowing that they give rise to quarrels ,
55002024	and the servant of the Lord must not quarrel , but be courteous to all , skillful in teaching , forbearing ,
55002025	instructing opponents with gentleness , for God may give them a change of heart which will lead them to knowledge of the truth ,
55002026	and they may return to soberness and escape the snare of the Devil when captured by the Lord's servant to do the Lord's will .
55003001	I WOULD have you know this , that in the last days trying times will come ;
55003002	for people will be lovers of self , lovers of money , boasters , haughty , abusive , disobedient to parents , ungrateful , profane ,
55003003	without family affection , relentless , slanderers , without self-control , brutal , haters of good ,
55003004	treacherous , reckless , conceited , lovers of pleasure rather than lovers of God .
55003005	They will have a form of religion , but will cast off its power . Avoid such people .
55003006	For of this class are those who make their way into houses and take captive weak women loaded with sins , led by varying passions ,
55003007	always learning and never able to come to the knowledge of the truth .
55003008	Just as Jannes and Jambres opposed Moses , so these men oppose the truth , depraved in mind , proved to be worthless as regards the faith .
55003009	But they will go no further , for their folly will be manifest to all as that of Jannes and Jambres became .
55003010	But you have kept track of my teaching , my course of life , my purpose , my faith , my slowness to anger , my love , my patience ,
55003011	my persecutions , my sufferings â what happened to me at Antioch , Iconium , Lystra , what persecutions I underwent . But the Lord delivered me out of all of them .
55003012	And all who are determined to live religiously in Christ Jesus will be persecuted .
55003013	Wicked men and impostors will go on from bad to worse , deceiving and being deceived .
55003014	But you must stand by what you learned and were persuaded of , knowing from whom you learned it
55003015	and that from childhood you have known the sacred writings which can give you wisdom to gain salvation through faith in Christ Jesus .
55003016	All Scripture is divinely inspired and is useful for teaching , for proof , for correction of error , for education in righteousness ,
55003017	that the man of God may be complete , equipped for every good work .
55004001	I CHARGE you before God and Christ Jesus , who will soon judge the living and the dead , and by his appearing and his kingdom :
55004002	proclaim the message , be at it in season and out of season , convince , rebuke , encourage , with all patience in teaching .
55004003	For there will be a time when they will not endure wholesome teaching , but following their own fancies and wishing to have their ears tickled , they will get a crowd of teachers .
55004004	They will turn their ears away from the truth and give attention to myths .
55004005	But you must be calm in all circumstances , suffer hardships , do the work of a bringer of the good news , carry out fully all the duties of your office .
55004006	For I am already being poured out like a drink offering , and the time of my departure is near .
55004007	I have played the grand hard game , I have finished my race , I have kept the faith .
55004008	Now the crown of righteousness is awaiting me . The Lord the righteous judge will give it to me on that day , and not only to me but to all those who have loved his appearing .
55004009	Make haste to come to me quickly .
55004010	For Demas deserted me because he loved the present world and has gone to Thessalonica . Crescens has gone to Galatia , Titus to Dalmatia .
55004011	Luke alone is with me . Get Mark and bring him with you , for he is useful to me in service .
55004012	I sent Tychicus to Ephesus .
55004013	When you come , bring the cloak that I left at Troas with Carpus , and the books , and particularly the parchments .
55004014	Alexander the coppersmith showed much ill will toward me . The Lord will repay him according to his deeds .
55004015	Be on your guard against him , for he strongly opposed our teachings .
55004016	At my first defense no one came to my help ; all deserted me . May it not be laid up against them !
55004017	But the Lord stood by me and strengthened me so that through me the proclamation might be fully published and all the Gentiles might hear it , and I was saved from the mouth of the lion .
55004018	The Lord will rescue me from every wicked attack and will keep me safe for his heavenly kingdom . To him be glory for the ages of the ages ! Amen .
55004019	Give my greetings to Prises and Aquila and the household of Onesiphorus .
55004020	Erastus stayed at Corinth . Trophimus I left at Miletus , sick .
55004021	Try to come before winter . Eubulus and Pudens and Linus and Claudia and all the brethren send their greetings to you .
55004022	The Lord be with your spirit . Grace be with you all .
56001001	PAUL , a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ to promote the faith of God's chosen and their knowledge of the truths of religion ,
56001002	in hope of life eternal , which the God who never lies promised ages ago
56001003	but in due time made known as his message through the proclamation with which I was entrusted by the commission of God our Savior ,
56001004	to Titus my true child in our common faith : Grace and peace from God the Father , and from Christ Jesus , our Savior .
56001005	For this reason I left you in Crete : to arrange the things that are lacking and appoint elders in every city as I directed you ,
56001006	wherever there is a man of irreproachable character , true to one woman , with believing children who are not charged with dissolute conduct and not unruly .
56001007	For a bishop , as God's steward , must be above reproach , not self-willed , not quick-tempered , not given to wine , not given to blows , not eager for base gain ,
56001008	but hospitable , a lover of good , self-controlled , just , holy , temperate ,
56001009	holding to the trustworthy message which is according to the teaching , so that he may be able also to encourage others by wholesome teaching and to refute opposers .
56001010	For there are many insubordinate persons , foolish talkers and deceivers , especially those who are of the circumcision ,
56001011	who ought to be silenced , for they are upsetting whole house-holds , teaching what they should not , merely for the sake of base gain .
56001012	One of themselves , a prophet of their own , said , " Cretans are always liars , base brutes , lazy gluttons . "
56001013	This testimony is true . For this reason rebuke them sharply , that they may be sound in the faith ,
56001014	not giving attention to Jewish myths and rules laid down by men who are turning away from the truth .
56001015	To the pure all things are pure ; but to the polluted and unbelieving nothing is pure . Even their minds and consciences are polluted .
56001016	They profess to know God , but by their deeds they disown him . They are detestable , disobedient , and worthless for any good work .
56002001	YOU must speak to them of the matters which should have a place in wholesome teaching .
56002002	Tell the older men to be temperate , dignified , self-controlled , sound in faith , in love , in patience .
56002003	Tell the older women , in the same way , to be reverent in behavior , not slanderers , not enslaved to much wine , teachers of what is noble ,
56002004	that they may train the young women to be loving wives and loving mothers ,
56002005	self-controlled , pure , home-workers , kind , submissive to their own husbands , that God's message may not be slandered .
56002006	Urge the younger men , in the same way , to practice self-control in everything .
56002007	Make yourself an example of good works , sincerity in teaching , dignified behavior
56002008	and wholesome talk that is above censure , that our opponents may be ashamed , having nothing evil to say about us .
56002009	Tell slaves to be submissive to their own masters in all things and to try to please them , not answering back ,
56002010	not pilfering , but showing all kindly fidelity , so as to make the teaching about God our Savior seem beautiful in all respects .
56002011	For the grace of God has appeared bringing salvation to all men ,
56002012	teaching us to renounce all irreligion and worldly passions and to live soberly , justly and piously in this present world ,
56002013	waiting for the blessed hope , the glorious appearing of the great God and of our Savior Christ Jesus ,
56002014	who gave himself for us to redeem us from all sin and purify us as his own people earnest in honorable work .
56002015	Tell them these things , urge , convince with all authority ; let no one slight you .
56003001	REMIND them to be submissive to ruling authorities , to be obedient , to be ready for every good work ,
56003002	to speak abusively to no one , to be peaceable , to be fair , showing all gentleness toward all men .
56003003	For we ourselves were once thoughtless , disobedient , astray , enslaved to passions and various pleasures , living in malice and envy , hateful and hating one another .
56003004	But when the kindness of our Savior , God , and his love to men appeared ,
56003005	" not because of works that we had done in righteousness , but out of his own mercy he saved us through the bath of the new birth and the renewing of the Holy Spirit
56003006	which he poured out upon us richly through Jesus Christ our Savior ,
56003007	that we might be declared righteous by his grace and become heirs with the hope of life eternal . "
56003008	That is a trustworthy saying . I wish you to insist on these things so that those who have put their faith in God may give earnest attention to honorable work . These things are honorable and also useful to men .
56003009	But avoid foolish disputes and genealogies and strife and quarrels about the Law ; for they are unprofitable and futile .
56003010	If a man is factious , after one or two warnings , have nothing more to do with him ,
56003011	knowing that such a one is perverted and goes on sinning though self-condemned .
56003012	When I send Artemas to you or Tychicus , try to come to me at Nicopolis , for I have decided to pass the winter there .
56003013	Do your best in helping Zenas , the lawyer , and Apollos forward on their journey so that they may lack nothing .
56003014	Our people too must learn to give attention to honorable work , so as to be able to meet pressing needs , that they may not be fruitless .
56003015	All who are with me send you their greetings . Give our greetings to those who love us in the faith . Grace be with all of you .
57001001	PAUL , a prisoner of Christ Jesus , and Timothy our brother , to Philemon , our beloved fellow worker ,
57001002	and to Apphia , our sister , and to Archippus , our fellow soldier , and to the Church that meets at your house :
57001003	Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
57001004	I always thank my God when I mention you in my prayers ,
57001005	for I hear of the love and the loyalty that you have to the Lord Jesus Christ and to all the holy .
57001006	I pray that your fellowship in the faith may become effective in the knowledge of all the good there is in us in our relation to Christ .
57001007	For I have had great joy and encouragement in your love , because the hearts of the holy have been refreshed by you , brother .
57001008	Therefore , though I might have great boldness in Christ to command you what is fitting ,
57001009	I beg you rather for love's sake , as Paul the old man and now the prisoner of Christ Jesus â
57001010	I beg you in behalf of my child Onesimus , born to me in my chains ,
57001011	who once was useless to you , but now is useful to you and to me .
57001012	I am sending him back to you , though he is my very heart .
57001013	I should like to have him for my own , to serve me in my chains for the good news , as your representative ,
57001014	but without your consent I am unwilling to do anything , so that your goodness may not be of necessity but of free will .
57001015	Perhaps it was for this that he was separated from you for a time , that you might have him back for ever ,
57001016	no longer as a slave , but more than a slave , a brother beloved , especially to me , but how much more to you , both in the flesh and in the Lord .
57001017	If then you hold me for a partner , receive him as you would me .
57001018	If he has wronged you in any way or owes you anything , charge that to my account .
57001019	I , Paul , write it with my own hand . I will pay it â not to mention to you that you owe me your own self besides .
57001020	Yes , brother , let me have this help from you in the Lord ; refresh my heart in Christ .
57001021	I am writing to you confident of your obedience and knowing that you will do more than I say .
57001022	At the same time I want you to prepare a lodging for me , for I hope that through your prayers I shall be given back to you .
57001023	Epaphras , my fellow prisoner in Christ Jesus ,
57001024	and Mark , Aristarchus , Demas and Luke , my fellow workers , send you their greetings .
57001025	The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with your spirits .
58001001	MANY times and in many ways God spoke of old to our fathers by the prophets ;
58001002	but at the end of these days he has spoken to us by a Son , whom he has appointed heir of all things and through whom he made the world ,
58001003	who is the reflection of his glory and the expression of his nature and sustains all things by his word of power , and who , when he had made purification from sins , took his seat at the right hand of the Majesty on high ,
58001004	having become as much superior to the angels as the name he has inherited surpasses theirs .
58001005	For to which of the angels did he ever say , " Thou art my son ; I have to-day become thy Father " ? and again , " I will be to him a Father and he shall be to me a Son " ?
58001006	And again when he brings his first-born into the world of men he says , " And let all the angels of God bow down to him . "
58001007	Referring to the angels he says , " He makes his angels winds , his servants a flame of fire . "
58001008	But regarding the Son he says , " Thy throne , O God , is forever and ever . Thy royal scepter is a scepter of justice .
58001009	Thou lovest righteousness and hatest lawlessness , therefore God , thy God , has anointed thee with the oil of gladness beyond thy companions . "
58001010	And , " Thou , in the beginning , O Lord , didst found the earth , and the heavens are works of thy hands .
58001011	They will perish , but thou wilt endure . They all will grow old like a garment
58001012	and like a mantle thou wilt roll them up . But thou art the same and thy years will never end . "
58001013	To which of the angels did he ever say , " Sit at my right hand till I make thine enemies thy footstool " ?
58001014	Are they not all ministering spirits sent forth for service in behalf of those who are to inherit salvation ?
58002001	FOR this reason we should give special attention to the things that we have heard , so as not to drift away from them .
58002002	For if the message spoken through angels was sure and every violation and disobedience received merited punishment ,
58002003	how shall we escape if we neglect so great a salvation , which at the beginning was spoken by the Lord and was confirmed to us by those who heard him ,
58002004	while God added his testimony by signs and wonders and many kinds of miracles and impartation of the Holy Spirit according to his will ?
58002005	For he has not subjected to angels the coming world of which we speak .
58002006	But somewhere one says , " What is man that thou rememberest him ? Or the son of man that thou carest for him ?
58002007	Thou hast made him a little lower than the angels . With glory and honor thou hast crowned him .
58002008	All things thou hast put under his feet . " When he put all things under him he left nothing that was not put under him . We do not yet see all things put under him ,
58002009	but we see Jesus , who was made a little lower than the angels for the suffering of death that by the grace of God he might taste of death for every man , now crowned with glory and honor .
58002010	For it was fitting that he through whom are all things and for whom are all things , when leading many sons to glory , should make the great Leader of their salvation perfect through sufferings .
58002011	For he who makes holy and they who are made holy are all of one . For this cause he is not ashamed to call them brothers ,
58002012	saying , " I will tell thy name to my brothers . In the midst of the assembly I will sing praise to thee , "
58002013	and again , " I will trust in him , " and again , " Here am I and the children whom God has given me . "
58002014	Since then the children share in blood and flesh , he himself in the same way shared in them , in order that through death he might defeat him who had the power of death , that is , the Devil ,
58002015	and set free all those who through fear of death were all their lives doomed to slavery .
58002016	For he does not come to the help of angels , but he comes to the help of the descendants of Abraham .
58002017	And for that reason he had to be made like his brethren in everything , so as to be a compassionate and faithful high priest in things relating to God , to make propitiation for the sins of the people .
58002018	For since he himself has suffered when tempted he is able to help those who are tempted .
58003001	THEREFORE , holy brethren , sharers in a heavenly call , consider the Apostle and High Priest of our confession , Jesus ,
58003002	who was faithful to him who made him as also Moses was in all God's house .
58003003	For he has been thought worthy of more glory than Moses , just as he who has built a house has more honor than the house .
58003004	For every house is built by some one , but he who built all things is God .
58003005	Moses was faithful in all God's house as a servant for a testimony to the things that were to be spoken ,
58003006	but Christ as a Son over his own house . We are his house if we hold firmly to the end our confidence and the hope of which we boast .
58003007	Wherefore , as the Holy Spirit says , " To-day if you will hear his voice ,
58003008	do not harden your hearts as when they made me angry on the day when they tried me in the desert ,
58003009	when your fathers put me to a test and saw my deeds for forty years .
58003010	Therefore I was much displeased with that generation and said , ' They always go astray in their hearts and they do not know my paths . '
58003011	So I swore in my wrath , ' They shall not enter into my rest . '
58003012	See to it , brethren , that there shall not be in any one of you a wicked , unbelieving heart ready to forsake the living God ,
58003013	but encourage one another daily while it is called " to-day , " that no one may be hardened by the deceitfulness of sin .
58003014	For we become sharers with Christ if we hold firmly to the end the assurance with which we began .
58003015	When it is said , " To-day if you will hear his voice , do not harden your hearts as when they made me angry " â
58003016	who when they heard made him angry ? Was it not all those who came out of Egypt with Moses ?
58003017	With whom was he much displeased for forty years ? Was it not with those who sinned , whose bodies fell in the desert ?
58003018	To whom did he swear that they should not enter his rest , except to those who had no faith ?
58003019	We see that they were unable to enter because of their lack of faith .
58004001	LET us , then , be afraid that , though the promise of entering his rest is still left , some one of you may seem to have missed it .
58004002	For we have received the good news just as they did , but the message that was heard did not benefit them , since it did not meet with faith in the hearers .
58004003	For we who have faith are entering into the rest , as he said , " As I swore in my wrath , ' They shall not enter into my rest , ' " although his works had been finished since the creation of the world .
58004004	For he has somewhere spoken of the seventh day thus , " And God rested on the seventh day from all his works , "
58004005	and in this place again , " They shall not enter into my rest . "
58004006	Since , then , it remains for some to enter into it , and those who first received the good news did not enter because of lack of faith â
58004007	again he indicates a day , " to-day , " saying in David so long after , as has been already quoted , " To-day if you will hear his voice , do not harden your hearts . "
58004008	For if Joshua had given them rest he would not be speaking of another day after that .
58004009	Therefore there still remains a rest for the people of God .
58004010	For he who has entered into God's rest has rested from his works as God did from his .
58004011	Let us endeavor then to enter into that rest so that no one shall fall , after that example of lack of faith .
58004012	For the word of God is living and effective and sharper than any two-edged sword , and it pierces until it divides soul and spirit , joints and marrow , and it judges the thoughts and purposes of the heart .
58004013	There is not a creature invisible to him , but all things are naked and defenseless before the eyes of him to whom we must account .
58004014	Since , then , we have a great High Priest who has passed through the heavens , Jesus , the Son of God , let us hold fast our confession .
58004015	For we have not a high priest who cannot sympathize with our weaknesses , for he has been tempted in every way just as we are , yet without sin .
58004016	Therefore let us come with confidence to the throne of grace and receive compassion and find grace for timely help .
58005001	FOR every high priest taken from among men is appointed in behalf of men in things relating to God to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins .
58005002	He is able to sympathize with the ignorant and the erring , since he himself is beset with weaknesses .
58005003	For this reason he must bring an offering for his own sins , just as he does for those of the people .
58005004	And no one takes this honor upon himself unless called by God , as Aaron was .
58005005	So too Christ did not take for himself the glory of becoming a high priest , but he who said to him , " Thou art my Son , to-day I have become thy Father , "
58005006	and who says in another place , " Thou art a priest forever after the order of Melchizedek . "
