58005007	Christ , in the days of his flesh , offered prayers and supplications to him who was able to save him from death , with strong outcries and tears , and was heard and saved from his terrors .
58005008	Although he was a Son he learned obedience from his sufferings ,
58005009	and being thus made perfect he became the author of eternal salvation to all who obey him ,
58005010	and was proclaimed by God a high priest after the order of Melchizedek .
58005011	Regarding Melchizedek we have much to say that is hard to explain , since you have become dull of hearing .
58005012	For when , considering the time , you ought to be teachers you need to have some one teach you again the first principles of the revelations of God . You have come to need milk and not solid food .
58005013	For every one who takes milk is inexperienced in the doctrine of righteousness , for he is a child .
58005014	But solid food is for adults who through practice have their senses exercised in distinguishing good and bad .
58006001	THEREFORE let us leave elementary teaching about Christ and hasten on to what is advanced , not laying again a foundation â change of heart from dead works , faith in God ,
58006002	the teaching about baptisms , the laying on of hands , resurrection of the dead , and eternal judgment .
58006003	This we will do if God permits .
58006004	For it is impossible for those who have been once for all enlightened and have tasted the heavenly gift and have become sharers in the Holy Spirit
58006005	and have tasted God's word and the powers of the coming world ,
58006006	and then have fallen away , to have again a change of heart , since they are crucifying for themselves afresh the Son of God and putting him to open shame .
58006007	For ground that drinks the rain that comes often upon it and bears plants useful to those for whom it is farmed shares in God's blessing ;
58006008	but if it bears thorns and thistles it is judged worthless and is near to being cursed . In the end it will be burnt over .
58006009	But we are persuaded of better things regarding you , beloved , things that belong with salvation , though we thus speak .
58006010	For God is not so unjust as to forget your work and the love that you have shown to his name as you have served and are still serving the holy .
58006011	But we desire to have each one of you show to the end the same earnestness for the fulfillment of our hope ,
58006012	that you may not be dull , but imitators of those who through faith and patience are inheriting the promises .
58006013	For God , when making the promise to Abraham , since he could swear by no one greater , swore by himself ,
58006014	saying , " Surely , I will greatly bless you and greatly multiply you . "
58006015	And so after patient waiting Abraham obtained what was promised .
58006016	For men swear by the greater and an oath for confirmation is to them the end of all dispute .
58006017	In this case God being abundantly willing to show to the heirs of the promise the unchangeable purpose of his will gave the surety of an oath ,
58006018	that by two unchangeable things , in which it was impossible for God to be false , we might have strong encouragement , we who have fled to lay hold on the hope that lies before us .
58006019	We have this hope as an anchor of the soul , sure and firm , and it enters into the tent within the curtain
58006020	where Jesus , our forerunner , has entered in our behalf , becoming forever a high priest after the order of Melchizedek .
58007001	FOR , this Melchizedek , king of Salem , priest of God Most High , who met Abraham when he was returning from the defeat of the kings and blessed him ,
58007002	and to whom Abraham gave a tenth of all ,
58007003	without father , without mother , without ancestors , without either birthday or end of life , but made like the Son of God , remains a priest permanently .
58007004	But see how great this man was , since Abraham the patriarch gave him a tenth of his choicest spoils .
58007005	And even those of the sons of Levi who attain the priesthood have command according to the Law to take a tenth from the people , their own brethren , although these have sprung from the loins of Abraham .
58007006	But he who had no genealogy from these took a tenth from Abraham and pronounced a blessing on him who had the promises .
58007007	Without dispute the less is blessed by the greater .
58007008	And here mortal men receive tenths , but there one of whom the witness is that he is living .
58007009	And , to put it frankly , Levi , who receives the tenths , was made to pay a tenth through Abraham .
58007010	For he was still in the loins of his father when Melchizedek met Abraham .
58007011	If , then , perfection had been through the Levitical priesthood , â for on the basis of that the people received the Law â what need was there for another kind of priest to arise and not be called of the order of Aaron ?
58007012	For when the priesthood has been changed there comes of necessity also a change of law .
58007013	For he of whom these things are said belongs to another tribe , from which no one has ever had anything to do with the altar .
58007014	For it is plain that our Lord has arisen from Judah , and in connection with that tribe Moses said nothing about priests .
58007015	And this is yet more abundantly evident if after the order of Melchizedek there arises a priest of a different kind
58007016	who has become such , not according to the law of a commandment made for the flesh , but according to the power of unending life .
58007017	For it is affirmed of him , " Thou art a priest forever after the order of Melchizedek . "
58007018	There is a setting aside of the earlier commandment because of its weakness and uselessness â
58007019	for the Law brought nothing to perfection â and there is the bringing in of a better hope through which we draw near to God .
58007020	And just as it was not without an oath â
58007021	for those men have become priests without an oath , but he with an oath from him who said to him , " The Lord has sworn and will not change his mind : thou art a priest forever " â
58007022	by so much better is the covenant of which Jesus has become surety .
58007023	And many of them became priests because they were prevented by death from continuing ,
58007024	but he , because he continues forever , has an unending priesthood .
58007025	And so he is able to save perfectly those who come to God through him , since he is forever living to intercede for them .
58007026	For such was the High Priest that we needed , holy , innocent , unstained , separated from sinners , and made higher than the heavens .
58007027	He has not the daily need , like the other priests , first to offer sacrifices for his own sins and then for those of the people . This latter he did once for all when he offered himself .
58007028	For the Law makes high priests of men who have infirmities , but the word of the oath , which comes after the Law , makes High Priest of a Son who is perfected forever .
58008001	THE chief point of what I have been saying is this : we have such a High Priest who has taken his seat at the right hand of the throne of Majesty in the heavens ,
58008002	and who ministers in the holy place and in the true Tent set up by the Lord , not by man .
58008003	Now every high priest is appointed to offer gifts and sacrifices . Whence it is necessary for this one to have something to offer .
58008004	If he were upon the earth he would not be a priest at all , since there are those who offer the gifts according to the Law .
58008005	They minister as an example and shadow of the things in heaven , just as Moses was divinely instructed when he was about to make the Tent . " See , " it was said , " that you make everything according to the model shown you on the mountain . "
58008006	But now Christ has obtained a ministry as much more excellent as the covenant of which he is mediator is better and based upon better promises .
58008007	For if that first covenant had been faultless a place would not have been sought for a second .
58008008	But finding fault with it he says , " The days are coming , says the Lord , when I will make for the house of Israel and for the house of Judah a new covenant ,
58008009	not in the manner of the covenant which I made with their fathers , on the day when I took them by the hand to lead them out of the land of Egypt . For they did not abide by my covenant and I ceased to care for them , says the Lord .
58008010	This is the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel after those days , says the Lord ; I will put my laws into their minds and will write them upon their hearts and I will be their God and they will be my people .
58008011	They shall not teach each one his fellow citizen and each one his brother saying , ' Know the Lord ' ; for all shall know me , from the least to the greatest of them ,
58008012	and I will be merciful to their wrong-doings and their sins I will remember no more . "
58008013	In saying " new " he has pronounced the first covenant old . But what grows old and decadent is near to disappearance .
58009001	THE first covenant had regulations of worship and its holy building in this world .
58009002	For a Tent was erected , in the first part of which were the lampstand and the table and the consecrated bread . This was called the Holy Place .
58009003	Behind the second curtain was the part called the Holy of Holies .
58009004	It had the golden altar of incense and the ark of the covenant all covered with gold . In this was a golden jar with the manna and Aaron's rod that sprouted and the tablets of the covenant .
58009005	Above it were cherubim of glory overshadowing the place of propitiation . Regarding these things it is not now possible to speak in detail .
58009006	But these things being thus arranged , the priests go constantly into the first part of the Tent , performing their services ,
58009007	but into the second part the High Priest alone goes once in the year , not without blood , which he offers for himself and for the sins ignorantly committed by the people .
58009008	The Holy Spirit shows this , that the way into the holy place has not yet been made plain while the first Tent is standing .
58009009	That is a symbol , for the time being , in accordance with which gifts and sacrifices are offered , though they cannot make the worshiper perfect in his conscience ,
58009010	since they consist only of foods and drinks and various baths â rules respecting the flesh , imposed until the time of reformation .
58009011	But when Christ came as High Priest of the good things that have come , he entered once for all through the greater and more perfect Tent not made by hands â that is , not of this creation â
58009012	and not with the blood of goats and calves , but with his own blood , into the holy place , and thereby found eternal redemption .
58009013	For if the blood of goats and bulls , and the ashes of a heifer sprinkling the defiled , makes them holy as regards purity of their flesh ,
58009014	how much more will the blood of Christ , who through an eternal Spirit offered himself an unblemished sacrifice to God , cleanse our consciences from dead works for the service of the living God .
58009015	For this reason he is the mediator of a better covenant that , a death having taken place for redemption from sins under the first covenant , those who have been called may receive the eternal inheritance promised to them .
58009016	For where there is a last will and testament the death of the testator must be put in evidence .
58009017	For a will is valid in the case of the dead : it never has any force while the testator is living .
58009018	Hence the first covenant was not introduced without blood .
58009019	When all the commands of the Law had been spoken by Moses to all the people , he took the blood of calves and goats , with water and scarlet wool and hyssop , and sprinkled it on the book and on all the people ,
58009020	saying , " This is the blood of the covenant which God has commanded for you . "
58009021	And the Tent and all the things used in worship he likewise sprinkled with blood .
58009022	Almost everything is cleansed with blood , according to the Law , and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness .
58009023	It was necessary , then , that the copies of the things in heaven should be cleansed with these sacrifices , but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these .
58009024	For Christ did not enter into a holy place made by hands , a copy of the true , but into heaven itself , now to appear before the face of God in our behalf .
58009025	Nor was it to offer himself often , as the High Priest enters into the holy place every year with blood not his own ;
58009026	then he must have suffered often since the foundation of the world . But now , once for all , at the end of the ages , he has appeared to do away with sin by his sacrifice .
58009027	And as it is appointed for men once for all to die and after this comes judgment ,
58009028	so Christ was once for all offered to bear the sins of many and will appear the second time , apart from sin , to those who are looking for him , and bring them salvation .
58010001	FOR the Law with a shadow of the good things that are coming , but not the very likeness of the things , cannot , by the same sacrifices which they offer constantly every year , ever make perfect those who come ,
58010002	since would they not have ceased offering them ? Because the worshipers , once for all cleansed , would have had no consciousness of sins .
58010003	But in the sacrifices these are called to mind every year .
58010004	For the blood of bulls and goats is powerless to take away sins .
58010005	Therefore on coming into the world he says , " Sacrifice and offering thou dost not desire : a body thou hast prepared for me .
58010006	Whole burnt offerings and sin offerings thou dost not delight in .
58010007	Then I said , ' Here I have come â in the roll of the book it is written of me â to do thy will , O God . ' "
58010008	He first says , " Sacrifices and offerings and whole burnt offerings and sin offerings thou dost not desire nor delight in , " such as are offered according to the Law ,
58010009	and then he says , " Here I have come to do thy will . " He takes away the first to establish the second .
58010010	By this " will " we are made holy through the offering of the body of Jesus Christ once for all .
58010011	Every priest stands daily doing service and offering many times the same sacrifices , although they never can take away sins .
58010012	But this Priest after offering one sacrifice for sins forever , took his seat at the right hand of God ,
58010013	for the future only waiting until his enemies are made his footstool .
58010014	For by one offering he has forever perfected those who are made holy .
58010015	The Holy Spirit testifies this to us ; for after having said ,
58010016	" This is the covenant that I will make with them after those days , says the Lord : I will put my laws in their hearts and on their minds I will write them , " he adds ,
58010017	" and their sins and their law-breakings I will remember no more . "
58010018	But where there is forgiveness of these , there is no longer any offering for sin .
58010019	Since we have , then , brethren , confidence in entering the holy place through the blood of Jesus ,
58010020	by the new and living way which he has made for us through the curtain , that is , his flesh ,
58010021	and since we have a great Priest over the house of God ,
58010022	let us come with true hearts in full assurance of faith , having our hearts sprinkled from an evil conscience and our bodies bathed in pure water .
58010023	Let us hold fast the confession of our hope without wavering , for he is faithful who has promised ,
58010024	and let us keep watch to incite one another to love and noble deeds ,
58010025	not neglecting to assemble yourselves , as some do , but encouraging one another , and so much the more , as you see the day drawing near .
58010026	For if we go on sinning willfully after receiving the knowledge of the truth , there remains no longer any sacrifice for sins ,
58010027	but a dreadful expectation of doom and a fury of fire that will devour the opposers .
58010028	Any one who sets aside a law of Moses dies without pity on the testimony of two or three witnesses .
58010029	Of how much worse punishment do you think he will be judged worthy who has trampled on the Son of God , who has thought the blood of the covenant , by which it was made holy , an unholy thing , and who has insulted the Spirit of grace ?
58010030	For we know him who said , " Vengeance is mine , I will repay , " and again , " The Lord will judge his people . "
58010031	It is dreadful to fall into the hands of the living God .
58010032	Remember the early days in which , after being enlightened , you endured a great struggle with sufferings ,
58010033	at one time made a public spectacle by reproaches and distresses , at another time making common cause with those who were thus treated .
58010034	For you even suffered with the prisoners and accepted the plundering of your property with joy , knowing that you had a better and enduring possession .
58010035	Do not , then , cast away your confidence , for it will have a great reward .
58010036	You have need of patience so that after doing the will of God you may gain the promised blessing .
58010037	For yet " a little , very little , while , and he who is coming will come and will not delay .
58010038	My righteous man will live by faith ; but if he shrinks back , my soul has no delight in him . "
58010039	But we are not of those who shrink back and perish , but of those who have faith and will win their souls .
58011001	FAITH is an assurance of things hoped for , a conviction of things not seen .
58011002	By this the men of old won their fame .
58011003	By faith we understand that the worlds came into order at the word of God , so that what is now seen did not come out of things that are visible .
58011004	By faith Abel offered to God a better sacrifice than Cain , for which he had witness borne to him that he was righteous , God testifying to his gifts , and by it , though dead , he still speaks .
58011005	By faith Enoch was taken from the earth so that he did not see death , and he was not found because God had taken him . For before being taken he had this testimony that he had pleased God .
58011006	But without faith it is impossible to please him . For he who comes to God must have faith that he exists and that he becomes the rewarder of those who seek him .
58011007	By faith Noah , after receiving a divine warning regarding things as yet unseen , reverently built an ark for the saving of his household . Thus he condemned the world and became an heir of the righteousness of faith .
58011008	By faith Abraham when called obeyed and came out into the place which he was to obtain for an inheritance . He came out not knowing where he was coming .
58011009	By faith he made his home in the promised land as in a foreign country , living in tents with Isaac and Jacob , the heirs with him of the same promise .
58011010	For he was looking for the city that has the foundations , whose architect and builder is God .
58011011	By faith Sarah received power to conceive a child even when past the natural time of life , since she thought him trustworthy who had given the promise .
58011012	And so from just one man , already dead in that respect , there sprang descendants " as the stars of heaven in multitude and as the sand on the seashore innumerable . "
58011013	These all died in faith , not having obtained the promised blessings , but they saw them and greeted them afar and confessed that they were strangers and foreigners in the land .
58011014	For those who say such things make it plain that they are seeking a fatherland .
58011015	And if they had been thinking of that land from which they came they would have had opportunity to return .
58011016	But now they desire a better land , that is , a heavenly one . Therefore God is not ashamed of them â of being called their God ; for he has prepared for them a city .
58011017	By faith Abraham when he was tested offered up Isaac , and he who had received the promises began offering his only son
58011018	regarding whom it had been said , " Those only whose descent is through Isaac shall be called your descendants . "
58011019	He reasoned that God was able to raise him even from the dead , and figuratively he did win him back from the dead .
58011020	By faith also Isaac blessed Jacob and Esau and spoke of things to come .
58011021	By faith Jacob when dying blessed each of the sons of Joseph and worshiped leaning on the top of his staff .
58011022	By faith Joseph , when at his end , mentioned the departure of the children of Israel and gave orders regarding his own bones .
58011023	By faith Moses at his birth was hidden three months by his parents , because they saw that the child was beautiful , and they did not fear the king's command .
58011024	By faith Moses when he had grown up refused to be called a son of Pharaoh's daughter .
58011025	He chose rather to suffer hard-ship with the people of God than to enjoy the brief pleasure of sin ,
58011026	and he thought the reproach of Christ greater riches than the treasures of Egypt . For he was looking to the final reward .
58011027	By faith he left Egypt , not fearing the king's anger ; for he endured as if seeing him who is unseen .
58011028	By faith he kept the Passover and the sprinkling of the blood , so that the destroyer might not touch their first-born .
58011029	By faith they crossed the Red Sea as on dry land ; but the Egyptians when they tried to do so were drowned .
58011030	By faith the walls of Jericho fell down after they had been encircled seven days .
58011031	By faith Rahab , the prostitute , did not perish with those who had refused to believe ; because she had welcomed the spies with peace .
58011032	And what shall I say further ? Time would fail me to tell of Gideon , Barak , Samson , Jephthah , and of David and Samuel and the prophets ;
58011033	who through faith struggled against kingdoms and subdued them , did deeds of righteousness , obtained promised blessings , shut the mouths of lions ,
58011034	quenched the power of fire , escaped the edge of the sword , out of weakness grew strong , became mighty in war , turned back armies of foreigners .
58011035	Women received back their dead by a resurrection . Others were tortured , refusing to pay for liberation , in order to gain a better resurrection .
58011036	Still others had experience of mockings and floggings , yes , of chains and prisons .
58011037	They were stoned , afflicted , sawn in two , murdered with the sword . They went about in sheepskins , in goatskins , destitute , distressed , maltreated .
58011038	The world was not worthy of them . They wandered in deserts and mountains , in caves and in holes in the earth .
58011039	All these won God's approval by their faith . Yet they did not obtain the fulfillment of the promise .
58011040	In reference to us God had something better in view , that they without us should not reach perfection .
58012001	THEREFORE , surrounded as we are by so great a cloud of witnesses , let us lay aside every weight and the sin that so easily besets us , and let us run with patience the race that lies before us ,
58012002	looking to Jesus the beginner and finisher of our faith , who for the joy set before him endured a cross , thinking little of the shame , and has taken his seat at the right hand of the throne of God .
58012003	Think of him who endured such hostile speaking of sinners against him , that you may not grow weary and despondent in heart .
58012004	You have not yet resisted to blood in the contest against sin ,
58012005	and you have forgotten the encouragement which reasons with you as with sons , " My son , do not think slightingly of the discipline of the Lord and be not faint-hearted when reproved by him :
58012006	for whom the Lord loves he disciplines and scourges every son whom he receives as his own . "
58012007	It is for discipline that you are enduring . God is laying it upon you as upon sons . For what son is there whom his father does not discipline ?
58012008	But if you are without discipline , in which all share , then you are bastards and not sons .
58012009	Besides , we had fathers of our flesh who disciplined us and we used to reverence them . Shall we not much more be submissive to the Father of our spirits and live ?
58012010	For they for a few days disciplined us as seemed good to them , but he for our profit , that we may share his holiness .
58012011	All discipline for the time being seems not joyous but grievous , but afterward it yields the peaceful fruit of righteousness to those who have passed through its training .
58012012	So raise the relaxed hands and straighten the unstrung knees
58012013	and make straight paths for your feet , so that the lame limb may not be put out of joint but rather cured .
58012014	Follow after peace with all men and holiness , without which no one will see the Lord .
58012015	Be on your guard that no one shall fail of the grace of God , that no bitter root shall sprout up and trouble you and through it many be stained ,
58012016	that there shall be none unchaste , or profane like Esau , who for one meal sold his birthright .
58012017	For you know that afterward when he wished to inherit the blessing he was rejected , for he found no place for a change in his father's mind though he sought it earnestly with tears .
58012018	For you have not come to something that may be touched , ablaze with fire , and to blackness and darkness and tempest
58012019	and the blast of a trumpet and the sound of words which those who heard begged not to have spoken of them .
58012020	For they could not bear the command , " If even an animal touches the mountain it must be stoned . "
58012021	And so dreadful was the sight that Moses said , " I am terrified and trembling . "
58012022	But you have come to Mount Zion and the city of the living God , heavenly Jerusalem , to tens of thousands of angels ,
58012023	to the festal assembly and congregation of first-born who are enrolled in heaven , and to God the Judge of all , and to the spirits of righteous men made perfect ,
58012024	and to Jesus the Mediator of the new covenant and to the sprinkled blood which tells something better than the blood of Abel .
58012025	Beware of rejecting him who is speaking . For if those did not escape who rejected him who taught the divine will on earth , much less shall we if we reject him who speaks from heaven .
58012026	His voice then shook the earth , but now he has announced , " Yet once for all I shall shake not only the earth but also heaven . "
58012027	And this expression " yet once for all " shows the removal of the things shaken , as of things that have been made , that the unshaken things may remain .
58012028	So then , since we are receiving an unshaken kingdom , let us have grace by which we may worship God acceptably with reverence and awe .
58012029	For our God is a consuming fire .
58013001	LET brotherly love continue .
58013002	Do not forget hospitality : for by this some have , without knowing it , had angels as their guests .
58013003	Keep in mind the prisoners , as if you were their fellow prisoners , and those who are suffering hardships , since you yourselves are also in the body .
58013004	Let marriage be held in honor by all and let the bed be undefiled ; for unchaste persons and adulterers God will judge .
58013005	Let your lives be free from the love of money . Be content with what you have . For he has said , " I will not fail you nor will I forsake you . "
58013006	So we may say with courage , " The Lord is my helper ; I will not fear . What can man do to me ? "
58013007	Remember your leaders , those who have spoken to you God's message , think how they ended their lives and imitate their faith .
58013008	Jesus Christ is yesterday and to-day the same â yes , and through the ages .
58013009	Do not be carried away with all sorts of foreign teachings . It is well to have the heart strengthened by grace , not by special kinds of food . Those who live in that way are not profited .
58013010	We have an altar of which those who worship in the Tent have no right to eat .
58013011	For the bodies of the animals whose blood is brought into the holy place by the High Priest are burned outside the camp .
58013012	For this reason Jesus also , to make the people holy by his own blood , suffered outside the gate .
58013013	Let us go out to him outside the camp and bear the reproaches cast on him .
58013014	For we have here no continuing city , but we are seeking the coming one .
58013015	Through him then let us offer to God always the sacrifice of praise , that is , the fruit of lips that make confession in his name .
58013016	Do not forget kindness and generosity , for with such sacrifices God is well pleased .
58013017	Obey your leaders and yield to their authority ; for they watch over your souls as those who must give account , that they may do it with joy and not with sighing . That would be unprofitable for you .
58013018	Pray for us : for we are confident that we have a good conscience , wishing to live nobly in every way .
58013019	I earnestly beg you to do this that I may be restored to you the sooner .
58013020	May the God of peace , who brought up from the dead our Lord Jesus , the great Shepherd of the sheep through the blood of an eternal covenant ,
58013021	equip you with every good thing for doing his will , doing in you what is well-pleasing in his sight through Jesus Christ , to whom be glory for the ages of the ages . Amen .
58013022	I beg you , brethren , to bear with my words of exhortation ; for I have written to you briefly .
58013023	I wish you to know that our brother Timothy has been set at liberty . With him , if he comes soon , I will see you .
58013024	Give my greetings to all your leaders and all the holy . Those who are from Italy send their greetings to you .
58013025	Grace be with you all .
59001001	JAMES , a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ , to the Twelve Tribes which are scattered in foreign lands : Greeting .
59001002	Think it all joy , my brethren , when you fall into all sorts of trials ,
59001003	since you know that the testing of your faith brings out endurance .
59001004	Let endurance do its complete work , that you may be complete and perfect , lacking in nothing .
59001005	If any one of you is lacking in wisdom , let him ask it from God , who gives to all freely without reproaching , and it will be given to him .
59001006	But he must ask in faith with never a doubt . For he who doubts is like a wave of the sea , driven by the wind and tossed .
59001007	For that man must not think that he will obtain anything from the Lord â
59001008	a two-minded man unsteady in all his ways .
59001009	Let the lowly brother glory in his high station ,
59001010	and let the rich brother glory in his lowly station , for he will pass away like a flower of the grass .
59001011	For the sun rises with scorching heat and dries up the grass , and the flower of it falls and the beauty of its face perishes . So shall the rich man wither in his pursuits .
59001012	Blessed is the man who endures trial , for when he has been tested he will gain the crown of life which the Lord has promised to those who love him .
59001013	No one must say when tempted , " My temptation comes from God . " For God cannot be tempted by evil , and he tempts no one .
59001014	Every one is tempted when he is drawn away by his own passions and enticed .
59001015	Then when passion has conceived it gives birth to sin , and sin , when it is full grown , gives birth to death .
59001016	Make no mistake , my beloved brethren ,
59001017	every good gift and every perfect boon is from above ; it descends from the Father of lights , with whom there is no change or shadow caused by turning .
59001018	Of his own will he made us his children through the message of truth , so that we might be a sort of first fruits of his creatures .
59001019	I wish you to know this , my beloved brethren : Every man must be quick to hear , but slow to speak , slow to anger .
59001020	For a man's anger does not work out God's righteousness .
59001021	So lay aside all that is vile and all that remains of malice , and receive with gentleness the implanted message which can save your souls .
59001022	Become doers of the message and not hearers only , deceiving your own selves .
59001023	For if one is a hearer of the message and not a doer , he is like a man who looks at his natural face in a mirror .
59001024	He looks at himself and is gone , and immediately forgets what sort of man he was .
59001025	But he who looks earnestly into the perfect law of liberty and continues to do so , and becomes not a forgetful hearer but a doer of work â that man will be blessed in what he does .
59001026	If any one thinks himself religious while he does not bridle his tongue , but deceives his own heart , that man's religion is worthless .
59001027	Pure and stainless religion in the sight of God the Father is to visit orphans and widows in their trouble and to keep one's self unspotted from the world .
59002001	MY brethren , do not hold the faith of our glorious Lord Jesus Christ with partiality for persons .
59002002	For if there comes into your assembly a man with gold rings and in fine clothes , and there comes in a poor man in soiled clothes ,
59002003	and you look up to the man who is wearing the fine clothes and say , " Take this good seat , " and say to the poor man , " Stand there , " or " Sit under my footstool , "
59002004	are you not making distinctions in your own minds and have you not become judges with wicked thoughts ?
59002005	Listen , my beloved brethren , did not God choose the poor of this world to be rich in faith and heirs of the kingdom which he has promised to those who love him ?
59002006	But you have dishonored the poor man . Do not the rich oppress you and drag you before courts ?
59002007	Do they not speak profanely of the noble name by which you are called ?
59002008	If you keep the royal law according to the Scripture , " Thou shalt love thy neighbor as thyself , " you do well .
59002009	But if you have partiality , you commit sin and are convicted by the law as law-breakers .
59002010	For he who keeps the whole law , but stumbles in one point , has become guilty of all .
59002011	For he who said , " Thou shalt not commit adultery , " said also , " Thou shalt not commit murder . " If you do not commit adultery , but do commit murder , you have become a law-breaker .
59002012	So speak and so act as those who are soon to be judged by a law of liberty .
59002013	For judgment is merciless to him who has shown no mercy . Mercy triumphs over judgment .
59002014	Of what use is it , my brethren , for any one to say that he has faith , if he has not works ? Can faith save him ?
59002015	If a brother or sister is naked and lacks food for the day
59002016	and one of you says to them , " Go in peace , be warmed and fed , " but you do not give them what the body needs , what is the good of it ?
59002017	Just so faith by itself , if it has no works , is dead .
59002018	But some one will say , " You have faith and I have works . Show me your faith without your works and I will show you my faith by my works . "
59002019	You have faith that there is one God . You do well . Even the demons have that faith , and they shudder .
59002020	Are you willing to learn , O vacant-minded man , that faith without works is useless ?
59002021	Was not Abraham , our father , pronounced righteous because of works when he laid Isaac his son on the altar ?
59002022	You see that faith worked with his works , and by works faith was made perfect
59002023	and the Scripture was fulfilled which says , " Abraham had faith in God and it was credited to him for righteousness " and he was called " God's friend . "
59002024	You see that a man is pronounced righteous because of works and not because of faith alone .
59002025	In the same way was not Rahab , the prostitute , pronounced righteous because of works when she had received the messengers and sent them out by a different road ?
59002026	For as the body without the spirit is dead , so faith without works is dead .
59003001	DO not , many of you , become teachers , my brethren , for you know that we will receive severer judgment .
59003002	For in many ways we all stumble . If any one never stumbles in his talk , he is a perfect man , able to bridle also the whole body .
59003003	If we put bits into the horses ' mouths to make them obey us , we turn about their whole bodies .
59003004	See the ships ; great as they are and driven by violent winds , they are turned about by a very small rudder wherever the desire of the helmsman chooses .
59003005	Just so the tongue is a small member , but boasts of great things . Think how small a fire may be and yet how vast the forest that it may set ablaze .
59003006	And the tongue is a fire , a world of wickedness . The tongue stands among our members as that which spots the whole body and sets on fire the wheel of nature and is itself set on fire by Gehenna .
59003007	For every kind of wild beasts and birds and reptiles and animals from the sea is tamed and has been tamed by human kind ,
59003008	but the tongue no man is able to tame . It is a restless evil ; it is full of deadly poison .
59003009	With it we bless the Lord our Father and with it we curse the men who are made in the image of God .
59003010	From the same mouth come blessing and cursing . This , my brethren , should not be so .
59003011	Does a spring pour out from the same opening sweet water and bitter ?
59003012	Can a fig tree , my brethren , bear olives , or a vine figs ? No more can salt water yield fresh water .
59003013	Who is wise and intelligent among you ? Let him show out of the noble life that he lives his works in wise gentleness .
59003014	But if you have bitter jealousy and party-spirit in your hearts , do not boast and falsely contradict the truth .
59003015	This wisdom does not come down from on high , but is earthly , animal , demoniacal .
59003016	For where jealousy and party-spirit are , there is confusion and every base affair .
59003017	But the wisdom from on high is first pure , then peaceable , fair-minded , easily persuaded , full of compassion and good fruits , impartial , sincere .
59003018	The fruit of righteousness is sown in peace by those who make peace .
59004001	WHENCE come wars and whence come strifes among you ? Is it not from your pleasures which carry on war in your members ?
59004002	You long for something and do not have it . You murder and envy and cannot obtain it . You battle and war . You do not have , because of your not asking .
59004003	You ask and do not receive , because you ask wickedly to waste it on your pleasures .
59004004	You adulteresses , do you not know that the friendship of the world is enmity to God ? Whoever chooses to be a friend to the world stands as an enemy of God .
59004005	Do you think that the Scripture speaks to no purpose ? Does the Spirit which he made dwell in us long enviously ?
59004006	But he gives greater grace . Therefore it says , " God opposes the proud , but gives grace to the humble . "
59004007	Submit yourselves , then , to God . Resist the Devil and he will flee from you .
59004008	Draw near to God and he will draw near to you . Make your hands clean , you sinners , and purify your hearts , you double-minded .
59004009	Be sorrowful and mourn and lament . Let your laughter be turned into grief and your gladness into gloom .
59004010	Humble yourselves before the Lord and he will exalt you .
59004011	Do not speak against one another , brethren . He who speaks against his brother speaks against the law and judges the law . But if you judge the law you are not a doer of the law , but a judge .
59004012	One is the Lawgiver and Judge â he who is able to save and to destroy . Who are you , to judge your neighbor ?
59004013	Come , now , you who say , " To-day or to-morrow we will go to such a city and spend a year and do business and make money , "
59004014	though you do not know what your life will be like on the morrow . For you are a vapor that appears for a little while and then disappears .
59004015	You should rather say , " If the Lord wills it , we shall live and do this or that . "
59004016	But now you glory in bragging . All such glorying is evil .
59004017	If any one , then , knows how to do good and is not doing it , he is committing sin .
59005001	COME , now , you rich men , wail and lament over the miseries that are coming upon you .
59005002	Your riches have rotted and your garments have become moth-eaten ,
59005003	your gold and silver are rusted over and the rust on them will be an evidence against you and will eat your flesh like fire .
59005004	You have laid up treasures in the last days . See , the wages of the laborers who reaped your fields , fraudulently kept back by you , call aloud , and the cries of the harvesters have come into the ears of the Lord of armies .
59005005	You have lived luxuriously in the land and have given yourselves up to pleasure . You have fattened your hearts in a day of slaughter .
59005006	You have condemned , you have murdered , the righteous ; he does not resist you .
59005007	Therefore be patient , brethren , until the coming of the Lord . See how the farmer waits for the precious fruit of the ground and is patient over it until he receives the early and the late rains .
59005008	You too must be patient . Keep your hearts steadfast , for the coming of the Lord is near .
59005009	Do not fret at one another , brethren , and then you will not be judged . The Judge is standing before your doors .
59005010	Take , brethren , the prophets who spoke in the name of the Lord as an example of patience in suffering evil .
59005011	We call them blessed because they endured . You have heard of the patience of Job and have seen the end of the Lord's dealings with him , that the Lord is very tender and compassionate .
59005012	Above all things , my brethren , do not swear , either by heaven or by the earth or by any other oath . Let your yes be yes and your no be no , that you may not fall under condemnation .
59005013	Is any one of you suffering hardship ? Let him pray . Is any one cheerful ? Let him sing with the harp .
59005014	Is any one of you sick ? Let him call in the elders of the church and let them pray over him and anoint him with olive oil in the name of the Lord .
59005015	The prayer of faith will save the sick and the Lord will raise him up , and if he has committed sins they will be forgiven him .
59005016	Confess your sins to one another and pray for one another in order to be healed . The effective prayer of a righteous man has great power .
59005017	Elijah was a man of the same weaknesses as ours , and he prayed earnestly that it might not rain and it did not rain on the land for three years and six months .
59005018	Then he prayed again and heaven gave rain and the land brought forth its fruits .
59005019	My brethren , if one of you strays from the truth and any one brings him back ,
59005020	I wish you to know that he who brings back a sinner from his wanderings will save his soul from death and will hide a host of sins .
60001001	PETER , an apostle of Jesus Christ , to the Chosen Ones of the scattered Jews in foreign lands who are living in Pontus , Galatia , Cappadocia , Asia and Bithynia â
60001002	chosen according to the foreknowledge of God the Father and made holy by the Spirit to obey Jesus Christ and be sprinkled with his blood : Grace be to you and peace be multiplied .
60001003	Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ , who according to his great mercy has given us a new birth into a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead â
60001004	a birth into an inheritance immortal , unstained and unfading , kept in heaven for you
60001005	who are guarded by the power of God through faith for the salvation which is ready to be revealed on the last day .
60001006	In this you rejoice , though now for a little while , if necessary , you are sorrowful in trials of many kinds ,
60001007	so that your tested faith , much more precious than gold that perishes though tested by fire , may be found to your praise and glory and honor when Jesus Christ is revealed ,
60001008	whom you love though you have not seen him ; in whom you have faith though now you do not see him , and you rejoice with unspeakable and glorious joy
60001009	while you receive the reward of your faith , the salvation of your souls .
60001010	Regarding this salvation the prophets who foretold the grace that was to come to you
60001011	inquired and searched , trying to find out what time , or what sort of time , the Spirit of Christ which was in them was disclosing when it witnessed beforehand regarding the sufferings of Christ and the glories to follow .
60001012	It was revealed to them that they were serving not themselves but you , in these things which now have been announced to you through those who have told you the good news by the Holy Spirit sent forth from heaven â things which angels earnestly long to look into .
60001013	Therefore brace up your minds , be calm and set your hope perfectly on the grace that is to be brought to you when Jesus Christ is revealed .
60001014	As obedient children , do not shape your lives by the passions that ruled you in the former days of ignorance ,
60001015	but , like the Holy One who has called you , become yourselves holy in all your way of life ,
60001016	for it is written , " You shall be holy because I am holy . "
60001017	And if you call upon him as Father who impartially judges by each one's work , live out the time of your sojourn here in reverence ,
60001018	for you know that you were not ransomed with perishable things , silver or gold , from your purposeless life handed down from your forefathers ,
60001019	but by precious blood , as of a faultless , spotless lamb , the blood of Christ ,
60001020	who was foreknown before the foundation of the world , but was manifested at the end of time for your sake
60001021	who through him are faithful to God , who raised him from the dead and gave him glory , so that your faith and hope are in God .
60001022	Now that you have made your souls holy by obedience to the truth for sincere brotherly love , you must love one another steadily from your hearts ,
60001023	for you have been reborn , not from mortal seed but from immortal by the living and enduring word of God .
60001024	For " All flesh is like grass and all its glory is like the flower of the grass ; the grass withers and the flower falls ,
60001025	but the word of the Lord endures forever . " And this is the word of good news that has been brought to you .
60002001	THEN lay aside all malice and all deceit and hypocrisy and envy and every kind of slander ,
60002002	and , like new-born babes , long for the reasonable pure milk , that by it you may grow up into salvation ,
60002003	if you have tasted that the Lord is kind .
60002004	Coming to him , a living stone , rejected by men but with the Lord chosen and precious ,
60002005	you also as living stones are built up , a spiritual house , and become a holy priesthood to offer spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ .
60002006	Therefore it is contained in Scripture , " See , I am laying in Zion a chosen stone , an honored corner stone . He who has faith in him will not be put to shame . "
60002007	To you who have faith is the " honor , " but to the unbelieving " the stone which the builders rejected â that has become the corner stone ,
60002008	a stone for the foot to strike , a rock to stumble over . " Their feet strike the message because of their unbelief , and to this they were destined .
60002009	But you are a chosen race , a kingly priesthood , a holy nation , God's own people , that you may proclaim the virtues of him who called you from darkness into his wonderful light .
60002010	Once you were not a people , but now you are the people of God : once you had not found compassion , but now you have found compassion .
60002011	Beloved , I beg you , as foreigners and resident aliens , to shun the passions of the flesh which war against the soul .
60002012	Keep your daily life among the Gentiles honorable , so that , although they talk against you as if you were wrongdoers , they may , from your noble deeds that they see , glorify God on the day of inspection .
60002013	Be submissive to every human institution for the Lord's sake , whether to the king as supreme ,
60002014	or to governors as those sent by him for the punishment of wrongdoers and the praise of those who do good .
60002015	For this is the will of God â that by doing good we shall silence the ignorance of thoughtless men .
60002016	Live as free men , yet not using freedom as a cloak for wickedness , but as God's slaves .
60002017	Honor all men , love the brotherhood , reverence God , honor the king .
60002018	Household servants , be submissive with all reverence to your lords , not only to the good and fair , but also to the surly .
60002019	For this is grace if for conscience toward God any one bears pain , suffering unjustly .
60002020	For what credit is it if when you sin and are struck with the fist you are patient ? But if though doing well , you suffer and are patient , that is grace in God's sight .
60002021	For to this you were called , because Christ too suffered for you , leaving you an example that you might follow in his foot-steps .
60002022	He had done no sin , nor was deceit found in his mouth .
60002023	When he was reviled he did not revile back ; he suffered , but made no threat ; he committed himself to him who judges justly .
60002024	He bore our sins in his own body on the tree that we might die to sins and live to righteousness .
60002025	For you were going astray like sheep , but have now returned to the shepherd and guardian of your souls .
60003001	IN the same way you wives are to be submissive to your own husbands , so that if any disbelieve the message they may be won over by the lives of their wives without argument ,
60003002	when they look at your pure , reverential behavior .
60003003	Your adornment must not be of the external kind â braiding the hair and putting on gold and wearing fine dresses ;
60003004	but the hidden personality of the heart must wear the imperishable beauty of a gentle and quiet spirit , which is in God's sight most precious .
60003005	For so of old the holy women who hoped in God adorned themselves . They were submissive to their own husbands ,
60003006	as Sarah obeyed Abraham and called him Master . You have become her children when you do well and feel no terror .
60003007	In the same way , you husbands must live with your wives wisely , since woman's sex is weaker , but you must give them honor as fellow heirs of the grace of life , so that your prayers may not be hindered .
60003008	Finally , all must be like-minded , sympathetic , full of brotherly love , compassionate , humble-minded ,
60003009	not repaying evil for evil or abuse for abuse , but rather blessing , for that is what you were called for â to inherit a blessing .
60003010	For " He who would love life and see good days must keep his tongue from evil and his lips from speaking deceit .
60003011	He must turn away from evil and do good ; he must seek peace and pursue it .
60003012	For the eyes of the Lord are upon the righteous and his ears are open to their prayer , but the face of the Lord is against wrongdoers . "
60003013	And who is it that will harm you if you become earnest for the good ?
60003014	But if you should suffer for being righteous , you are blessed . Have no fear of them and do not be disturbed ;
60003015	but exalt Christ as Lord in your hearts and be always ready to defend yourselves to every one who asks you to give account of the hope that is in you , yet with gentleness and reverence .
60003016	Keep a good conscience that , although you are slandered , those who misrepresent your good life in Christ may be put to shame .
60003017	For it is better to suffer , if that should be God's will , for doing good than for doing wrong .
60003018	For Christ once for all died for sins , a righteous man for unrighteous men , so that he might lead us to God . He was put to death in the flesh , but made alive in the spirit ,
60003019	in which he went and made proclamation to the imprisoned spirits
60003020	who were once disobedient , when the long-suffering of God waited in the days of Noah while the ark was being prepared , into which a few , that is eight souls , went and were saved through water .
60003021	This is a type of baptism , which now saves us â not the putting off of soil from the flesh , but the endeavor for a good conscience toward God through the resurrection of Jesus Christ .
60003022	Now that he has gone into heaven he is at the right hand of God , and angels and authorities and powers have been made subject to him .
60004001	SINCE , then , Christ suffered in the flesh , you also must arm yourselves with the same mind . For he who has suffered in the flesh has ceased from sin ,
60004002	so that he does not go on living what remains of his time in the flesh according to human passions , but according to God's will .
60004003	The time that has passed was enough to spend doing the will of the Gentiles , when you went on in indecencies , passions , hard drinking , revelries , carousings , and lawless idolatries .
60004004	In these they think it strange that you are not running with them to the same excess of profligacy , and they slander you .
60004005	But they will have to give account to him who holds himself ready to judge the living and the dead .
60004006	And for this purpose the good news was told even to the dead , that they might be judged like men in the flesh , but live as God does in the spirit .
60004007	The end of all things is near . Therefore be serious and sober and give yourselves to prayer .
60004008	Above all things have earnest love to one another , for love hides a host of sins .
60004009	Be hospitable to one another without grumbling .
60004010	Let each , as he has received a spiritual gift , serve the others in that way , as good stewards of the varied grace of God .
60004011	If any one speaks , let it be as uttering the oracles of God . If any one serves , let it be from the strength that God supplies . Thus in all things let God be glorified through Jesus Christ . To him be glory and strength for the ages of the ages ! Amen .
60004012	Beloved , do not be surprised at the fiery fury that is among you , which has come to try you , as if some strange thing were happening to you .
60004013	But rejoice since to this extent you are sharing the sufferings of Christ , that when his glory is revealed you may rejoice and exult .
60004014	If you are reproached for the name of Christ you are blessed , for the spirit of glory and of God rests upon you .
60004015	No one of you must suffer as a murderer or as a thief or as a wrongdoer or as a meddler in other men's affairs .
60004016	But if he suffers as a Christian he should not be ashamed , but should glorify God by that name .
60004017	For the time has come for judgment to begin at the house of God . And if it begins first with us , what will be the end of those who disobey the good news of God ?
60004018	If the righteous is saved with difficulty , where will the godless and sinful appear ?
60004019	So then let those who are suffering according to the will of God commit their souls in well-doing to a faithful Creator .
60005001	THE elders among you I beg â I who am a fellow elder and a witness to the sufferings of Christ and a sharer in the glory soon to be revealed â
60005002	I beg you to shepherd the flock of God that is among you , not because you must , but willingly , not for base gain , but eagerly ,
60005003	not lording it over your charges , but becoming examples to the flock .
60005004	Then when the chief Shepherd appears you will be repaid with the never-fading crown of glory .
60005005	In the same way you younger men must be subject to your elders . You all must put on the apron of humble service for one another . For God opposes the proud , but gives grace to the humble .
60005006	Humble yourselves , then , under the mighty hand of God so that he may lift you up at the right time .
60005007	Cast all your anxiety on him , for he cares for you .
60005008	Be sober , watch . Your enemy the Devil , like a roaring lion , goes about seeking some one to devour .
60005009	Resist him firm in the faith and knowing that the same experiences of suffering are being completed in your brotherhood throughout the world .
60005010	The God of all grace , who called you to his eternal glory in Christ , after you have suffered a little will equip , establish and strengthen you .
60005011	To him be power for the ages of the ages ! Amen .
60005012	By Silvanus , your faithful brother , as I esteem him , I am writing to you briefly , to encourage you and to testify that this is the true grace of God . Take your stand in it .
60005013	She who is in Babylon , chosen with you , sends her greeting to you , and so does Mark my son .
60005014	Salute one another with a kiss of love . Peace be to you all in Christ .
61001001	SIMON PETER , a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ , to those who by the righteousness of our God and Savior Jesus Christ have been allotted a faith as precious as ours :
61001002	Grace be to you and peace be multiplied in the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord .
61001003	Since his divine power has given us all things helpful to life and piety through the knowledge of him who has called us by his own glory and virtue ,
61001004	and thereby great and precious promises have been granted to us , that through them you may escape the corruption that is in the world through passion and become sharers in the divine nature ,
61001005	for this very reason make it your whole endeavor to supply to your faith virtue , and to your virtue knowledge ,
61001006	and to your knowledge self-control , and to your self-control endurance , and to your endurance reverence ,
61001007	and to your reverence brotherliness , and to your brotherliness love .
61001008	For when you have these in abundance they make you to be neither idle nor fruitless regarding the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ .
61001009	But he who lacks these is blind , dim-sighted , and has forgotten that he was cleansed from his former sins .
61001010	Therefore endeavor more earnestly , brethren , to make sure that you have been called and chosen . For while doing these things you will never stumble .
61001011	For so entrance into the eternal kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ will be richly provided for you .
61001012	For this reason I shall always keep reminding you of these things , although you know them and are steadfast in the truth that you have .
61001013	I think it right so long as I am in this tent to arouse you by reminding you ,
61001014	since I know that the laying aside of my tent will come soon , as our Lord Jesus Christ has made plain to me .
61001015	I will endeavor also on every occasion to make it so that after my going you shall have these things in memory .
61001016	For we were not following cunningly devised myths when we told you of the power and coming of our Lord Jesus Christ , but we had been eye-witnesses of his majesty .
61001017	For he received from God the Father honor and glory when such words as these were borne to him from the majestic glory , " This is my Son , the Beloved ; in him I delight . "
61001018	And this voice we heard borne from heaven when we were with him on the holy mountain .
61001019	Thus have we the words of the prophets confirmed , and you will do well to give attention to them as to a lamp shining in a dark place , until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts ;
61001020	since you know this first , that no prophecy of Scripture comes from any one's private interpretation ,
61001021	for prophecy never came by the will of man , but men spoke from God as they were moved by the Holy Spirit .
61002001	BUT false prophets also arose among the people , just as there will be false teachers among yourselves , and they will craftily bring in deadly heresies , even disowning the Lord who bought them and bringing on themselves quick ruin .
61002002	Many will follow their shameless ways and by these the path of truth will be profanely spoken of .
61002003	In covetousness they will make gain out of you by their cunning words . But their condemnation from of old has not been inactive , and their destruction has not been sleeping .
61002004	For if God did not spare angels that had sinned , but thrust them down to Tartarus and committed them to pits of darkness to be kept for judgment ,
61002005	and did not spare the ancient world , but guarded Noah , a herald of righteousness , and seven others , when he brought the flood on the world of the ungodly ;
61002006	and if reducing to ashes the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah he condemned them to destruction , making them an example for the godless of what would come upon them ,
61002007	and rescued righteous Lot worn out by the indecent lives of the lawless , â
61002008	for that righteous man living among them was tortured day and night in his righteous soul by the sight and hearing of their lawless deeds , â
61002009	the Lord knows how to rescue the pious from trial and how to keep the wicked under punishment for the day of judgment ,
61002010	especially those who go after flesh in polluting passions , and despise lordship . They are daring , self-willed ; they do not tremble to speak insultingly of glorious beings
61002011	even where angels greater in strength and power do not bring against them an insulting charge before the Lord .
61002012	But they , like irrational creatures , born mere animals for capture and destruction , while speaking profanely of things they are ignorant of , will be corrupted by their own corruption ,
61002013	and will suffer unrighteously as the reward of their own unrighteousness . They think it pleasure to revel in the daytime . They are spots and blots as they revel in their deceptions while they feast sumptuously with you .
61002014	They have eyes engrossed with some adulteress , eyes which never cease from sin . They seduce unsteady souls . They have hearts practiced in covetousness . They are children of a curse .
61002015	Leaving the straight path they have wandered away following the path of Balaam the son of Beor , who loved the wages of unrighteousness .
61002016	But he was reproved for his sin ; a dumb beast of draught , speaking with human voice , checked the madness of the prophet .
61002017	These men are springs without water , storm-driven mists for whom the blackness of darkness is reserved .
61002018	For by speaking great empty swelling words they entrap in the passions of the flesh â wanton excesses â those who are nearly escaping from those who live in error .
61002019	While they promise them liberty they themselves are the slaves of corruption ; for by whatever any one is overcome to that he is enslaved .
61002020	For if , after they have escaped the defilement of the world by the knowledge of the Lord and Savior Jesus Christ , they have been again entangled and overcome , their last state has become worse than the first .
61002021	For it would be better for them not to have known the way of righteousness than after knowing it to turn back from the holy commandment that has been committed to them .
61002022	That has happened to them which the true proverb says , " The dog returns to his own vomit and the sow after bathing returns to wallowing in the mire . "
61003001	THIS second letter , beloved , I am writing you . In both I have tried , by awakening your memory ,
61003002	to arouse your honest minds to recall the predictions of the holy prophets and the commands of your apostles from the Lord and Savior .
61003003	First you should know this , that in the last days scoffers will come with their scoffing , living according to their own passions
61003004	and saying , " Where is his promised coming ? for since the fathers fell asleep all things remain as they have been since the beginning of the creation ? "
61003005	For they willfully forget that there were heavens of old and an earth formed out of water and through water by God's word .
61003006	By these means the world that then was was flooded with water and destroyed .
61003007	But the present heavens and the earth are by the same word treasured up and kept for fire on the day of judgment and destruction of ungodly men .
61003008	Do not forget this one thing , beloved , that one day with the Lord is like a thousand years and a thousand years are like one day .
61003009	The Lord is not slow about what he has promised , as some think of slowness , but is long-suffering toward us , wishing not to have any perish but to have all come to a change of heart .
61003010	But the day of the Lord will come like a thief . On that day the heavens will pass away with a loud noise and the burning elements will be dissolved and the earth and the things in it will not be found .
61003011	Since all of these things are to be dissolved , what sort of persons ought you to be in holy lives and piety ,
61003012	you who are looking for and hastening toward the coming of the day of God , when the blazing heavens will be dissolved and the burning elements melted ?
61003013	But according to his promise we are expecting new heavens and a new earth in which righteousness will dwell .
61003014	Therefore , beloved , since you expect this , endeavor earnestly to be found by him in peace , spotless and faultless ,
61003015	and regard the long-suffering of our Lord as salvation , as also our beloved brother Paul has written to you , according to the wisdom given to him .
61003016	So he writes in all his letters when speaking in them of these things . In those letters are some things hard to understand , and these the unlearned and unsteady twist , as they do the rest of the Scriptures , to their own ruin .
61003017	You , then , beloved , since you know these things beforehand , be on your guard not to be led away by the error of the lawless and fall from your own steadfastness ,
61003018	but grow in grace and in knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ . To him be glory now and to the day of eternity !
62001001	WHAT was from the beginning , what we have heard , what we have seen with our eyes , what we looked upon and our hands touched â it is about the Word of Life
62001002	
62001003	what wo have seen and heard we are telling you also , so that you may have fellowship with us . And our fellowship is with the Father and with his Son Jesus Christ .
62001004	We are writing this that our joy may be complete .
62001005	This is the message which we have heard from him and tell to you , God is light and in him is no darkness at all .
62001006	If we say , " We have fellowship with him , " and live in darkness , we lie and are not acting the truth .
62001007	If we live in the light , as he is in the light , we have fellowship with one another and the blood of Jesus his Son cleanses us from all sin .
62001008	If we say , " We have no sin , " we deceive ourselves and the truth is not in us .
62001009	If we confess our sins , he is faithful and just to forgive us our sins and cleanse us from all unrighteousness :
62001010	If we say , " We have not sinned , " we make him a liar and his message is not in us .
62002001	MY children , I am writing this to you in order that you may not sin . Even if any one sins , we have an advocate with the Father , Jesus Christ , who is righteous .
62002002	And he is an atoning sacrifice for our sins , and not for ours only but for those of the whole world .
62002003	By this we know that we have come to know him , if we keep his commands .
62002004	He who says , " I know him , " and does not keep his commands , is a liar and truth is not in him .
62002005	But whoever keeps his word , truly in him the love of God has been made perfect . By this we know that we are in him .
62002006	He who says that he is abiding in him ought himself to live as he lived .
62002007	Beloved , I am not writing a new command for you , but an old command , which you have had from the beginning . The old command is the message that you have heard .
62002008	Again I am writing a new command , which is true in him and in you , because the darkness is passing away and the true Light is already shining .
62002009	He who says that he is in the light and hates his brother is in darkness still .
62002010	He who loves his brother remains in the light and there is no stumbling block in him .
62002011	He who hates his brother is in darkness and walks in darkness and knows not where he is going , because the darkness has blinded his eyes .
62002012	I am writing to you , little children , because your sins have been forgiven for his name's sake .
62002013	I am writing to you , fathers , because you have come to know him who has been from the beginning . I am writing to you , young men , because you have conquered the Evil One . I have written to you , little children , because you have come to know the Father .
62002014	I have written to you , fathers , because you have come to know him who has been from the beginning . I have written to you , young men , because you are strong and the message of God remains in you and you have conquered the Evil One .
62002015	Do not love the world nor the things that are in the world . If any one loves the world , the love of the Father is not in him ;
62002016	for all that is in the world , the passions of the flesh and the lust of the eyes and the show and pride of life , is not from the Father , but from the world .
62002017	And the world is passing away with its passions . But he who does the will of God endures forever .
62002018	Little children , it is the last hour , and as you have heard that Antichrist is coming , even now many Antichrists have arisen . By this we know that it is the last hour .
62002019	They went out from us , but they were not of us , for if they had been of us they would have continued with us . But they went out so that it might be plainly seen that not all are of us .
62002020	You have an anointing from the Holy One and you all know .
62002021	I am not writing to you because you do not know the truth , but because you know it and know that no lie is from the truth .
62002022	Who is a liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ ? He is the Antichrist who denies the Father and the Son .
62002023	No one who denies the Son has the Father either . He who confesses the Son has the Father also .
62002024	Let what you have heard from the beginning remain in you . If what you have heard from the beginning remains in you , you also will remain in the Son and in the Father .
62002025	And this is the promise that he has promised us â the life eternal .
62002026	I am writing this to you in regard to those who are misleading you .
62002027	But as for you , the anointing that you have received from him remains in you and you have no need for any one to teach you , but as his anointing teaches you about all things and is true and is no lie and as it has taught you , you must remain in him .
62002028	And now , little children , remain in him so that if he appears we may have confidence and not shrink in shame from him at his coming .
62002029	If you know that he is righteous , you know that every one who does righteousness has been born of him .
62003001	SEE what love the Father has bestowed on us that we should be called children of God . And so we are . The reason why tho world does not know us is that it did not know him .
62003002	Beloved , we are now children of God and it is not yet plain what we shall be . But we know that if he appears we shall be like him , for we shall see him as he is .
62003003	And every one who has this hope set upon Christ purifies himself just as Christ is pure .
62003004	Every one who commits sin commits also lawlessness ; for sin is lawlessness .
62003005	You know that Christ appeared to take away sins and in him there is no sin .
62003006	Whoever remains in him does not sin ; whoever sins has not seen him nor known him .
62003007	Little children , let no one deceive you . He who is doing righteousness is righteous as Christ is righteous .
62003008	He who is committing sin is of the Devil , for the Devil has been sinning from the beginning . For this the Son of God appeared â to undo the works of the Devil .
62003009	No one who has been born of God commits sin , for God's life-giving germ remains in him and he cannot continue sinning , because he has been born of God .
62003010	By this the children of God are plain to see , also the children of the Devil . Every one who is not doing righteousness is not of God , nor is he who does not love his brother .
62003011	For this is the message which you have heard from the beginning , that we must love one another .
62003012	Not like Cain , who was of the Wicked One and killed his brother . And for what reason did he kill him ? Because his own deeds were wicked and his brother's righteous .
62003013	Do not be surprised , brethren , if the world hates you .
62003014	We know that we have passed from death into life because we love the brethren . Whoever does not love remains in death .
62003015	Every one who hates his brother is a murderer , and you know that no murderer has life eternal remaining in him .
62003016	By this we have come to know love â that Christ laid down his life for us , and we ought to lay down our lives for the brethren .
62003017	But if any one has this world's goods and sees his brother in need and shuts away his sympathies from him , how can the love of God remain in him ?
62003018	Let us not love in word or in tongue , but in deed and in truth .
62003019	By this we shall know that we are of the truth and shall give confidence to our hearts in his presence ,
62003020	because if our hearts condemn us God is greater than our hearts and knows all things .
62003021	Beloved , if our hearts do not condemn us we have confidence toward God ,
62003022	and whatever we ask we receive from him , because we keep his commands and do what is pleasing in his sight .
62003023	And this is his command â to believe in the name of his Son Jesus Christ and love one another as he has given us command .
62003024	He who keeps his commands remains in God and God remains in him . By this we know that God remains in us â by the Spirit which he has given to us .
62004001	BELOVED , do not trust every spirit , but test the spirits whether they are from God . For many false prophets have come out into the world .
62004002	By this we know the Spirit of God : every spirit that confesses that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is from God ,
62004003	and no spirit that does not confess Jesus is from God . This is the spirit of Antichrist , which you have heard is coming into the world and is already in the world .
62004004	But you are of God , little children , and have conquered them , because he who is in us is greater than he who is in the world .
62004005	They belong to the world and for that reason they speak as the world speaks and the world listens to them .
62004006	We are of God . Whoever knows God listens to us : whoever is not of God does not listen to us . In this way we know the spirit of truth and the spirit of error .
62004007	Beloved , let us love one another , for love is from God , and every one who loves has been born of God and knows God .
62004008	He who does not love does not know God ; for God is love .
62004009	By this the love of God to us was made plain : that God sent his only Son into the world so that we may have life through him .
62004010	In this is love â not that we loved God , but that he loved us and sent his Son to be an atoning sacrifice for our sins .
62004011	Beloved , if God has so loved us , we ought also to love one another .
62004012	No one has ever seen God . If we love one another God abides in us and his love is made perfect in us .
62004013	By this we know that we abide in him and he in us , because he has imparted to us of his Spirit .
62004014	We have seen and we bear witness that the Father has sent the Son to be the Savior of the world .
62004015	Whoever confesses that Jesus is the Son of God , God abides in him and he in God .
62004016	We have come to know and have put our trust in the love which God has for us . God is love , and he who remains in love remains in God and God remains in him .
62004017	Thus love has been made perfect with us so that we may have confidence on the day of judgment , because as God is we also are in this world .
62004018	There is no fear in love , but perfect love casts out fear , because fear has pain . He who fears has not been made perfect in love .
62004019	We love because he first loved us .
62004020	If any one says , " I love God , " and hates his brother , he is a liar . For he who does not love his brother whom he has seen cannot love God whom he has not seen .
62004021	This command we have from him , that he who loves God shall love his brother also .
62005001	EVERY one who believes that Jesus is the Christ has been born of God , and every one who loves the father who gave him life loves every one who has received life from that father .
62005002	By this we know that we love the children of God , when we love God and do his commands .
62005003	For this is the love of God , our keeping his commands . And his commands are not burden-some ,
62005004	because all that is born of God conquers the world . And this is the victory that conquers the world , our faith .
62005005	Who is the conqueror of the world but he who believes that Jesus is the Son of God ?
62005006	This is he who came through water and blood , Jesus Christ . Not with the water only , but with the water and the blood . And the Spirit is the witness , because the Spirit is the truth .
62005008	For there are three that bear witness , the Spirit and the water and the blood , and the three are in accord .
62005009	If we accept the testimony of men the testimony of God is greater ; for this is God's testimony , that he has testified regarding his Son .
62005010	He who believes in the Son of God has the testimony within himself . He who does not believe God has made him a liar ; because he has not believed the testimony which God has borne regarding his Son .
62005011	This is the testimony : that God has given to us life eternal and this life is in his Son .
62005012	He who has the Son has life ; he who has not the Son of God has not life .
62005013	I am writing this to you so that you may know that you have life eternal , you who believe in the name of the Son of God .
62005014	This is the confidence that we have toward him : that if we ask anything according to his will he hears us .
62005015	And if we know that he hears us when we ask anything , we know that we obtain the things that we have asked of him .
