62005016	If any one sees his brother committing a sin that is not deadly , he must ask and God will give him life for those who are committing sin that is not deadly . There is sin that is deadly . I do not say that he should pray in behalf of that .
62005017	All unrighteousness is sin , and there is sin that is not deadly .
62005018	We know that every one who has been born of God lives without sinning , but he who was born of God keeps him , and the Evil One does not lay hold of him .
62005019	We know that we are of God and the whole world lies in the Evil One .
62005020	We know that the Son of God has come and has given us understanding to know him who is true , and we are in him who is true and in his Son , Jesus Christ . This is the true God and life eternal .
62005021	Little children , guard yourselves from idols .
63001001	THE Elder to the chosen Lady and her children , whom I love in truth
63001002	for the sake of the truth which remains in us and will be with us forever :
63001003	Grace , mercy , and peace will be with us from God the Father and from Jesus Christ , the Son of the Father , in truth and love .
63001004	I rejoiced greatly to find some of your children living in truth , as we received command from the Father .
63001005	And now I pray you , Lady , not as if writing a new command for you , but one that we have had from the beginning , let us love one another .
63001006	This is love : to live by his commands . This is the command , as you heard from the beginning that you must live by it .
63001007	For many deceivers have come out into the world and they do not confess that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh . Such a one is the deceiver and the Antichrist .
63001008	Guard yourselves so as not to lose what we have worked for , but so that you may gain a full reward .
63001009	Every one who goes forward and does not remain in the teaching of Christ is without God . He who remains in the teaching , he has the Father and the Son .
63001010	If any one comes to you and does not bring this teaching , do not take him into your house and do not bid him welcome .
63001011	He who bids him welcome becomes a sharer in his wicked works .
63001012	I have much to write to you , but I will not do it with paper and ink . I hope to be with you soon and to speak face to face so that our joy may be complete .
63001013	The children of your chosen sister send greetings to you .
64001001	THE Elder to Gaius the beloved , whom I love in truth :
64001002	Beloved , I pray that in everything you may prosper and be in health , just as your soul now prospers .
64001003	For I rejoiced greatly when brethren came and testified to your truth â that you are living in the truth .
64001004	I have no greater joy than this : to hear that my children are living in the truth .
64001005	Beloved , you do faithfully whatever work you do for the brethren , even when they are strangers ,
64001006	and they have testified to your love before the church . You will do well to help them forward on their journey in a manner worthy of God .
64001007	For it was for the Name that they came out , taking nothing from the Gentiles .
64001008	We ought to help such men so as to be fellow workers with the truth .
64001009	I wrote something to the church ; but Diotrephes , who desires to be first among them , does not receive us .
64001010	Therefore , if I come I will bring to mind the works that he is doing , accusing us with wicked words , and not satisfied with that , neither does he receive the brethren , and he hinders those who wish to do so and expels them from the church .
64001011	Beloved , do not imitate evil , but good . He who does good is of God . He who does evil has not seen God .
64001012	Testimony has been borne to Demetrius by all and by the truth itself . We too bear testimony , and you know that our testimony is true .
64001013	I had much to write to you , but I will not write to you with ink and pen .

65001001	JUDE , a servant of Jesus Christ and a brother of James , to those who are in God the Father , beloved , kept for Jesus Christ and called :
65001002	Mercy and peace and love be multiplied to you .
65001003	Beloved , although I have been making every effort to write to you regarding our common salvation , I now find it necessary to write and urge you to contend vigorously for the faith that was once for all delivered to the holy .
65001004	For certain persons have crept in , who of old were written of as predestined to this doom , godless , changing the grace of our God into profligacy and disowning our only Ruler and Lord , Jesus Christ .
65001005	I wish to remind you , although you know all things once for all , that the Lord , after saving a people from the land of Egypt , then destroyed those who had no faith ;
65001006	and angels who did not keep their own rank , but left their own abode , he has kept for the judgment of the great day in everlasting chains under blackness of darkness .
65001007	So Sodom and Gomorrah , and the cities around them , which in the same way gave themselves up to unchastity and the pursuit of unnatural vices , serve as an example while they undergo the punishment of eternal fire .
65001008	Just so these dreamers defile the flesh , reject government , and speak abusively of glorious beings .
65001009	But Michael , the arch-angel , when in dispute with the Devil he was arguing about the body of Moses , did not venture to bring against him an abusive judgment , but said , " The Lord rebuke you . "
65001010	But these speak profanely of whatever they do not know , and all that physically as irrational animals they do understand , in these things they corrupt themselves .
65001011	Alas for them ! for they have traveled in the path of Cain , and for hire have rushed headlong into the error of Balaam , and have perished in the rebellious talk of Korah .
65001012	These are the hidden reefs in your love-feasts while they feast freely with you without fear , shepherds who care only for themselves , waterless clouds driven by winds , trees in autumn fruitless , twice dead , uprooted ,
65001013	wild waves of the sea foaming out their own shame , wandering stars for which the blackness of darkness is reserved forever .
65001014	Enoch , the seventh from Adam , prophesied of these men when he said , " See , the Lord has come with ten thousand of his holy ones
65001015	to do judgment upon all and to convict all the irreverent of all their deeds of irreverence which they have irreverently done , and of all the hard things which they have spoken against him , irreverent sinners that they are . "
65001016	These men are complaining grumblers , living according to their own passions , and their mouths speak great swelling words . They show admiration for persons for the sake of their own gain .
65001017	But you , beloved , remember the words which were long ago spoken by the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ ,
65001018	how they told you that in the latter time there would be scoffers living according to their own ungodly passions .
65001019	These are those who cause divisions , sensual and unspiritual .
65001020	But you , beloved , building yourselves up in your most holy faith and praying in the Holy Spirit ,
65001021	must keep yourselves in the love of God , looking for the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ to bring you into life eternal .
65001022	On some have pity when they are in doubt ;
65001023	pull them out of the fire and save them . Others pity with fear , hating even the tunic spotted by the flesh .
65001024	To him who is able to guard you from falling and to make you stand faultless before his glory in great joy ,
65001025	to the only God our Savior , be , through Jesus Christ our Lord , glory , majesty , might , and authority , before all time and now and for all the ages ! Amen .

66008007	The first sounded his trumpet and there came hail and fire mixed with blood , and it was hurled upon the earth . A third of the earth was burned up and a third of the trees were burned up and all green grass was burned up .
66008008	The second angel sounded his trumpet and , as it were , a great mountain burning with fire was hurled into the sea . A third of the sea became blood
66008009	and a third of the creatures in the sea , those that had life , died , and a third of the ships were destroyed .
66008010	The third angel sounded his trumpet and there fell from heaven a great star burning like a torch . It fell upon a third of the rivers and upon the springs of water .
66008011	The name of the star is called Wormwood . Then a third of the waters became worm-wood , and many people died from the waters because they had been made bitter .
66008012	The fourth angel sounded his trumpet and a blight fell upon a third part of the sun and a third part of the moon and a third part of the stars , so that a third part of them was darkened , and the day had no light for a third part of it , and the night was darkened in the same way .
66008013	Then I looked and I heard an eagle that was flying in mid-heaven say with a loud voice , " Woe , woe , woe to those who are living on the earth , because of the rest of the trumpet-blasts which the three angels are soon to sound ! "
66009001	THE fifth angel sounded his trumpet and I saw a star that had fallen from heaven to the earth . There was given to him the key of the pit of the abyss .
66009002	And he opened the pit of the abyss and smoke came up from the pit like the smoke of a great furnace , and the sun was darkened and the air also by the smoke of the pit .
66009003	Out of the smoke came locusts upon the earth , and power was given to them such as earthly scorpions have .
66009004	It was said to them that they should not harm the grass of the earth nor anything green nor any tree , but only the people that did not have the seal of God on their foreheads .
66009005	It was not granted to them to kill such , but to torment them five months . Their torture was like the torture of a scorpion when it strikes a man .
66009006	In those days men will seek for death and will not find it and will long to die , but death will fly from them .
66009007	The appearance of the locusts was like that of horses equipped for battle . On their heads were , as it were , crowns like gold , and their faces were like human faces .
66009008	They had hair like the hair of women . Their teeth were like those of lions .
66009009	They had breastplates like breastplates of iron . The noise of their wings was like the noise of many-horsed chariots rushing into battle .
66009010	They have tails as scorpions have , and stings , and with their tails they have power to harm men five months .
66009011	They have over them a king , the angel of the abyss , whose name is in Hebrew Abaddon , but in Greek Apollyon .
66009012	One woe has passed . Two woes are still to come .
66009013	The sixth angel sounded his trumpet and I heard a voice from the horns of the golden altar before God
66009014	saying to the sixth angel with the trumpet , " Loose the four angels that are chained at the great river Euphrates . "
66009015	So the four angels were loosed , they who were prepared for the hour and day and month and year to kill a third of men .
66009016	The number of the troops of cavalry was twice ten thousand times ten thousand . I heard their number .
66009017	This is how the horses and those who sat on them appeared to me in the vision : The riders had breastplates , fiery red , dark blue , and sulphur yellow . The heads of the horses were like the heads of lions , and from their mouths came fire and smoke and sulphur .
66009018	By these three plagues a third of men were killed â by the fire and the smoke and the sulphur that came out of their mouths .
66009019	For the power of the horses is in their mouths and in their tails . For their tails are like serpents with heads , and with these they do injury .
66009020	But the rest of men , who were not killed by these plagues , neither repented of the deeds of their hands nor ceased worshiping the demons and their idols of gold and silver and brass and stone and wood , which can neither see nor hear nor walk ,
66009021	nor did they repent of their murders nor of their magic nor of their unchastities nor of their thefts .
66010001	THEN I saw another strong angel descending from heaven . He was clothed in a cloud and the rainbow was over his head . His face was like the sun and his legs were like pillars of fire .
66010002	He had in his hand a little book open . He set his right foot on the sea and his left on the land
66010003	and shouted with a loud voice like the roar of a lion . When he had shouted the seven thunders spoke , each its own message .
66010004	When the seven thunders had spoken I was about to write . But I heard a voice from heaven saying , " Seal up what the seven thunders have spoken and do not write it . "
66010005	Then the angel whom I had seen standing on the sea and on the land lifted his right hand to heaven
66010006	and swore by him who lives for the ages of the ages , who formed heaven and all things in it and the earth and all things upon it and the sea and all things in it , " There shall be no more delay ,
66010007	but in the days of the blast of the seventh angel , when he soon shall sound his trumpet , then the mystery of God has been finished , according to the good news that he gave to his servants the prophets . "
66010008	Then the voice which I had heard from heaven spoke again with me and said , " Go , take the little book which is open in the hand of the angel who is standing on the sea and on the land . "
66010009	So I went to the angel and told him to give me the little book . He said to me , " Take it and eat it . It will make your stomach bitter , though in your mouth it will be sweet like honey . "
66010010	I took the little book from the hand of the angel and ate it , and in my mouth it was sweet like honey , but after I had eaten it my stomach was made bitter .

66019015	From his mouth issues a sharp sword to smite the nations . He will shepherd them with a rod of iron , and he treads the winepress of the fierce wrath of God Almighty .
66019016	He has on his robe and on his thigh a name written , " King of kings and Lord of lords . "
66019017	Then I saw one angel standing on the sun , and he shouted with a loud voice , saying to all the birds that fly in mid-heaven , " Come , gather for the great feast of God ,
66019018	to eat the flesh of kings and the flesh of generals and the flesh of mighty men , and the flesh of horses and of those who sit on them , and the flesh of freemen and of slaves , of small and great . "
66019019	Then I saw the Beast and the kings of the earth and their armies gathered to do battle with him who sits on the horse and with his army .
66019020	And the Beast was captured and with him the False Prophet who did miracles in his presence and thereby misled those who received the mark of the Beast and who worshiped his image . The two were flung alive into the lake of fire that burns with brimstone .
66019021	The rest were slain with the sword of him who sits upon the horse , the sword that issued from his mouth , and all the birds were gorged with their flesh .
66020001	THEN I saw an angel descending from heaven with the key of the abyss and a great chain in his hand .
66020002	He laid hold of the Dragon , the ancient Serpent , who is the Devil and Satan , and chained him for a thousand years
66020003	and flung him into the abyss and shut it and sealed it over him , so that he should not mislead the nations until the thousand years were ended . After that he must be loosed for a little while .
66020004	Then I saw thrones , and men took their seats on them and the power to judge was granted to them . I saw the souls of those who had been beheaded for their testimony to Jesus and for God's message , and who had not worshiped the Beast nor his image and had not received his mark on their foreheads or on their hands . They lived and reigned as kings with Christ a thousand years ,
66020005	but the rest of the dead did not return to life until the thousand years were finished . This is the first resurrection .
66020006	Blessed and holy is he who has part in the first resurrection ! Over these the second death has no power , but they will be priests and kings of God and of Christ , and will reign with him the thousand years .
66020007	When the thousand years are ended , Satan will be loosed from his prison
66020008	and will come out to mislead the nations that are at the four corners of the earth â Gog and Magog â and gather them to battle in number like the sand of the sea .
66020009	They went up over the breadth of the earth and encircled the camp of the holy and the beloved city . But fire fell from heaven and consumed them ,
66020010	and the Devil who was misleading them was flung into the lake of fire and brimstone , where are also the Beast and the False Prophet , and they will be tormented day and night for the ages of the ages .
66020011	Then I saw a great white throne and him who was sitting on it , from whose face earth and heaven fled away and no place was found for them .
66020012	And I saw the dead , the great and the small , standing before the throne , and books were opened . And another book was opened which is the Book of Life . The dead were judged out of what was written in the books according to their deeds .
66020013	The sea gave up the dead that were in it , and Death and Hades gave up the dead that were in them , and they were judged each according to his deeds .
66020014	Death and Hades were flung into the lake of fire . This is the second death â the lake of fire .
66020015	If any one was not found written in the Book of Life he was flung into the lake of fire .
66021001	THEN I saw a new heaven and a new earth , for the first heaven and the first earth had passed away and the sea was no more .
66021002	I saw the holy city , new Jerusalem , descending out of heaven from God , prepared as a bride adorned for her husband .
66021003	And I heard a loud voice from the throne saying , " The Tent of God is with men . He will tent with them and they will be his people and he will be their God .
66021004	He will wipe every tear from their eyes . Death shall be no more ; neither shall there any longer be sorrow or wailing or painful toil ; for the first things have passed away . "
66021005	He who was sitting on the throne said , " See , I am making all things new . " He said , " Write ; for these words are trustworthy and true . "
66021006	He said to me , " They have come to pass . I am the Alpha and the Omega , the beginning and the end . To him who is thirsting I will give from the spring of the water of life freely .
66021007	He who conquers shall inherit all things , and I will be his God and he shall be to me a son .
66021008	But the timid and faithless and abominable and murderers and the unchaste and sorcerers and idolaters and all liars will have their lot in the lake that burns with fire and brimstone , which is the second death . "
66021009	Then one of the angels that had the seven bowls filled with the seven last plagues came and spoke with me . " Come here , " he said , " and I will show you the Bride , the Lamb's wife . "
66021010	Then he carried me in Spirit to the top of a great and high mountain and showed me the holy city Jerusalem descending out of heaven from God ,
66021011	having the glory of God . Her brilliance was like that of a most precious stone , like crystalline jasper .
66021012	She had a wall great and high , and she had twelve gates and at the gates twelve angels , and there were names written upon the gates . They are the names of the twelve tribes of the sons of Israel .
66021013	On the east were three gates and on the north three gates and on the south three gates and on the west three gates .
66021014	The wall of the city had twelve foundations and upon them were twelve names , the names of the twelve apostles of the Lamb .
66021015	He who was speaking with me had a golden reed as a measure , to measure the city and her gates and her wall .
66021016	The city stands foursquare and the length is the same as the breadth . He measured the city with the reed . It extends twelve thousand furlongs . The length and the breadth and the height of it are equal .
66021017	He measured the wall of it , a hundred and forty-four cubits by human measure , which is also that of an angel .
66021018	The material of the wall of it was jasper and the city was pure gold like clear glass .
66021019	The foundations of the wall of the city were decorated with every kind of precious stone . The first foundation was jasper , the second sapphire , the third chalcedony , the fourth emerald ,
66021020	the fifth sardonyx , the sixth sardius , the seventh chrysolite , the eighth beryl , the ninth topaz , the tenth chrysoprase , the eleventh jacinth , the twelfth amethyst .
66021021	The twelve gates were twelve pearls . Each one of the gates was of one pearl . The street of the city was pure gold like transparent glass .
66021022	I saw no temple in it ; for its temple is the Lord God the Almighty and the Lamb .
66021023	And the city has no need of the sun or of the moon to shine in it ; for the glory of God illumines it and the Lamb is its light .
66021024	The nations will walk by its light and the kings of the earth will bring their glory into it ,
66021025	and its gates will not be closed by day , and there will be no night there .
66021026	They will bring the glory and honor of the nations into it .
66021027	But there will not enter into it anything unholy or any one who makes an abomination or a lie , but only those who are written in the Lamb's Book of Life .
66022001	THEN he showed me a river of water of life bright as crystal , issuing from the throne of God and of the Lamb .
66022002	In the space between the street and the river , on this side and on that , grew trees of life bearing twelve kinds of fruit , and yielding their fruit every month . The leaves of the tree were for the healing of the nations .
66022003	There will no longer be any accursed thing . The throne of God and of the Lamb will be in it and his servants will worship him with holy rites .
66022004	They will see his face and his name will be on their foreheads .
66022005	There will not be night any more and they will have no need of lamplight or of sunlight ; for the Lord God will shine upon them and they will be kings for the ages of the ages .
66022006	Then he said to me , " These words are trustworthy and true . The Lord God of the spirits of the prophets has sent his angel to show to his servants what must soon come to pass .
66022007	I am coming soon . Blessed is he who is keeping the words of the prophecy of this book . "
66022008	I , John , am he who heard and saw these things . And when I had heard and seen I fell down to worship at the feet of the angel who had shown them to me .
66022009	But he said to me , " No , no . I am a fellow servant of yours and of your brethren and of the prophets and of those who are keeping the words of this book . Worship God . "
66022010	Then he said to me , " Do not seal up the words of the prophecy of this book . For the time is near .
66022011	Let the wrongdoer do wrong still , and let him who is filthy be filthy still , and let the righteous do righteousness still , and let the holy be holy still .
66022012	I am coming soon and my reward is with me , to pay each in full as his work is .
66022013	I am the Alpha and the Omega , the First and the Last , the Beginning and the End .
66022014	Blessed will those be who wash their robes so that they may have the right to the tree of life and may enter by the gates into the city .
66022015	Outside are the dogs and the sorcerers and the unchaste and the murderers and the idolaters and every one who loves and makes a lie .
66022016	" I , Jesus , have sent my angel to give you this testimony for the churches . I am the Root and the Offspring of David , the bright morning Star . "
66022017	The Spirit and the Bride say , " Come . " Let him who hears say , " Come . " Let him who thirsts come . Let him who will take the water of life freely .
66022018	I testify to every one who hears the words of the prophecy of this book , if any one adds to these things , God will add to him the plagues that are written in this book ,
66022019	and if any one takes away anything from the words of the book of this prophecy , God will take away his share from the tree of life and from the holy city , which are written of in this book .
66022020	He who bears this testimony says , " Yes , I am coming soon . " Amen , come , Lord Jesus .
66022021	The grace of the Lord Jesus be with all !
